288/**
289 * Implementation Guide Publisher
290 *
291 * If you want to use this inside a FHIR server, and not to access content
292 * on a local folder, provide your own implementation of the file fetcher
293 *
294 * rough sequence of activities:
295 *
296 *   load the context using the internal validation pack
297 *   connect to the terminology service
298 *
299 *   parse the implementation guide
300 *   find all the source files and determine the resource type
301 *   load resources in this order:
302 *     naming system
303 *     code system
304 *     value set
305 *     data element?
306 *     structure definition
307 *     concept map
308 *     structure map
309 *
310 *   validate all source files (including the IG itself)
311 *   
312 *   for each source file:
313 *     generate all outputs
314 *
315 *   generate summary file
316 *
317 * Documentation: see http://wiki.hl7.org/index.php?title=IG_Publisher_Documentation
318 * 
319 * @author Grahame Grieve
320 */
321
322public class Publisher implements IWorkerContext.ILoggingService, IReferenceResolver, IValidationProfileUsageTracker {
323
324  public class CopyRightUsageStatement {
325
326    private String name;
327    private String html;
328
329    public CopyRightUsageStatement(String name, String html) {
330      super();
331      this.name = name;
332      this.html = html;
333    }
334
335    public String getSystemName() {
336      return name;
337    }
338
339    public String getHtml() {
340      return html;
341    }
342
343  }

345  public class JsonDependency {
346    private String name;
347    private String canonical;
348    private String npmId;
349    private String version;
350    public JsonDependency(String name, String canonical, String npmId, String version) {
351      super();
352      this.name = name;
353      this.canonical = canonical;
354      this.npmId = npmId;
355      this.version = version;
356    }
357    public String getName() {
358      return name;
359    }
360    public String getCanonical() {
361      return canonical;
362    }
363    public String getNpmId() {
364      return npmId;
365    }
366    public String getVersion() {
367      return version;
368    }
369    
370
371  }

373  public class IGPublisherHostServices implements IEvaluationContext {
374
375    @Override
376    public List<Base> resolveConstant(Object appContext, String name, boolean beforeContext) throws PathEngineException {
377       return new ArrayList<>();
378    }
379
380    @Override
381    public TypeDetails resolveConstantType(Object appContext, String name) throws PathEngineException {
382      throw new NotImplementedException("Not done yet (IGPublisherHostServices.resolveConstantType)");
383    }
384
385    @Override
386    public boolean log(String argument, List<Base> focus) {
387      return false;
388    }
389
390    @Override
391    public FunctionDetails resolveFunction(String functionName) {
392      throw new NotImplementedException("Not done yet (IGPublisherHostServices.resolveFunction)");
393    }
394
395    @Override
396    public TypeDetails checkFunction(Object appContext, String functionName, List<TypeDetails> parameters) throws PathEngineException {
397      throw new NotImplementedException("Not done yet (IGPublisherHostServices.checkFunction)");
398    }
399
400    @Override
401    public List<Base> executeFunction(Object appContext, List<Base> focus, String functionName, List<List<Base>> parameters) {
402      throw new NotImplementedException("Not done yet (IGPublisherHostServices.executeFunction)");
403    }
404
405    @Override
406    public Base resolveReference(Object appContext, String url, Base refContext) {
407      if (Utilities.isAbsoluteUrl(url)) {
408        if (url.startsWith(igpkp.getCanonical())) {
409          url = url.substring(igpkp.getCanonical().length());
410          if (url.startsWith("/")) {
411            url = url.substring(1);
412          }
413        } else
414          return null;;
415      }
416      for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
417        for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
418          if (r.getElement() != null && url.equals(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId())) {
419            return r.getElement();
420          }
421        }
422      }
423      return null;
424    }
425
426    @Override
427    public boolean conformsToProfile(Object appContext, Base item, String url) throws FHIRException {
428      IResourceValidator val = context.newValidator();
429      List<ValidationMessage> valerrors = new ArrayList<ValidationMessage>();
430      if (item instanceof Resource) {
431        val.validate(appContext, valerrors, (Resource) item, url);
432        boolean ok = true;
433        for (ValidationMessage v : valerrors) {
434          ok = ok && v.getLevel().isError();
435        }
436        return ok;
437      }
438      throw new NotImplementedException("Not done yet (IGPublisherHostServices.conformsToProfile), when item is element");
439    }
440
441    @Override
442    public ValueSet resolveValueSet(Object appContext, String url) {
443      throw new NotImplementedException("Not done yet (IGPublisherHostServices.resolveValueSet)"); // cause I don't know when we 'd need to do this
444    }
445  }

447  public class TypeParserR2 implements ITypeParser {
448
449    @Override
450    public Base parseType(String xml, String type) throws IOException, FHIRException {
451      org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.model.Type t = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.XmlParser().parseType(xml, type); 
452      return VersionConvertorFactory_10_50.convertType(t);
453    }
454  }

722  private class PreProcessInfo {
723    private String xsltName;
724    private byte[] xslt;
725    private String relativePath;
726    public PreProcessInfo(String xsltName, String relativePath) throws IOException {
727      this.xsltName = xsltName;
728      if (xsltName!=null) {
729        this.xslt = TextFile.fileToBytes(xsltName);
730      }
731      this.relativePath = relativePath;
732    }
733    public boolean hasXslt() {
734      return xslt!=null;
735    }
736    public byte[] getXslt() {
737      return xslt;
738    }
739    public boolean hasRelativePath() {
740      return relativePath != null && !relativePath.isEmpty();
741    }
742    public String getRelativePath() {
743      return relativePath;
744    }
745  }
746
747  public void execute() throws Exception {
748    tt = new TimeTracker();
749    initialize();
750    if (isBuildingTemplate) {
751      packageTemplate();
752    } else {
753      log("Load Content");
754      try {
755        createIg();
756      } catch (Exception e) {
757        recordOutcome(e, null);
758        throw e;
759      }
760
761      if (watch) {
762        firstExecution = false;
763        log("Watching for changes on a 5sec cycle");
764        while (watch) { // terminated externally
765          Thread.sleep(5000);
766          if (load()) {
767            log("Processing changes to "+Integer.toString(changeList.size())+(changeList.size() == 1 ? " file" : " files")+" @ "+genTime());
768            long startTime = System.nanoTime();
769            loadConformance();
770            generateNarratives();
771            checkDependencies();
772            if (!noValidation) {
773              validate();
774            }
775            generate();
776            clean();
777            long endTime = System.nanoTime();
778            processTxLog(Utilities.path(destDir != null ? destDir : outputDir, "qa-tx.html"));
779            BallotChecker bc = new BallotChecker(repoRoot);
780            ValidationPresenter val = new ValidationPresenter(version, workingVersion(), igpkp, childPublisher == null? null : childPublisher.getIgpkp(), outputDir, npmName, childPublisher == null? null : childPublisher.npmName, 
781                bc.check(igpkp.getCanonical(), npmName, workingVersion(), historyPage, version), IGVersionUtil.getVersion(), fetchCurrentIGPubVersion(), realmRules, previousVersionComparator,
782                new DependencyRenderer(pcm, outputDir, npmName, templateManager).render(publishedIg), new HTAAnalysisRenderer(context, outputDir, markdownEngine).render(publishedIg.getPackageId(), fileList, publishedIg.present()), 
783                new VersionCheckRenderer(npm.version(), publishedIg.getVersion(), bc.getPackageList(), igpkp.getCanonical()).generate(), copyrightYear, context,
784                    noNarrativeResources, noValidateResources, noValidation, noGenerate);
785            log("Finished. "+Utilities.presentDuration(endTime - startTime)+". Validation output in "+val.generate(sourceIg.getName(), errors, fileList, Utilities.path(destDir != null ? destDir : outputDir, "qa.html"), suppressedMessages));
786            recordOutcome(null, val);
787          }
788        }
789      } else {
790        log("Done"+(!publishing && mode != IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD ? ". This IG has been built using the 'normal' process for local use. If building to host on an an external website, use the process documented [yet to be documented]])" : ""));
791      }
792    }
793    if (templateLoaded && new File(rootDir).exists()) {
794      Utilities.clearDirectory(Utilities.path(rootDir, "template"));
795    }
796    if (folderToDelete != null) {
797      try {
798        Utilities.clearDirectory(folderToDelete);
799        new File(folderToDelete).delete();
800      } catch (Throwable e) {
801        // nothing
802      }
803    }
804  }
805
806  private void packageTemplate() throws IOException {
807    Utilities.createDirectory(outputDir);
808    long startTime = System.nanoTime();
809    JsonObject qaJson = new JsonObject();
810    qaJson.addProperty("url", templateInfo.get("canonical").getAsString());
811    qaJson.addProperty("package-id", templateInfo.get("name").getAsString());
812    qaJson.addProperty("ig-ver", templateInfo.get("version").getAsString());
813    qaJson.addProperty("date", new SimpleDateFormat("EEE, dd MMM, yyyy HH:mm:ss Z", new Locale("en", "US")).format(execTime.getTime()));
814    qaJson.addProperty("version", Constants.VERSION);
815    qaJson.addProperty("tool", Constants.VERSION+" ("+ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION+")");
816    try {
817      File od = new File(outputDir);
818      FileUtils.cleanDirectory(od);
819      npm = new NPMPackageGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "package.tgz"), templateInfo, execTime.getTime(), !publishing);
820      npm.loadFiles(rootDir, new File(rootDir), ".git", "output", "package");
821      npm.finish();
822
823      TextFile.stringToFile(makeTemplateIndexPage(), Utilities.path(outputDir, "index.html"), false);
824      TextFile.stringToFile(makeTemplateJekyllIndexPage(), Utilities.path(outputDir, "jekyll.html"), false);
825      TextFile.stringToFile(makeTemplateQAPage(), Utilities.path(outputDir, "qa.html"), false);
826      
827      if (mode != IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD) {
828        pcm.addPackageToCache(templateInfo.get("name").getAsString(), templateInfo.get("version").getAsString(), new FileInputStream(npm.filename()), Utilities.path(outputDir, "package.tgz"));
829        pcm.addPackageToCache(templateInfo.get("name").getAsString(), "dev", new FileInputStream(npm.filename()), Utilities.path(outputDir, "package.tgz"));
830      }
831    } catch (Exception e) {
832       e.printStackTrace();
833       qaJson.addProperty("exception", e.getMessage());
834    }
835    long endTime = System.nanoTime();
836    Gson gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
837    String json = gson.toJson(qaJson);
838    TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(outputDir, "qa.json"), false);
839
840    ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(tempDir, "full-ig.zip"));
841    zip.addFolder(outputDir, "site/", false);
842    zip.addFileSource("index.html", REDIRECT_SOURCE, false);
843    zip.close();
844    Utilities.copyFile(Utilities.path(tempDir, "full-ig.zip"), Utilities.path(outputDir, "full-ig.zip"));
845
846    // registering the package locally
847    log("Finished. "+Utilities.presentDuration(endTime - startTime)+". Output in "+outputDir);
848  }

851  private String makeTemplateIndexPage() {
852    String page = "<!DOCTYPE HTML>\r\n"+
853       "<html xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\" xml:lang=\"en\" lang=\"en\">\r\n"+
854       "<head>\r\n"+
855       "  <title>Template Page</title>\r\n"+
856       "</head>\r\n"+
857       "<body>\r\n"+
858       "  <p><b>Template {{npm}}</b></p>\r\n"+
859       "  <p>You can <a href=\"package.tgz\">download the template</a>, though you should not need to; just refer to the template as {{npm}} in your IG configuration.</p>\r\n"+
860       "  <p>A <a href=\"{{canonical}}/history.html\">full version history is published</a></p>\r\n"+
861       "</body>\r\n"+
862       "</html>\r\n";
863    return page.replace("{{npm}}", templateInfo.get("name").getAsString()).replace("{{canonical}}", templateInfo.get("canonical").getAsString());
864  }

869       "title: {{npm}}"+

872       "  <p>You can <a href=\"package.tgz\">download the template</a>, though you should not need to; just refer to the template as {{npm}} in your IG configuration.</p>\r\n"+
873       "  <p>A <a href=\"{{canonical}}/history.html\">full version history is published</a></p>\r\n";
874    return page.replace("{{npm}}", templateInfo.get("name").getAsString()).replace("{{canonical}}", templateInfo.get("canonical").getAsString());

877  private String makeTemplateQAPage() {
878    String page = "<!DOCTYPE HTML><html xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\" xml:lang=\"en\" lang=\"en\"><head><title>Template QA Page</title></head><body><p><b>Template {{npm}}</b></p><p>You  can <a href=\"package.tgz\">download the template</a>, though you should not need to; just refer to the template as {{npm}} in your IG configuration.</p></body></html>";

882  private void processTxLog(String path) throws FileNotFoundException, IOException {
883    if (txLog != null) {
884      String tx = TextFile.fileToString(txLog);
885      PrintStream f = new PrintStream(new FileOutputStream(path));
886      String title = "Terminology Server Log";
887      f.println("<html><head><title>"+title+"</title></head><body><h2>"+title+"</h2>");
888      f.print(tx);
889      f.println("</head></html>");
890      f.close();
891    } 
892  }

895  public void createIg() throws Exception, IOException, EOperationOutcome, FHIRException {
896    try {
897      TimeTracker.Session tts = tt.start("loading");
898      load();
899      tts.end();
900
901      tts = tt.start("generate");
902      log("Processing Conformance Resources");
903      loadConformance();
904      if (!noValidation) {
905        log("Validating Resources");
906        try {
907          validate();
908        } catch (Exception ex){
909          log("Unhandled Exception: " +ex.toString());
910          throw(ex);
911        }
912      }
913      log("Processing Provenance Records");
914      processProvenanceDetails();
915      log("Generating Outputs in "+outputDir);
916      generate();
917      clean();
918      BallotChecker bc = new BallotChecker(repoRoot);
919      ValidationPresenter val = new ValidationPresenter(version, workingVersion(), igpkp, childPublisher == null? null : childPublisher.getIgpkp(), rootDir, npmName, childPublisher == null? null : childPublisher.npmName, 
920          bc.check(igpkp.getCanonical(), npmName, workingVersion(), historyPage, version), IGVersionUtil.getVersion(), fetchCurrentIGPubVersion(), realmRules, previousVersionComparator,
921          new DependencyRenderer(pcm, outputDir, npmName, templateManager).render(publishedIg), new HTAAnalysisRenderer(context, outputDir, markdownEngine).render(publishedIg.getPackageId(), fileList, publishedIg.present()), 
922          new VersionCheckRenderer(npm.version(), publishedIg.getVersion(), bc.getPackageList(), igpkp.getCanonical()).generate(), copyrightYear, context, noNarrativeResources, noValidateResources, noValidation, noGenerate);
923      tts.end();
924      if (isChild()) {
925        log("Finished. "+tt.report());      
926      } else {
927        processTxLog(Utilities.path(destDir != null ? destDir : outputDir, "qa-tx.html"));
928        log("Finished. "+tt.report());      
929        log("Validation output in "+val.generate(sourceIg.getName(), errors, fileList, Utilities.path(destDir != null ? destDir : outputDir, "qa.html"), suppressedMessages));
930      }
931      recordOutcome(null, val);
932    } catch (Exception e) {
933      try {
934        recordOutcome(e, null);        
935      } catch (Exception ex) {
936        ex.printStackTrace();
937      }
938      throw e;
939    }
940  }
941
942  private void processProvenanceDetails() throws Exception {
943    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
944      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
945        if (!r.isExample()) {
946          if (r.fhirType().equals("Provenance")) { 
947            logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Process Provenance "+f.getName()+" : "+r.getId());
948            if (processProvenance(igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true), r.getElement(), r.getResource()))
949              r.setProvenance(true);
950          } else if (r.fhirType().equals("Bundle")) {
951            if (processProvenanceEntries(f, r))
952              r.setProvenance(true);              
953          }
954        }
955      }
956    }    
957  }
958
959  public boolean processProvenanceEntries(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) throws Exception {
960    boolean isHistory = false;
961    Bundle b = (Bundle) r.getResource();
962    List<Element> entries = r.getElement().getChildrenByName("entry");
963    for (int i = 0; i < entries.size(); i++) {
964      Element entry = entries.get(i);
965      Element res = entry.getNamedChild("resource");
966      if (res != null && "Provenance".equals(res.fhirType())) {
967        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Process Provenance "+f.getName()+" : "+r.getId()+".entry["+i+"]");
968        if (processProvenance(igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true), res, b == null ? null : b.getEntry().get(i).getResource()))
969          isHistory = true;
970      }
971    }
972    return isHistory;
973  }
974
975  private ProvenanceDetails processProvenanceForBundle(FetchedFile f, String path, Element r) throws Exception {
976    Provenance pv = (Provenance) convertFromElement(r);
977    ProvenanceDetails pd = processProvenance(path, pv);
978
979    for (Reference entity : pv.getTarget()) {
980      String ref = entity.getReference();
981      FetchedResource target = getResourceForRef(f, ref);
982      String p, d;
983      if (target == null) {
984        p = null;
985        d = entity.hasDisplay() ? entity.getDisplay() : ref;
986      } else {
987        p = igpkp.getLinkFor(target, true);
988        d = target.getTitle() != null ? target.getTitle() : entity.hasDisplay() ? entity.getDisplay() : ref;
989      }
990      pd.getTargets().add(pd.new ProvenanceDetailsTarget(p, d));
991    }    
992    return pd;    
993  }
994  
995  private boolean processProvenance(String path, Element resource, Resource r) {
996    boolean containsHistory = false;
997    Provenance pv = null;
998    try {
999      pv = (Provenance) (r == null ? convertFromElement(resource) : r);
1000      RendererFactory.factory(pv, rc.setParser(getTypeLoader(null))).render(pv);
1001    } catch (Exception e) {
1002      // nothing, if there's a problem, we'll take it up elsewhere
1003    }
1004    if (pv != null) {
1005      for (Reference entity : pv.getTarget()) {
1006        if (entity.hasReference()) {
1007          String[] ref = entity.getReference().split("\\/");
1008          int i = chooseType(ref);
1009          if (i >= 0) {
1010            FetchedResource res = fetchByResource(ref[i], ref[i+1]);
1011            if (res != null) {
1012              res.getAudits().add(processProvenance(path, pv));
1013              containsHistory = true;
1014            }
1015          }
1016        }
1017      }
1018    }
1019    return containsHistory;
1020  }
1021
1022  private ProvenanceDetails processProvenance(String path, Provenance pv) {
1023    ProvenanceDetails res = new ProvenanceDetails();
1024    res.setPath(path);
1025    res.setAction(pv.getActivity().getCodingFirstRep());
1026    res.setDate(pv.hasOccurredPeriod() ? pv.getOccurredPeriod().getEndElement() : pv.hasOccurredDateTimeType() ? pv.getOccurredDateTimeType() : pv.getRecordedElement());
1027    if (pv.hasReason()) {
1028      res.setComment(pv.getReasonFirstRep().getText());
1029    }
1030    for (ProvenanceAgentComponent agent : pv.getAgent()) {
1031      for (Coding c : agent.getType().getCoding()) {
1032        res.getActors().put(c, agent.getWho());
1033      }
1034    }
1035    return res;
1036  }
1037
1038  private int chooseType(String[] ref) {
1039    int res = -1;
1040    for (int i = 0; i < ref.length-1; i++) { // note -1 - don't bother checking the last value, which might also be a resource name (e.g StructureDefinition/XXX)
1041      if (context.getResourceNames().contains(ref[i])) {
1042        res = i;
1043      }
1044    }
1045    return res;
1046  }
1047
1048  private void recordOutcome(Exception ex, ValidationPresenter val) {
1049    try {
1050      JsonObject j = new JsonObject();
1051      if (sourceIg != null) {
1052        j.addProperty("url", sourceIg.getUrl());
1053        j.addProperty("name", sourceIg.getName());
1054      }
1055      if (publishedIg != null && publishedIg.hasPackageId()) {
1056        j.addProperty("package-id", publishedIg.getPackageId());
1057        j.addProperty("ig-ver", publishedIg.getVersion());
1058      }
1059      j.addProperty("date", new SimpleDateFormat("EEE, dd MMM, yyyy HH:mm:ss Z", new Locale("en", "US")).format(execTime.getTime()));
1060      if (val != null) {
1061        j.addProperty("errs", val.getErr());
1062        j.addProperty("warnings", val.getWarn());
1063        j.addProperty("hints", val.getInfo());
1064      }
1065      if (ex != null) {
1066        j.addProperty("exception", ex.getMessage());
1067      }
1068      j.addProperty("version", version);
1069      if (templatePck != null) {
1070        j.addProperty("template", templatePck);
1071      }
1072      j.addProperty("tool", Constants.VERSION+" ("+ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION+")");
1073      Gson gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
1074      String json = gson.toJson(j);
1075      TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(destDir != null ? destDir : outputDir, "qa.json"), false);
1076    } catch (Exception e) {
1077      // nothing at all
1078    }
1079  }

1091  @Override
1092  public ResourceWithReference resolve(RenderingContext context, String url) {
1093    if (url == null) {
1094      return null;
1095    }
1096    
1097    String[] parts = url.split("\\/");
1098    if (parts.length >= 2 && !Utilities.startsWithInList(url, "urn:uuid:", "urn:oid:", "cid:")) {
1099      for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1100        for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
1101          if (r.getElement() != null && r.fhirType().equals(parts[0]) && r.getId().equals(parts[1])) {
1102            String path = igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true);
1103            return new ResourceWithReference(path, new ElementWrappers.ResourceWrapperMetaElement(context, r.getElement()));
1104          }
1105          if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
1106            if (url.equals(((CanonicalResource) r.getResource()).getUrl())) {
1107              String path = igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true);
1108              return new ResourceWithReference(path, new DirectWrappers.ResourceWrapperDirect(context, r.getResource()));            
1109            }
1110          }
1111        }
1112      }
1113      for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1114        for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
1115          if (r.fhirType().equals("Bundle")) {
1116            List<Element> entries = r.getElement().getChildrenByName("entry");
1117            for (Element entry : entries) {
1118              Element res = entry.getNamedChild("resource");
1119              if (res != null && res.fhirType().equals(parts[0]) && res.hasChild("id") && res.getNamedChildValue("id").equals(parts[1])) {
1120                String path = igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true)+"#"+parts[0]+"_"+parts[1];
1121                return new ResourceWithReference(path, new ElementWrappers.ResourceWrapperMetaElement(context, r.getElement()));
1122              }
1123            }
1124          }
1125        }
1126      }
1127    }
1128    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1129      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
1130        if (r.fhirType().equals("Bundle")) {
1131          List<Element> entries = r.getElement().getChildrenByName("entry");
1132          for (Element entry : entries) {
1133            Element res = entry.getNamedChild("resource");
1134            String fu = entry.getNamedChildValue("fullUrl");
1135            if (res != null && fu != null && fu.equals(url)) {
1136              String path = igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true)+"#"+fu.replace(":", "-");
1137              return new ResourceWithReference(path, new ElementWrappers.ResourceWrapperMetaElement(context, r.getElement()));
1138            }
1139          }
1140        }
1141      }
1142    }
1143    
1144    for (SpecMapManager sp : specMaps) {
1145      String fp = sp.getBase()+"/"+url;
1146      String path;
1147      try {
1148        path = sp.getPath(fp, null);
1149      } catch (Exception e) {
1150        path = null;
1151      }
1152      if (path != null)
1153        return new ResourceWithReference(path, null);
1154    }
1155    return null;
1156
1157  }
1158
1159  private void generateNarratives() throws Exception {
1160    Session tts = tt.start("narrative generation");
1161    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "gen narratives");
1162    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1163      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {        
1164        if (r.getExampleUri()==null || genExampleNarratives) {
1165          if (!passesNarrativeFilter(r)) {
1166            noNarrativeResources.add(r);
1167            logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "narrative for "+f.getName()+" : "+r.getId()+" suppressed");
1168            if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource) {
1169              ((DomainResource) r.getResource()).setText(null);
1170            }
1171            r.getElement().removeChild("text");
1172          } else {
1173            logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "narrative for "+f.getName()+" : "+r.getId());
1174            if (r.getResource() != null && isConvertableResource(r.getResource().fhirType())) {
1175              boolean regen = false;
1176              rc.setDefinitionsTarget(igpkp.getDefinitionsName(r));
1177              if (r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource && !(((DomainResource) r.getResource()).hasText() && ((DomainResource) r.getResource()).getText().hasDiv())) {
1178                regen = true;
1179                RendererFactory.factory(r.getResource(), rc).render((DomainResource) r.getResource());
1180              } else if (r.getResource() instanceof Bundle) {
1181                regen = true;
1182                new BundleRenderer(rc).render((Bundle) r.getResource());
1183              } else if (r.getResource() instanceof Parameters) {
1184                regen = true;
1185                Parameters p = (Parameters) r.getResource();
1186                new ParametersRenderer(rc, new ResourceContext(ResourceContextType.PARAMETERS , p, null)).render(p);
1187              } else if (r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource) {
1188                checkExistingNarrative(f, r, ((DomainResource) r.getResource()).getText().getDiv());
1189              }
1190              if (regen)
1191                r.setElement(convertToElement(r.getResource()));
1192            } else {
1193              RenderingContext lrc = rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f,r));
1194              if ("http://hl7.org/fhir/StructureDefinition/DomainResource".equals(r.getElement().getProperty().getStructure().getBaseDefinition()) && !hasNarrative(r.getElement())) {
1195                ResourceWrapper rw = new ElementWrappers.ResourceWrapperMetaElement(lrc, r.getElement());
1196                RendererFactory.factory(rw, lrc).render(rw);
1197              } else if (r.fhirType().equals("Bundle")) {
1198                for (Element e : r.getElement().getChildrenByName("entry")) {
1199                  Element res = e.getNamedChild("resource");
1200                  if (res!=null && "http://hl7.org/fhir/StructureDefinition/DomainResource".equals(res.getProperty().getStructure().getBaseDefinition()) && !hasNarrative(res)) {
1201                    ResourceWrapper rw = new ElementWrappers.ResourceWrapperMetaElement(lrc, res);
1202                    RendererFactory.factory(rw, lrc, new ResourceContext(ResourceContextType.BUNDLE, r.getElement(), res)).render(rw);
1203                  }
1204                }
1205              } else if ("http://hl7.org/fhir/StructureDefinition/DomainResource".equals(r.getElement().getProperty().getStructure().getBaseDefinition()) && hasNarrative(r.getElement())) {
1206                checkExistingNarrative(f, r, r.getElement().getNamedChild("text").getNamedChild("div").getXhtml());
1207              }
1208            }
1209          }
1210        } else {
1211          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "skipped narrative for "+f.getName()+" : "+r.getId());
1212        }
1213      }
1214    }
1215    tts.end();
1216  }
1217
1218  private boolean passesNarrativeFilter(FetchedResource r) {
1219    for (String s : noNarratives) {
1220      String[] p = s.split("\\/");
1221      if (p.length == 2) {
1222        if (("*".equals(p[0]) || r.fhirType().equals(p[0])) &&
1223            ("*".equals(p[1]) || r.getId().equals(p[1]))) {
1224          return false;
1225        }
1226      }
1227    }
1228    return true;
1229  }
1230
1231  private boolean passesValidationFilter(FetchedResource r) {
1232    for (String s : noValidate) {
1233      String[] p = s.split("\\/");
1234      if (p.length == 2) {
1235        if (("*".equals(p[0]) || r.fhirType().equals(p[0])) &&
1236            ("*".equals(p[1]) || r.getId().equals(p[1]))) {
1237          return false;
1238        }
1239      }
1240    }
1241    return true;
1242  }
1243
1244  private void checkExistingNarrative(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, XhtmlNode xhtml) {
1245    if (xhtml != null) {
1246      boolean hasGenNarrative = scanForGeneratedNarrative(xhtml);
1247      if (hasGenNarrative) {
1248        f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.NOTFOUND, r.fhirType()+".text.div", "Resource has provided narrative, but the narrative indicates that it is generated - remove the narrative or fix it up", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
1249        r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.NOTFOUND, r.fhirType()+".text.div", "Resource has provided narrative, but the narrative indicates that it is generated - remove the narrative or fix it up", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
1250      }
1251    }
1252  }
1253
1254  private boolean scanForGeneratedNarrative(XhtmlNode x) {
1255    if (x.getContent() != null && x.getContent().contains("Generated Narrative")) {
1256      return true;
1257    }
1258    for (XhtmlNode c : x.getChildNodes()) {
1259      if (scanForGeneratedNarrative(c)) {
1260        return true;
1261      }
1262    }
1263    return false;
1264  }
1265
1266  private boolean isConvertableResource(String t) {
1267    return Utilities.existsInList(t, "StructureDefinition", "ValueSet", "CodeSystem", "Conformance", "CapabilityStatement", "Questionnaire", "NamingSystem", 
1268        "ConceptMap", "OperationOutcome", "CompartmentDefinition", "OperationDefinition", "ImplementationGuide");
1269  }

1272  private ITypeParser getTypeLoader(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) throws Exception {
1273    String ver = r.getConfig() == null ? null : ostr(r.getConfig(), "version");
1274    return getTypeLoader(ver);
1275  }
1276  
1277  private ITypeParser getTypeLoader(String ver) throws Exception {
1278    if (ver == null)
1279      ver = version; // fall back to global version
1280    if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(ver)) {
1281      return new TypeParserR3();
1282    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(ver)) {
1283      return new TypeParserR4();
1284    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(ver)) {
1285      return new TypeParserR14();
1286    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(ver)) {
1287      return new TypeParserR2();
1288    } else if (ver.equals(Constants.VERSION) || VersionUtilities.isR4BVer(ver)) {
1289      return new TypeParserR5();
1290    } else
1291      throw new FHIRException("Unsupported version "+ver);
1292  }
1293
1294  private boolean hasNarrative(Element element) {
1295    return element.hasChild("text") && element.getNamedChild("text").hasChild("div");
1296  }

1298  private void clean() throws Exception {
1299    for (Resource r : loaded) {
1300      context.dropResource(r);
1301    }
1302    if (destDir != null) {
1303      if (!(new File(destDir).exists()))
1304        Utilities.createDirectory(destDir);
1305      Utilities.copyDirectory(outputDir, destDir, null);
1306    }
1307  }

1309  private String genTime() {
1310    return new SimpleDateFormat("EEE, MMM d, yyyy HH:mmZ", new Locale("en", "US")).format(execTime.getTime());
1311  }

1313  private String genDate() {
1314    return new SimpleDateFormat("dd/MM/yyyy", new Locale("en", "US")).format(execTime.getTime());
1315  }
1316
1317  private void checkDependencies() {
1318    // first, we load all the direct dependency lists
1319    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1320      if (f.getDependencies() == null) {
1321        loadDependencyList(f);
1322      }
1323    }
1324
1325    // now, we keep adding to the change list till there's no change
1326    boolean changed;
1327    do {
1328      changed = false;
1329      for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1330        if (!changeList.contains(f)) {
1331          boolean dep = false;
1332          for (FetchedFile d : f.getDependencies())
1333            if (changeList.contains(d))
1334              dep = true;
1335          if (dep) {
1336            changeList.add(f);
1337            changed = true;
1338          }
1339        }
1340      }
1341    } while (changed);
1342  }
1343
1344  private void loadDependencyList(FetchedFile f) {
1345    f.setDependencies(new ArrayList<FetchedFile>());
1346    for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
1347      if (r.fhirType().equals("ValueSet"))
1348        loadValueSetDependencies(f, r);
1349      else if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition"))
1350        loadProfileDependencies(f, r);
1351      else
1352        ; // all other resource types don't have dependencies that we care about for rendering purposes
1353    }
1354  }
1355
1356  private void loadValueSetDependencies(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) {
1357    ValueSet vs = (ValueSet) r.getResource();
1358    for (ConceptSetComponent cc : vs.getCompose().getInclude()) {
1359      for (UriType vsi : cc.getValueSet()) {
1360        FetchedFile fi = getFileForUri(vsi.getValue());
1361        if (fi != null)
1362          f.getDependencies().add(fi);
1363      }
1364    }
1365    for (ConceptSetComponent cc : vs.getCompose().getExclude()) {
1366      for (UriType vsi : cc.getValueSet()) {
1367        FetchedFile fi = getFileForUri(vsi.getValue());
1368        if (fi != null)
1369          f.getDependencies().add(fi);
1370      }
1371    }
1372    for (ConceptSetComponent vsc : vs.getCompose().getInclude()) {
1373      FetchedFile fi = getFileForUri(vsc.getSystem());
1374      if (fi != null)
1375        f.getDependencies().add(fi);
1376    }
1377    for (ConceptSetComponent vsc : vs.getCompose().getExclude()) {
1378      FetchedFile fi = getFileForUri(vsc.getSystem());
1379      if (fi != null)
1380        f.getDependencies().add(fi);
1381    }
1382  }
1383
1384  private FetchedFile getFileForFile(String path) {
1385    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1386      if (f.getPath().equals(path))
1387        return f;
1388    }
1389    return null;
1390  }
1391

1393  private FetchedFile getFileForUri(String uri) {
1394    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1395      if (getResourceForUri(f, uri) != null)
1396        return f;
1397    }
1398    return null;
1399  }
1400
1401  private FetchedResource getResourceForUri(FetchedFile f, String uri) {
1402    for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
1403      if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
1404        CanonicalResource bc = (CanonicalResource) r.getResource();
1405        if (bc.getUrl() != null && bc.getUrl().equals(uri))
1406          return r;
1407      }
1408    }
1409    return null;
1410  }
1411
1412  private FetchedResource getResourceForRef(FetchedFile f, String ref) {
1413    for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
1414      if ((r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId()).equals(ref))
1415        return r;
1416    }
1417    for (FetchedFile f1 : fileList) {
1418      for (FetchedResource r : f1.getResources()) {
1419        if ((r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId()).equals(ref))
1420          return r;
1421        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource && ((CanonicalResource) r.getResource()).getUrl().equals(ref))
1422          return r;
1423      }
1424    }
1425    
1426    return null;
1427  }
1428
1429  private FetchedResource getResourceForUri(String uri) {
1430    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
1431      FetchedResource r = getResourceForUri(f, uri);
1432      if (r != null)
1433        return r;
1434    }
1435    return null;
1436  }

1438  private void loadProfileDependencies(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) {
1439    StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
1440    FetchedFile fi = getFileForUri(sd.getBaseDefinition());
1441    if (fi != null)
1442      f.getDependencies().add(fi);
1443  }

1445  private boolean bool(JsonObject obj, String name) throws Exception {
1446    if (!obj.has(name))
1447      return false;
1448    if (!(obj.get(name) instanceof JsonPrimitive))
1449      return false;
1450    JsonPrimitive p = (JsonPrimitive) obj.get(name);
1451    if (p.isBoolean())
1452      return p.getAsBoolean();
1453    return false;
1454  }
1455  
1456  private String str(JsonObject obj, String name) throws Exception {
1457    if (!obj.has(name))
1458      throw new Exception("Property '"+name+"' not found");
1459    if (!(obj.get(name) instanceof JsonPrimitive))
1460      throw new Exception("Property '"+name+"' not a primitive");
1461    JsonPrimitive p = (JsonPrimitive) obj.get(name);
1462    if (!p.isString())
1463      throw new Exception("Property '"+name+"' not a string");
1464    return p.getAsString();
1465  }
1466
1467  private String ostr(JsonObject obj, String name) throws Exception {
1468    if (obj == null)
1469      return null;
1470    if (!obj.has(name))
1471      return null;
1472    if (!(obj.get(name) instanceof JsonPrimitive))
1473      return null;
1474    JsonPrimitive p = (JsonPrimitive) obj.get(name);
1475    if (p.isBoolean())
1476      return p.getAsString();
1477    if (!p.isString())
1478      return null;
1479    return p.getAsString();
1480  }
1481
1482  private String str(JsonObject obj, String name, String defValue) throws Exception {
1483    if (obj == null || !obj.has(name))
1484      return defValue;
1485    if (!(obj.get(name) instanceof JsonPrimitive))
1486      throw new Exception("Property "+name+" not a primitive");
1487    JsonPrimitive p = (JsonPrimitive) obj.get(name);
1488    if (!p.isString())
1489      throw new Exception("Property "+name+" not a string");
1490    return p.getAsString();
1491  }
1492
1493  public void initialize() throws Exception {
1494    firstExecution = true;
1495    pcm = new FilesystemPackageCacheManager(mode == null || mode == IGBuildMode.MANUAL || mode == IGBuildMode.PUBLICATION, ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION);
1496    if (mode == IGBuildMode.PUBLICATION)
1497      log("Build Formal Publication package, intended for "+getTargetOutput());
1498    
1499    if (apiKeyFile == null) {
1500      apiKeyFile = new IniFile(Utilities.path(System.getProperty("user.home"), "fhir-api-keys.ini"));
1501    }
1502    log("API keys loaded from "+apiKeyFile.getFileName());
1503    templateManager = new TemplateManager(pcm, logger, gh());
1504    templateProvider = new IGPublisherLiquidTemplateServices();
1505    extensionTracker = new ExtensionTracker();
1506    log("Package Cache: "+pcm.getFolder());
1507    if (packagesFolder != null) {
1508      log("Also loading Packages from "+packagesFolder);
1509      pcm.loadFromFolder(packagesFolder);
1510    }
1511    fetcher.setRootDir(rootDir);
1512    fetcher.setResourceDirs(resourceDirs);
1513    if (configFile != null && focusDir().contains(" ")) {
1514      throw new Error("There is a space in the folder path: \""+focusDir()+"\". Please fix your directory arrangement to remove the space and try again");
1515    }
1516    if (configFile != null) {
1517      File fsh = new File(Utilities.path(focusDir(), "fsh"));
1518      if (fsh.exists() && fsh.isDirectory() && !noFSH) {
1519        runFsh(new File(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(fsh.getAbsolutePath())));
1520      } else {
1521        File fsh2 = new File(Utilities.path(focusDir(), "input", "fsh"));
1522        if (fsh2.exists() && fsh2.isDirectory() && !noFSH) {
1523          runFsh(new File(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(fsh.getAbsolutePath())));   
1524        }
1525      }
1526    }
1527    IniFile ini = checkNewIg();
1528    if (ini != null) {
1529      newIg = true;
1530      initializeFromIg(ini);   
1531    } else if (isTemplate())
1532      initializeTemplate();
1533    else
1534      initializeFromJson();
1535    expectedJurisdiction = checkForJurisdiction();
1536    realmRules = makeRealmBusinessRules();
1537    previousVersionComparator = makePreviousVersionComparator();
1538  }
1539  
1540  private Coding checkForJurisdiction() {
1541    String id = npmName;
1542    if (!id.startsWith("hl7.") || !id.contains(".")) {
1543      return null;
1544    }
1545    String[] parts = id.split("\\.");
1546    if (Utilities.existsInList(parts[1], "terminology")) {
1547      return null;
1548    }
1549    if (Utilities.existsInList(parts[1], "fhir") && Utilities.existsInList(parts[2], "cda")) {
1550      return null;
1551    }
1552    if (Utilities.existsInList(parts[1], "fhir") && !Utilities.existsInList(parts[1], "nothing-yet")) {
1553      if (parts[2].equals("uv")) {
1554        igrealm = "uv";
1555        return new Coding("http://unstats.un.org/unsd/methods/m49/m49.htm", "001", "World");
1556      } else {
1557        igrealm = parts[2];
1558        return new Coding("urn:iso:std:iso:3166", parts[2].toUpperCase(), null);
1559      }
1560    } else {
1561      return null;
1562    }
1563  }
1564
1565  private String focusDir() {
1566    String dir = configFile.endsWith("ig.ini") ? configFile.substring(0, configFile.length()-6) : configFile;
1567    if (dir.endsWith(File.separatorChar+".")) {
1568      dir = dir.substring(0, dir.length()-2);
1569    }
1570    return Utilities.noString(dir) ? getCurentDirectory() : dir;
1571  }
1572
1573  public class MySushiHandler extends OutputStream {
1574
1575    private byte[] buffer;
1576    private int length;
1577    private int errorCount = -1;
1578
1579    public MySushiHandler() {
1580      buffer = new byte[256];
1581    }
1582
1583    public String getBufferString() {
1584      return new String(this.buffer, 0, length);
1585    }
1586
1587    private boolean passSushiFilter(String s) {
1588      if (Utilities.noString(s))
1589        return false;
1590      return true;
1591    }
1592
1593    @Override
1594    public void write(int b) throws IOException {
1595      buffer[length] = (byte) b;
1596      length++;
1597      if (b == 10) { // eoln
1598        String s = new String(buffer, 0, length);
1599        if (passSushiFilter(s)) {
1600          log("Sushi: "+s.trim());
1601          if (s.trim().startsWith("Errors:")) {
1602            errorCount = Integer.parseInt(s.substring(10).trim());
1603          }
1604        }
1605        length = 0;
1606      }
1607    }
1608  }
1609
1610  private void runFsh(File file) throws IOException { 
1611    File inif = new File(Utilities.path(file.getAbsolutePath(), "fsh.ini"));
1612    if (!inif.exists()) {
1613      inif = new File(Utilities.path(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(file.getAbsolutePath()), "fsh.ini"));
1614    }
1615    String fshVersion = null;
1616    if (inif.exists()) {
1617      IniFile ini = new IniFile(new FileInputStream(inif));
1618      if (ini.hasProperty("FSH", "timeout")) {
1619        fshTimeout = ini.getLongProperty("FSH", "timeout") * 1000;
1620      }
1621      if (ini.hasProperty("FSH", "sushi-version")) {
1622        fshVersion = ini.getStringProperty("FSH", "sushi-version");
1623      }
1624    }
1625    log("Run Sushi on "+file.getAbsolutePath());
1626    DefaultExecutor exec = new DefaultExecutor();
1627    exec.setExitValue(0);
1628    MySushiHandler pumpHandler = new MySushiHandler();
1629    PumpStreamHandler pump = new PumpStreamHandler(pumpHandler);
1630    exec.setStreamHandler(pump);
1631    exec.setWorkingDirectory(file);
1632    ExecuteWatchdog watchdog = new ExecuteWatchdog(fshTimeout);
1633    exec.setWatchdog(watchdog);
1634    String cmd = fshVersion == null ? "sushi" : "npx fsh-sushi@"+fshVersion;
1635    try {
1636      if (SystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS) {
1637        exec.execute(org.apache.commons.exec.CommandLine.parse("cmd /C "+cmd+" . -o ."));
1638      } else {
1639        exec.execute(org.apache.commons.exec.CommandLine.parse(cmd+" . -o ."));
1640      }
1641    } catch (IOException ioex) {
1642      log("Sushi couldn't be run. Complete output from running Sushi : " + pumpHandler.getBufferString());
1643      log("Note: Check that Sushi is installed correctly (\"npm install -g fsh-sushi\". On windows, get npm from https://www.npmjs.com/get-npm)");
1644      log("Exception: "+ioex.getMessage());
1645      throw ioex;
1646    }    
1647    if (pumpHandler.errorCount > 0) {
1648      throw new IOException("Sushi failed with errors. Complete output from running Sushi : " + pumpHandler.getBufferString());
1649    }
1650  }
1651
1652
1653  private void initializeTemplate() throws IOException {
1654    rootDir = configFile;
1655    outputDir = Utilities.path(rootDir, "output");
1656  }

1659  private boolean isTemplate() throws IOException {
1660    File pack = new File(Utilities.path(configFile, "package", "package.json"));
1661    if (pack.exists()) {
1662      JsonObject json = JsonTrackingParser.parseJson(pack);
1663      if (json.has("type") && "fhir.template".equals(json.get("type").getAsString())) {
1664        isBuildingTemplate = true;
1665        templateInfo = json;
1666        npmName = json.get("name").getAsString();
1667        System.out.println("targetOutput: "+targetOutput);
1668        return true;
1669      }
1670    }
1671    
1672    return false;
1673  }
1674  
1675  private IniFile checkNewIg() throws IOException {
1676    if (configFile == null)
1677      return null;
1678    if (configFile.endsWith(File.separatorChar+".")) {
1679      configFile = configFile.substring(0, configFile.length()-2);
1680    }
1681    File cf = mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD ? new File(configFile) : new CSFile(configFile);
1682    if (!cf.exists())
1683      return null;
1684    if (cf.isDirectory())
1685      cf = mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD ? new File(Utilities.path(configFile, "ig.ini")) : new CSFile(Utilities.path(configFile, "ig.ini"));
1686    if (!cf.exists())
1687      return null;
1688    String s = TextFile.fileToString(cf);
1689    if (s.startsWith("[IG]"))
1690        return new IniFile(cf.getAbsolutePath());
1691    else
1692      return null;
1693  }
1694
1695
1696  private void initializeFromIg(IniFile ini) throws Exception {
1697    configFile = ini.getFileName();
1698    igMode = true;
1699    repoRoot = Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(ini.getFileName());
1700    rootDir = repoRoot;
1701    // ok, first we load the template
1702    String templateName = ini.getStringProperty("IG", "template");
1703    if (templateName == null)
1704      throw new Exception("You must nominate a template - consult the IG Publisher documentation");
1705    igName = Utilities.path(repoRoot, ini.getStringProperty("IG", "ig"));
1706    try {
1707      try {
1708        sourceIg = (ImplementationGuide) org.hl7.fhir.r5.formats.FormatUtilities.loadFile(igName);
1709      } catch (Exception e) {
1710        sourceIg = (ImplementationGuide) VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(FormatUtilities.loadFile(igName));
1711      }
1712    } catch (Exception e) {
1713      throw new Exception("Error Parsing File "+igName+": "+e.getMessage(), e);
1714    }
1715    template = templateManager.loadTemplate(templateName, rootDir, sourceIg.getPackageId(), mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD);
1716
1717    if (template.hasExtraTemplates()) {
1718      processExtraTemplates(template.getExtraTemplates());
1719    }
1720    
1721    if (template.hasPreProcess()) {
1722      for (JsonElement e : template.getPreProcess()) {
1723        handlePreProcess((JsonObject)e, rootDir);
1724      }
1725    }
1726    
1727    Map<String, List<ValidationMessage>> messages = new HashMap<String, List<ValidationMessage>>();
1728    sourceIg = template.onLoadEvent(sourceIg, messages);
1729    checkOutcomes(messages);
1730    // ok, loaded. Now we start loading settings out of the IG
1731    tool = GenerationTool.Jekyll;
1732    version = processVersion(sourceIg.getFhirVersion().get(0).asStringValue()); // todo: support multiple versions
1733
1734    if (!VersionUtilities.isSupportedVersion(version)) {
1735      throw new Exception("Error: the IG declares that is based on version "+version+" but this IG publisher only supports publishing the following versions: "+VersionUtilities.listSupportedVersions());
1736    }
1737    pubVersion = FhirPublication.fromCode(version);
1738
1739    specPath = pathForVersion();
1740    qaDir = null;
1741    vsCache = Utilities.path(repoRoot, "txCache");
1742    templateProvider.clear();
1743    
1744    String expParams = null;
1745    List<String> exemptHtmlPatterns = new ArrayList<>();
1746    boolean hintAboutNonMustSupport = false;
1747    boolean anyExtensionsAllowed = false;
1748    boolean checkAggregation = false;
1749    boolean autoLoad = false;
1750    boolean showReferenceMessages = false;
1751    copyrightYear = null;
1752    Boolean useStatsOptOut = null;
1753    List<String> extensionDomains = new ArrayList<>();
1754    tempDir = Utilities.path(rootDir, "temp");
1755    outputDir = Utilities.path(rootDir, "output");
1756    Map<String, String> expParamMap = new HashMap<>();
1757    
1758    int count = 0;
1759    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionParameterComponent p : sourceIg.getDefinition().getParameter()) {
1760      // documentation for this list: https://confluence.hl7.org/display/FHIR/Implementation+Guide+Parameters
1761      if (p.getCode().equals("logging")) { // added
1762        logOptions.add(p.getValue());        
1763      } else if (p.getCode().equals("generate")) { // added
1764        if ("example-narratives".equals(p.getValue()))
1765          genExampleNarratives = true;
1766        if ("examples".equals(p.getValue()))
1767          genExamples = true;
1768      } else if (p.getCode().equals("no-narrative")) {
1769        noNarratives.add(p.getValue());
1770      } else if (p.getCode().equals("no-validate")) {
1771        noValidate.add(p.getValue());
1772      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-resource")) {
1773        resourceDirs.add(Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue()));
1774      } else if (p.getCode().equals("autoload-resources")) {     
1775        autoLoad = "true".equals(p.getValue());
1776      } else if (p.getCode().equals("codesystem-property")) {     
1777        codeSystemProps.add(p.getValue());
1778      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-pages")) {     
1779        pagesDirs.add(Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue()));
1780      } else if (p.getCode().equals("copyrightyear")) {     
1781        copyrightYear = p.getValue();
1782      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-qa")) {     
1783        qaDir = Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue());
1784      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-tx-cache")) {     
1785        vsCache =  Paths.get(p.getValue()).isAbsolute() ? p.getValue() : Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue());
1786      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-liquid")) {
1787        templateProvider.load(Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue()));
1788      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-temp")) {
1789        tempDir = Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue());
1790        if (!tempDir.startsWith(rootDir))
1791          throw new Exception("Temp directory must be a sub-folder of the base directory");
1792      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-output") && mode != IGBuildMode.WEBSERVER) {
1793        // Can't override outputDir if building using webserver
1794        outputDir = Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue());
1795        if (!outputDir.startsWith(rootDir))
1796          throw new Exception("Output directory must be a sub-folder of the base directory");
1797      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-history")) {     
1798        historyPage = p.getValue();
1799      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-expansion-params")) {     
1800        expParams = p.getValue();
1801      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-suppressed-warnings")) {     
1802        loadSuppressedMessages(Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue()), "ImplementationGuide.definition.parameter["+count+"].value");
1803      } else if (p.getCode().equals("html-exempt")) {     
1804        exemptHtmlPatterns.add(p.getValue());
1805      } else if (p.getCode().equals("usage-stats-opt-out")) {     
1806        useStatsOptOut = "true".equals(p.getValue());
1807      } else if (p.getCode().equals("extension-domain")) {
1808        extensionDomains.add(p.getValue());
1809      } else if (p.getCode().equals("bundle-references-resolve")) {
1810        bundleReferencesResolve = "true".equals(p.getValue());        
1811      } else if (p.getCode().equals("active-tables")) {
1812        HierarchicalTableGenerator.ACTIVE_TABLES = "true".equals(p.getValue());
1813      } else if (p.getCode().equals("ig-expansion-parameters")) {     
1814        expParamMap.put(p.getCode(), p.getValue());
1815      } else if (p.getCode().equals("special-url")) {     
1816        listedURLExemptions.add(p.getValue());
1817      } else if (p.getCode().equals("template-openapi")) {     
1818        openApiTemplate = p.getValue();
1819      } else if (p.getCode().equals("template-html")) {     
1820        htmlTemplate = p.getValue();
1821      } else if (p.getCode().equals("template-md")) {     
1822        mdTemplate = p.getValue();
1823      } else if (p.getCode().equals("path-binary")) {     
1824        binaryPaths.add(Utilities.path(rootDir, p.getValue()));
1825      } else if (p.getCode().equals("show-inherited-invariants")) {     
1826        allInvariants = "true".equals(p.getValue());
1827      } else if (p.getCode().equals("apply-contact") && p.getValue().equals("true")) {
1828        contacts = sourceIg.getContact();
1829      } else if (p.getCode().equals("apply-context") && p.getValue().equals("true")) {
1830        contexts = sourceIg.getUseContext();
1831      } else if (p.getCode().equals("apply-copyright") && p.getValue().equals("true")) {
1832        copyright = sourceIg.getCopyright();
1833      } else if (p.getCode().equals("apply-jurisdiction") && p.getValue().equals("true")) {
1834        jurisdictions = sourceIg.getJurisdiction();
1835      } else if (p.getCode().equals("apply-license") && p.getValue().equals("true")) {
1836        licenseInfo = sourceIg.getLicense();
1837      } else if (p.getCode().equals("apply-publisher") && p.getValue().equals("true")) {
1838        publisher = sourceIg.getPublisher();
1839      } else if (p.getCode().equals("apply-version") && p.getValue().equals("true")) {
1840        businessVersion = sourceIg.getVersion();
1841      } else if (p.getCode().equals("generate-version")) {     
1842        generateVersions.add(p.getValue());
1843      } else if (p.getCode().equals("version-comparison")) {     
1844        if (comparisonVersions == null) {
1845          comparisonVersions = new ArrayList<>();
1846        }
1847        if ("n/a".equals(p.getValue())) {
1848          comparisonVersions.add(p.getValue());
1849        }        
1850      } else if (p.getCode().equals("validation")) {
1851        if (p.getValue().equals("check-must-support"))
1852          hintAboutNonMustSupport = true;
1853        else if (p.getValue().equals("allow-any-extensions"))
1854          anyExtensionsAllowed = true;
1855        else if (p.getValue().equals("check-aggregation"))
1856          checkAggregation = true;
1857        else if (p.getValue().equals("no-broken-links"))
1858          brokenLinksError = true;
1859        else if (p.getValue().equals("show-reference-messages"))
1860          showReferenceMessages = true;
1861      }
1862      count++;
1863    }
1864    
1865    // ok process the paths
1866    log("Root directory: "+rootDir);
1867    if (resourceDirs.isEmpty())
1868      resourceDirs.add(Utilities.path(rootDir, "resources"));
1869    if (pagesDirs.isEmpty())
1870      pagesDirs.add(Utilities.path(rootDir, "pages"));
1871    if (mode == IGBuildMode.WEBSERVER) 
1872      vsCache = Utilities.path(System.getProperty("java.io.tmpdir"), "fhircache");
1873    else if (vsCache == null) {
1874     if (mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD)
1875       vsCache = Utilities.path(System.getProperty("java.io.tmpdir"), "fhircache");
1876     else
1877       vsCache = Utilities.path(System.getProperty("user.home"), "fhircache");
1878    }
1879    
1880    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Check folders");
1881    List<String> missingDirs = new ArrayList<String>();
1882    for (String s : resourceDirs) {
1883      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Source: "+s);
1884      if (!checkDir(s, true))
1885        missingDirs.add(s);
1886    }
1887    resourceDirs.removeAll(missingDirs);
1888    
1889    missingDirs.clear();
1890    for (String s : pagesDirs) {
1891      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Pages: "+s);
1892      if (!checkDir(s, true))
1893        missingDirs.add(s);
1894    }
1895    pagesDirs.removeAll(missingDirs);
1896
1897    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Temp: "+tempDir);
1898    Utilities.clearDirectory(tempDir);
1899    forceDir(tempDir);
1900    forceDir(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_includes"));
1901    forceDir(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data"));
1902    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Output: "+outputDir);
1903    forceDir(outputDir);
1904    Utilities.clearDirectory(outputDir);
1905    if (qaDir != null) {
1906      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "QA Dir: "+qaDir);
1907      forceDir(qaDir);
1908    }
1909    makeQA = mode == IGBuildMode.WEBSERVER ? false : qaDir != null;
1910
1911    if (Utilities.existsInList(version.substring(0,  3), "1.0", "1.4", "1.6", "3.0"))
1912      markdownEngine = new MarkDownProcessor(Dialect.DARING_FIREBALL);
1913    else
1914      markdownEngine = new MarkDownProcessor(Dialect.COMMON_MARK);
1915    
1916    // loading the specifications
1917    context = loadCorePackage();
1918    context.setProgress(true);
1919    context.setIgnoreProfileErrors(true);
1920    context.setLogger(logger);
1921    context.setAllowLoadingDuplicates(true);
1922    context.setExpandCodesLimit(1000);
1923    context.setExpansionProfile(makeExpProfile());
1924
1925    // initializing the tx sub-system
1926    Utilities.createDirectory(vsCache);
1927    if (cacheOption == CacheOption.CLEAR_ALL) {
1928      log("Terminology Cache is at "+vsCache+". Clearing now");
1929      Utilities.clearDirectory(vsCache);
1930    } else if (mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD) {
1931      log("Terminology Cache is at "+vsCache+". Trimming now");
1932      Utilities.clearDirectory(vsCache, "snomed.cache", "loinc.cache", "ucum.cache");
1933    } else if (cacheOption == CacheOption.CLEAR_ERRORS) {
1934      log("Terminology Cache is at "+vsCache+". Clearing Errors now");
1935      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Deleted "+Integer.toString(clearErrors(vsCache))+" files");
1936    } else {
1937      log("Terminology Cache is at "+vsCache+". "+Integer.toString(Utilities.countFilesInDirectory(vsCache))+" files in cache");
1938    }
1939    if (!new File(vsCache).exists())
1940      throw new Exception("Unable to access or create the cache directory at "+vsCache);
1941    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Load Terminology Cache from "+vsCache);
1942    context.initTS(vsCache);
1943    if (expParams != null) {
1944      context.setExpansionProfile((Parameters) VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(FormatUtilities.loadFile(Utilities.path(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(igName), expParams))));
1945    } else if (!expParamMap.isEmpty()) {
1946      context.setExpansionProfile(new Parameters());      
1947    }
1948    for (String n : expParamMap.values())
1949      context.getExpansionParameters().addParameter(n, expParamMap.get(n));
1950    
1951    txLog = Utilities.createTempFile("fhir-ig-", ".log").getAbsolutePath();
1952    if (mode != IGBuildMode.WEBSERVER) {
1953      if (txServer == null || !txServer.contains(":")) {
1954        log("WARNING: Running without terminology server - terminology content will likely not publish correctly");
1955        context.setCanRunWithoutTerminology(true);
1956        txLog = null;
1957      } else {
1958        log("Connect to Terminology Server at "+txServer);
1959        checkTSVersion(vsCache, context.connectToTSServer(TerminologyClientFactory.makeClient(txServer, "fhir/publisher", FhirPublication.fromCode(version)), txLog));
1960      }
1961    } else 
1962      checkTSVersion(vsCache, context.connectToTSServer(TerminologyClientFactory.makeClient(webTxServer.getAddress(), "fhir/publisher", FhirPublication.fromCode(version)), txLog));
1963    
1964    loadPubPack();
1965    igpkp = new IGKnowledgeProvider(context, checkAppendSlash(specPath), determineCanonical(sourceIg.getUrl(), "ImplementationGuide.url"), template.config(), errors, VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(version), template, listedURLExemptions);
1966    if (autoLoad) {
1967      igpkp.setAutoPath(true);
1968    }
1969    fetcher.setPkp(igpkp);
1970    template.loadSummaryRows(igpkp.summaryRows());
1971    if (!dependsOnUTG(sourceIg.getDependsOn()) && !sourceIg.getPackageId().contains("hl7.terminology")) {
1972      loadUTG();
1973    }
1974    
1975    inspector = new HTLMLInspector(outputDir, specMaps, this, igpkp.getCanonical(), sourceIg.getPackageId());
1976    inspector.getManual().add("full-ig.zip");
1977    if (historyPage != null) {
1978      inspector.getManual().add(historyPage);
1979      inspector.getManual().add(Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), historyPage));
1980    }
1981    inspector.getManual().add("qa.html");
1982    inspector.getManual().add("qa-tx.html");
1983    inspector.getExemptHtmlPatterns().addAll(exemptHtmlPatterns);
1984    inspector.setPcm(pcm);
1985    
1986    int i = 0;
1987    for (ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent dep : sourceIg.getDependsOn()) {
1988      loadIg(dep, i);
1989      i++;
1990    }
1991    generateLoadedSnapshots();
1992    
1993    // set up validator;
1994    validator = new InstanceValidator(context, new IGPublisherHostServices(), context.getXVer()); // todo: host services for reference resolution....
1995    validator.setAllowXsiLocation(true);
1996    validator.setNoBindingMsgSuppressed(true);
1997    validator.setNoExtensibleWarnings(true);
1998    validator.setHintAboutNonMustSupport(hintAboutNonMustSupport);
1999    validator.setAnyExtensionsAllowed(anyExtensionsAllowed);
2000    validator.setAllowExamples(true);
2001    validator.setCrumbTrails(true);
2002    validator.setWantCheckSnapshotUnchanged(true);
2003    
2004    pvalidator = new ProfileValidator(context, context.getXVer());
2005    csvalidator = new CodeSystemValidator(context, context.getXVer());
2006    pvalidator.setCheckAggregation(checkAggregation);
2007    pvalidator.setCheckMustSupport(hintAboutNonMustSupport);
2008    validator.setShowMessagesFromReferences(showReferenceMessages);
2009    validator.getExtensionDomains().addAll(extensionDomains);
2010    validator.getExtensionDomains().add(IGHelper.EXT_PRIVATE_BASE);
2011    validationFetcher = new ValidationServices(context, igpkp, fileList, npmList, bundleReferencesResolve);
2012    validator.setFetcher(validationFetcher);
2013    validator.setTracker(this);
2014    for (String s : context.getBinaries().keySet()) {
2015      if (needFile(s)) {
2016        if (makeQA)
2017          checkMakeFile(context.getBinaries().get(s), Utilities.path(qaDir, s), otherFilesStartup);
2018        checkMakeFile(context.getBinaries().get(s), Utilities.path(tempDir, s), otherFilesStartup);
2019      }
2020    }
2021    otherFilesStartup.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data"));
2022    otherFilesStartup.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "fhir.json"));
2023    otherFilesStartup.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "structuredefinitions.json"));
2024    otherFilesStartup.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "questionnaires.json"));
2025    otherFilesStartup.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "pages.json"));
2026    otherFilesStartup.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_includes"));
2027
2028    if (sourceIg.hasLicense())
2029      license = sourceIg.getLicense().toCode();
2030    npmName = sourceIg.getPackageId();
2031    if (Utilities.noString(npmName)) {
2032      throw new Error("No packageId provided in the implementation guide resource - cannot build this IG");
2033    }
2034    appendTrailingSlashInDataFile = true;
2035    includeHeadings = template.getIncludeHeadings();
2036    igArtifactsPage = template.getIGArtifactsPage();
2037    doTransforms = template.getDoTransforms();
2038    template.getExtraTemplates(extraTemplates);
2039    
2040    for (Extension e : sourceIg.getExtensionsByUrl(IGHelper.EXT_SPREADSHEET)) {
2041      spreadsheets.add(e.getValue().primitiveValue());
2042    }
2043    ToolingExtensions.removeExtension(sourceIg, IGHelper.EXT_SPREADSHEET);
2044
2045    for (Extension e : sourceIg.getExtensionsByUrl(IGHelper.EXT_MAPPING_CSV)) {
2046      mappings.add(e.getValue().primitiveValue());
2047    }
2048    for (Extension e : sourceIg.getExtensionsByUrl(IGHelper.EXT_BUNDLE)) {
2049      bundles.add(e.getValue().primitiveValue());
2050    }
2051    if (mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD)
2052      extensionTracker.setoptIn(true);
2053    else if (npmName.contains("hl7.") || npmName.contains("argonaut.") || npmName.contains("ihe."))
2054      extensionTracker.setoptIn(true);
2055    else if (useStatsOptOut != null) 
2056      extensionTracker.setoptIn(!useStatsOptOut);
2057    else
2058      extensionTracker.setoptIn(!ini.getBooleanProperty("IG", "usage-stats-opt-out"));
2059    
2060    log("Initialization complete");
2061  }
2062
2063  private void generateLoadedSnapshots() {
2064    for (StructureDefinition sd : context.allStructures()) {
2065      if (!sd.hasSnapshot() && sd.hasBaseDefinition()) {
2066        generateSnapshot(sd);
2067      }
2068    }
2069  }
2070
2071  private void generateSnapshot(StructureDefinition sd) {
2072    List<ValidationMessage> messages = new ArrayList<>();
2073    ProfileUtilities utils = new ProfileUtilities(context, messages, igpkp);
2074    StructureDefinition base = context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, sd.getBaseDefinition());
2075    if (base == null) {
2076      System.out.println("Cannot find or generate snapshot for base definition "+sd.getBaseDefinition()+" from "+sd.getUrl());
2077    } else {
2078      if (!base.hasSnapshot()) {
2079        generateSnapshot(base);
2080      }
2081      utils.setIds(sd, true);
2082      try {
2083        utils.generateSnapshot(base, sd, sd.getUrl(), Utilities.extractBaseUrl(base.getUserString("path")), sd.getName());
2084        if (!sd.hasSnapshot()) {
2085          System.out.println("Unable to generate snapshot for "+sd.getUrl()+": "+messages.toString());        
2086        }
2087      } catch (Exception e) {
2088        System.out.println("Exception generating snapshot for "+sd.getUrl()+": "+e.getMessage());        
2089      }      
2090    }
2091    
2092  }
2093
2094  private boolean dependsOnUTG(JsonArray arr) throws Exception {
2095    if (arr == null) {
2096      return false;
2097    }
2098    for (JsonElement d : arr) {
2099      JsonObject dep = (JsonObject) d;
2100      String canonical = ostr(dep, "location");
2101      if (canonical != null && canonical.contains("terminology.hl7")) {
2102        return true;
2103      }
2104      String packageId = ostr(dep, "package");
2105      if (packageId != null && packageId.contains("hl7.terminology")) {
2106        return true;
2107      }
2108    }
2109    return false;
2110  }
2111
2112
2113  private boolean dependsOnUTG(List<ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent> dependsOn) {
2114    for (ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent d : dependsOn) {
2115      if (d.hasPackageId() && d.getPackageId().contains("hl7.terminology")) {
2116        return true;
2117      }
2118      if (d.hasUri() && d.getUri().contains("terminology.hl7")) {
2119        return true;
2120      }
2121    }
2122    return false;
2123  }
2124
2125  private String determineCanonical(String url, String path) throws FHIRException {
2126    if (url == null)
2127      return url;
2128    if (url.contains("/ImplementationGuide/"))
2129      return url.substring(0, url.indexOf("/ImplementationGuide/"));
2130    if (path != null) {
2131      errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.INVALID, path, "The canonical URL for an Implementation Guide must point directly to the implementation guide resource, not to the Implementation Guide as a whole", IssueSeverity.WARNING));
2132    }
2133    return url;
2134  }
2135
2136
2137  private String pathForVersion() {
2138    String v = version;
2139    while (v.indexOf(".") != v.lastIndexOf(".")) {
2140      v = v.substring(0, v.lastIndexOf("."));
2141    }
2142    if (v.equals("1.0"))
2143      return PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl("http://hl7.org/fhir/DSTU2");
2144    if (v.equals("1.4"))
2145      return PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl("http://hl7.org/fhir/2016May");
2146    if (v.equals("3.0"))
2147      return PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl("http://hl7.org/fhir/STU3");
2148    if (v.equals("4.0"))
2149      return PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl("http://hl7.org/fhir/R4");
2150    if (v.equals("4.1"))
2151      return PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl("http://hl7.org/fhir/2021Mar");
2152    return PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl("http://build.fhir.org");
2153  }
2154
2155
2156  private String processVersion(String v) {
2157    return v.equals("$build") ? Constants.VERSION : v;
2158  }

2160
2161  private void initializeFromJson() throws Exception {
2162    JsonObject configuration = null;
2163    if (configFile == null) {
2164      adHocTmpDir = Utilities.path(System.getProperty("java.io.tmpdir"), "fhir-ig-scratch");
2165      log("Using inbuilt IG template in "+sourceDir);
2166      copyDefaultTemplate();
2167      buildConfigFile();
2168    } else
2169      log("Load Configuration from "+configFile);
2170    if (!new File(configFile).exists())
2171      throw new Exception("Unable to find file " + configFile + " and no ig.ini file specified - nothing to build.");
2172    try {
2173      configuration = JsonTrackingParser.parseJsonFile(configFile);
2174    } catch (Exception e) {
2175      throw new Exception("Error Reading JSON Config file at "+configFile+": "+e.getMessage(), e);
2176    }
2177    repoRoot = Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(configFile);
2178    if (configuration.has("redirect")) { // redirect to support auto-build for complex projects with IG folder in subdirectory
2179      String redirectFile = Utilities.path(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(configFile), configuration.get("redirect").getAsString());
2180      log("Redirecting to Configuration from " + redirectFile);
2181      configFile = redirectFile;
2182      configuration = JsonTrackingParser.parseJsonFile(redirectFile);
2183    }

2530  private void loadPubPack() throws FHIRException, IOException {
2531    NpmPackage npm = pcm.loadPackage("hl7.fhir.pubpack", "0.0.9");
2532    context.loadFromPackage(npm, null);
2533    npm = pcm.loadPackage("hl7.fhir.xver-extensions", "0.0.5");
2534    context.loadFromPackage(npm, null);
2535  }
2536
2537  private void loadUTG() throws FHIRException, IOException {
2538    String vs = null;
2539    if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(version)) {
2540      vs = "hl7.terminology.r3";
2541    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(version)) {
2542      vs = "hl7.terminology.r4";
2543    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR5Ver(version)) {
2544      vs = "hl7.terminology.r5";
2545    }
2546    if (vs != null) {
2547      NpmPackage npm = pcm.loadPackage(vs, null);
2548      SpecMapManager spm = new SpecMapManager(TextFile.streamToBytes(npm.load("other", "spec.internals")), npm.fhirVersion());
2549      IContextResourceLoader loader = new PublisherLoader(npm, spm, npm.getWebLocation(), igpkp).makeLoader();
2550      context.loadFromPackage(npm, loader);
2551    }
2552  }
