2555  private void processExtraTemplates(JsonArray templates) throws Exception {
2556    if (templates!=null) {
2557      boolean hasDefns = false;  // is definitions page in list of templates?
2558      boolean hasFormat = false; // are format pages in list of templates?
2559      boolean setExtras = false; // See if templates explicitly declare which are examples/history or whether we need to infer by name
2560      String name = null;
2561      for (JsonElement template : templates) {
2562        if (template.isJsonPrimitive())
2563          name = template.getAsString();
2564        else {
2565          if (!((JsonObject)template).has("name") || !((JsonObject)template).has("description"))
2566            throw new Exception("extraTemplates must be an array of objects with 'name' and 'description' properties");
2567          name = ((JsonObject)template).get("name").getAsString();
2568          if (((JsonObject)template).has("isHistory") || ((JsonObject)template).has("isExamples"))
2569            setExtras = true;
2570        }
2571        if (name.equals("defns"))
2572          hasDefns = true;
2573        else if (name.equals("format"))
2574          hasFormat = true;
2575        
2576      }
2577      if (!hasDefns) {
2578        extraTemplateList.add("defns");
2579        extraTemplates.put("defns", "Definitions");
2580      }
2581      if (!hasFormat) {
2582        extraTemplateList.add("format");
2583        extraTemplates.put("format", "FMT Representation");
2584      }
2585      for (JsonElement template : templates) {
2586        if (template.isJsonPrimitive()) {
2587          extraTemplateList.add(template.getAsString());
2588          extraTemplates.put(template.getAsString(), template.getAsString());
2589          if (template.equals("examples"))
2590            exampleTemplates.add(template.getAsString());
2591          if (template.getAsString().endsWith("-history"))
2592            historyTemplates.add(template.getAsString());
2593        } else {
2594          String templateName = ((JsonObject)template).get("name").getAsString();
2595          extraTemplateList.add(templateName);
2596          extraTemplates.put(templateName, ((JsonObject)template).get("description").getAsString());
2597          if (!setExtras) {
2598            if (templateName.equals("examples"))
2599              exampleTemplates.add(templateName);
2600            if (templateName.endsWith("-history"))
2601              historyTemplates.add(templateName);
2602          } else if (((JsonObject)template).has("isExamples") && ((JsonObject)template).get("isExamples").getAsBoolean()) {
2603            exampleTemplates.add(templateName);
2604          } else if (((JsonObject)template).has("isHistory") && ((JsonObject)template).get("isHistory").getAsBoolean()) {
2605            historyTemplates.add(templateName);
2606          }            
2607        }
2608      }
2609    }
2610  }
2611
2612  void handlePreProcess(JsonObject pp, String root) throws Exception {
2613    String path = Utilities.path(root, str(pp, "folder"));
2614    if (checkDir(path, true)) {
2615      prePagesDirs.add(path);
2616      String prePagesXslt = null;
2617      if (pp.has("transform")) {
2618        prePagesXslt = Utilities.path(root, str(pp, "transform"));
2619        checkFile(prePagesXslt);
2620      }
2621      String relativePath = null;
2622      if (pp.has("relativePath")) {
2623        relativePath = str(pp, "relativePath");
2624      }
2625      System.out.println("Pre-Process: "+path+" = "+relativePath+" | "+prePagesXslt);
2626      PreProcessInfo ppinfo = new PreProcessInfo(prePagesXslt, relativePath);
2627      preProcessInfo.put(path, ppinfo);
2628    }
2629  }
2630
2631  private void loadSuppressedMessages(String messageFile, String path) throws Exception {
2632    File f = new File(messageFile);
2633    if (!f.exists()) {
2634      errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.NOTFOUND, path, "Supressed messages file not found", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
2635    } else {
2636      String s = TextFile.fileToString(messageFile);
2637      if (s.toLowerCase().startsWith("== suppressed messages ==")) {
2638        String[] lines = s.split("\\r?\\n");
2639        String reason = null;
2640        for (int i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
2641          String l = lines[i].trim();
2642          if (!Utilities.noString(l)) {
2643            if (l.startsWith("# ")) {
2644              reason = l.substring(2);
2645            } else {
2646              if (reason == null) { 
2647                errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.NOTFOUND, path, "Supressed messages file has errors with no reason ("+l+")", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
2648                suppressedMessages.add(l, "?pub-msg-1?");
2649              } else {
2650                suppressedMessages.add(l, reason);
2651              }
2652            }
2653          }
2654        }
2655      } else {
2656        errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.NOTFOUND, path, "Supressed messages file is not using the new format (see https://confluence.hl7.org/display/FHIR/Implementation+Guide+Parameters)", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
2657        InputStreamReader r = new InputStreamReader(new FileInputStream(messageFile));
2658        StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
2659        while (r.ready()) {
2660          char c = (char) r.read();
2661          if (c == '\r' || c == '\n') {
2662            if (b.length() > 0)
2663              suppressedMessages.add(b.toString(), "?pub-msg-2?");
2664            b = new StringBuilder();
2665          } else
2666            b.append(c);
2667        }
2668        if (b.length() > 0)
2669          suppressedMessages.add(b.toString(), "?pub-msg-3?");
2670        r.close();
2671      }
2672    }
2673  }
2674  
2675  private void checkTSVersion(String dir, String version) throws FileNotFoundException, IOException {
2676    if (Utilities.noString(version))
2677      return;
2678
2679    // we wipe the terminology cache if the terminology server version has changed
2680    File verFile = new File(Utilities.path(dir, "version.ctl"));
2681    if (verFile.exists()) {
2682      String ver = TextFile.fileToString(verFile);
2683      if (!ver.equals(FIXED_CACHE_VERSION+"|"+version)) {
2684        if (!ver.startsWith(FIXED_CACHE_VERSION+"|")) {
2685          if (!ver.contains("|")) {
2686            logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Terminology Cache Version has changed from 1 to "+FIXED_CACHE_VERSION+", so clearing txCache");
2687          } else {
2688            logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Terminology Cache Version has changed from "+ver.substring(0, ver.indexOf("|"))+" to "+FIXED_CACHE_VERSION+", so clearing txCache");
2689          }
2690        } else {
2691          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Terminology Server Version has changed from "+ver.substring(ver.indexOf("|")+1)+" to "+version+", so clearing txCache");
2692        }
2693        Utilities.clearDirectory(dir);
2694        context.clearTS();
2695      }
2696    }
2697    TextFile.stringToFile(FIXED_CACHE_VERSION+"|"+version, verFile, false);
2698  }

2701  private int clearErrors(String dirName) throws FileNotFoundException, IOException {
2702    File dir = new File(dirName);
2703    int i = 0;
2704    for (File f : dir.listFiles()) {
2705      String s = TextFile.fileToString(f);
2706      if (s.contains("OperationOutcome")) {
2707        f.delete();
2708        i++;
2709      }
2710    }
2711    return i;
2712  }

2744  private void copyDefaultTemplate() throws IOException, FHIRException {
2745    if (!new File(adHocTmpDir).exists())
2746      Utilities.createDirectory(adHocTmpDir);
2747    Utilities.clearDirectory(adHocTmpDir);
2748
2749    FilesystemPackageCacheManager pcm = new FilesystemPackageCacheManager(true, ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION);
2750    
2751    NpmPackage npm = null; 
2752    if (specifiedVersion == null) {
2753      npm = pcm.loadPackage("hl7.fhir.r5.core", Constants.VERSION);
2754    } else {
2755      String vid = VersionUtilities.getCurrentVersion(specifiedVersion);
2756      String pid = VersionUtilities.packageForVersion(vid);
2757      npm = pcm.loadPackage(pid, vid);
2758    }
2759    
2760    ZipInputStream zip = new ZipInputStream(npm.load("other", "ig-template.zip"));
2761    byte[] buffer = new byte[2048];
2762    ZipEntry entry;
2763    while((entry = zip.getNextEntry())!=null) {
2764      String filename = Utilities.path(adHocTmpDir, entry.getName());
2765      String dir = Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(filename);
2766      Utilities.createDirectory(dir);
2767      FileOutputStream output = new FileOutputStream(filename);
2768      int len = 0;
2769      while ((len = zip.read(buffer)) > 0)
2770        output.write(buffer, 0, len);
2771      output.close();
2772    }
2773    zip.close();
2774  }

2804  private SimpleWorkerContext loadCorePackage() throws Exception {
2805    NpmPackage pi = null;
2806    
2807    String v = version.equals(Constants.VERSION) ? "current" : version;
2808
2809    if (Utilities.noString(igPack)) {
2810      System.out.println("Core Package "+VersionUtilities.packageForVersion(v)+"#"+v);
2811      pi = pcm.loadPackage(VersionUtilities.packageForVersion(v), v);
2812    } else {
2813      System.out.println("Load from provided file "+igPack);
2814      pi = NpmPackage.fromPackage(new FileInputStream(igPack));
2815    }
2816    if (pi == null) {
2817      // gg: I don't think this works anymore
2818      throw new Error("Unsupported code - contact Grahame Grieve");
2819//      String url = getMasterSource();
2820//      InputStream src = fetchFromSource("hl7.fhir.core-"+v, url);
2821//      pi = pcm.addPackageToCache("hl7.fhir.core", v, src, url);
2822    }
2823    if (v.equals("current")) {
2824      // currency of the current core package is a problem, since its not really version controlled.
2825      // we'll check for a specified version...
2826      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Checking hl7.fhir.core-"+v+" currency");
2827      int cacheVersion = getBuildVersionForCorePackage(pi);
2828      int lastAcceptableVersion = ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION;
2829      if (cacheVersion < lastAcceptableVersion) {
2830        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Updating hl7.fhir.core-"+version+" package from source (too old - is "+cacheVersion+", must be "+lastAcceptableVersion);
2831        pi = pcm.addPackageToCache("hl7.fhir.core", "current", fetchFromSource("hl7.fhir.core-"+v, getMasterSource()), getMasterSource());
2832      } else {
2833        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "   ...  ok: is "+cacheVersion+", must be "+lastAcceptableVersion);
2834      }
2835    }
2836    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Load hl7.fhir.core-"+v+" package from "+pi.summary());
2837    npmList.add(pi);
2838    
2839    SpecMapManager spm = loadSpecDetails(TextFile.streamToBytes(pi.load("other", "spec.internals")));
2840    SimpleWorkerContext sp;
2841    IContextResourceLoader loader = new PublisherLoader(pi, spm, specPath, igpkp).makeLoader();
2842    sp = SimpleWorkerContext.fromPackage(pi, loader);
2843    sp.loadBinariesFromFolder(pi);
2844    sp.setCacheId(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
2845    if (!version.equals(Constants.VERSION)) {
2846      // If it wasn't a 4.0 source, we need to set the ids because they might not have been set in the source
2847      ProfileUtilities utils = new ProfileUtilities(context, new ArrayList<ValidationMessage>(), igpkp);
2848      for (StructureDefinition sd : sp.allStructures()) {
2849        utils.setIds(sd, true);
2850      }
2851    }
2852    return sp;    
2853  }

2855  private int getBuildVersionForCorePackage(NpmPackage pi) throws IOException {
2856    if (!pi.getNpm().has("tools-version"))
2857      return 0;
2858    return pi.getNpm().get("tools-version").getAsInt();
2859  }

2862  private String getMasterSource() {
2863    if (VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(version)) return "http://hl7.org/fhir/DSTU2/hl7.fhir.r2.core.tgz";
2864    if (VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(version)) return "http://hl7.org/fhir/2016May/hl7.fhir.r2b.core.tgz";
2865    if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(version)) return "http://hl7.org/fhir/STU3/hl7.fhir.r3.core.tgz";
2866    if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(version)) return "http://hl7.org/fhir/STU3/hl7.fhir.r4.core.tgz";
2867    if (Constants.VERSION.equals(version)) return "http://build.fhir.org/package.tgz";
2868    throw new Error("unknown version "+version);
2869  }

2871  private InputStream fetchFromSource(String id, String source) throws IOException {
2872    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Fetch "+id+" package from "+source);
2873    URL url = new URL(source+"?nocache=" + System.currentTimeMillis());
2874    URLConnection c = url.openConnection();
2875    return c.getInputStream();
2876  }

2885  private void loadIg(ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent dep, int index) throws Exception {
2886    String name = dep.getId();
2887    if (!dep.hasId()) {
2888      logMessage("Dependency '"+idForDep(dep)+"' has no id, so can't be referred to in markdown in the IG");
2889      name = "u"+Utilities.makeUuidLC().replace("-", "");
2890    }
2891    if (!isValidIGToken(name))
2892      throw new Exception("IG Name must be a valid token ("+name+")");
2893    String canonical = determineCanonical(dep.getUri(), "ImplementationGuide.dependency["+index+"].url");
2894    String packageId = dep.getPackageId();
2895    if (Utilities.noString(packageId))
2896      packageId = pcm.getPackageId(canonical);
2897    if (Utilities.noString(canonical) && !Utilities.noString(packageId))
2898      canonical = pcm.getPackageUrl(packageId);
2899    if (Utilities.noString(canonical))
2900      throw new Exception("You must specify a canonical URL for the IG "+name);
2901    String igver = dep.getVersion();
2902    if (Utilities.noString(igver))
2903      throw new Exception("You must specify a version for the IG "+packageId+" ("+canonical+")");
2904    
2905    NpmPackage pi = packageId == null ? null : pcm.loadPackageFromCacheOnly(packageId, igver);
2906    if (pi != null)
2907      npmList.add(pi);
2908    if (pi == null) {
2909      pi = resolveDependency(canonical, packageId, igver);
2910      if (pi == null) {
2911        if (Utilities.noString(packageId))
2912          throw new Exception("Package Id for guide at "+canonical+" is unknown (contact FHIR Product Director");
2913        else
2914          throw new Exception("Unknown Package "+packageId+"#"+igver);
2915      }
2916    }
2917    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Load "+name+" ("+canonical+") from "+packageId+"#"+igver);
2918
2919    if (dep.hasUri() && !dep.getUri().contains("/ImplementationGuide/")) {
2920      String cu = getIgUri(pi);
2921      if (cu != null) {
2922        errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.INFORMATIONAL, "ImplementationGuide.dependency["+index+"].url", 
2923            "The correct canonical URL for this dependency is "+cu, IssueSeverity.INFORMATION));
2924      }
2925    }
2926    String webref = pi.getWebLocation();
2927    webref = PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl(webref);
2928
2929    SpecMapManager igm = pi.hasFile("other", "spec.internals") ?  new SpecMapManager( TextFile.streamToBytes(pi.load("other", "spec.internals")), pi.fhirVersion()) : SpecMapManager.createSpecialPackage(pi);
2930    igm.setName(name);
2931    igm.setBase(canonical);
2932    igm.setBase2(PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl(pi.url()));
2933    specMaps.add(igm);
2934    if (!VersionUtilities.versionsCompatible(version, igm.getVersion())) {
2935      log("Version mismatch. This IG is version "+version+", while the IG '"+name+"' is from version "+igm.getVersion()+" (will try to run anyway)");
2936    }
2937    
2938    loadFromPackage(name, canonical, pi, webref, igm);
2939    
2940  }

2943  private boolean isValidIGToken(String tail) {
2944      if (tail == null || tail.length() == 0)
2945        return false;
2946      boolean result = Utilities.isAlphabetic(tail.charAt(0));
2947      for (int i = 1; i < tail.length(); i++) {
2948        result = result && (Utilities.isAlphabetic(tail.charAt(i)) || Utilities.isDigit(tail.charAt(i)) || (tail.charAt(i) == '_'));
2949      }
2950      return result;
2951
2952  }

2954  private String idForDep(ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent dep) {
2955    if (dep.hasPackageId()) {
2956      return dep.getPackageId();
2957    }
2958    if (dep.hasUri()) {
2959      return dep.getUri();
2960    }
2961    return "{no id}";
2962  }

2966  private String getIgUri(NpmPackage pi) throws IOException {
2967    for (String rs : pi.listResources("ImplementationGuide")) {
2968      JsonObject json = JsonTrackingParser.parseJson(pi.loadResource(rs));
2969      if (json.has("packageId") && json.get("packageId").getAsString().equals(pi.name()) && json.has("url")) {
2970        return json.get("url").getAsString();
2971      }
2972    }
2973    return null;
2974  }

2978  public void loadFromPackage(String name, String canonical, NpmPackage pi, String webref, SpecMapManager igm) throws IOException {
2979    for (String dep : pi.dependencies()) {
2980      if (!context.hasPackage(dep)) {        
2981        String coreVersion = VersionUtilities.getVersionForPackage(dep);
2982        if (coreVersion != null) {
2983          log("Ignore Core Dependency on FHIR version "+coreVersion+", from package '"+pi.name()+"#"+pi.version()+"'");
2984        } else {
2985          NpmPackage dpi = pcm.loadPackage(dep);
2986          if (dpi == null) {
2987            logDebugMessage(LogCategory.CONTEXT, "Unable to find package dependency "+dep+". Will proceed, but likely to be be errors in qz.html etc");
2988          } else {
2989            if (!VersionUtilities.versionsCompatible(version, pi.fhirVersion())) {
2990              log("Version mismatch. This IG is for FHIR version "+version+", while the package '"+pi.name()+"#"+pi.version()+"' is for FHIR version "+pi.fhirVersion()+" (will ignore that and try to run anyway)");
2991            }
2992            logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Load package dependency "+dep);
2993            SpecMapManager smm = dpi.hasFile("other", "spec.internals") ?  new SpecMapManager(TextFile.streamToBytes(dpi.load("other", "spec.internals")), dpi.fhirVersion()) : SpecMapManager.createSpecialPackage(dpi);
2994            smm.setName(dpi.name());
2995            smm.setBase(dpi.canonical());
2996            smm.setBase2(PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl(dpi.url()));
2997            specMaps.add(smm);
2998            loadFromPackage(dpi.title(), dpi.canonical(), dpi, dpi.url(), smm);          
2999          }
3000        }
3001      }
3002    }
3003    IContextResourceLoader loader = new PublisherLoader(pi, igm, webref, igpkp).makeLoader();
3004    context.loadFromPackage(pi, loader);
3005  }

3007  private void loadIg(JsonObject dep) throws Exception {
3008    String name = str(dep, "name");
3009    if (!isValidIGToken(name))
3010      throw new Exception("IG Name must be a valid token ("+name+")");
3011    String canonical = ostr(dep, "location");
3012    String igver = ostr(dep, "version");
3013    if (Utilities.noString(igver))
3014      throw new Exception("You must specify a version for the IG "+name+" ("+canonical+")");
3015    String packageId = ostr(dep, "package");
3016    if (Utilities.noString(packageId))
3017      packageId = pcm.getPackageId(canonical);
3018    if (Utilities.noString(canonical) && !Utilities.noString(packageId))
3019      canonical = pcm.getPackageUrl(packageId);
3020    
3021    NpmPackage pi = packageId == null ? null : pcm.loadPackageFromCacheOnly(packageId, igver);
3022    if (pi != null)
3023      npmList.add(pi);
3024    if (pi == null) {
3025      if (Utilities.noString(canonical))
3026        throw new Exception("You must specify a canonical URL for the IG "+name);
3027      pi = resolveDependency(canonical, packageId, igver);
3028      if (pi == null) {
3029        if (Utilities.noString(packageId))
3030          throw new Exception("Package Id for guide at "+canonical+" is unknown (contact FHIR Product Director");
3031        else
3032          throw new Exception("Unknown Package "+packageId+"#"+igver);
3033      }
3034    }
3035    if (packageId == null) {
3036      packageId = pi.name();
3037    }
3038    if (Utilities.noString(canonical)) {
3039      canonical = pi.canonical();
3040    }
3041  
3042    log("Load "+name+" ("+canonical+") from "+packageId+"#"+igver);
3043    if (ostr(dep, "package") == null && packageId != null)
3044      dep.addProperty("package", packageId);
3045
3046    String webref = pi.getWebLocation();
3047    String location = dep.has("location") ? dep.get("location").getAsString() : ""; 
3048    if (location.startsWith(".."))
3049      webref = location;
3050    webref = PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl(webref);
3051    
3052    String ver = pi.fhirVersion();
3053    SpecMapManager igm = new SpecMapManager(TextFile.streamToBytes(pi.load("other", "spec.internals")), ver);
3054    igm.setName(name);
3055    igm.setBase2(PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl(webref));
3056    igm.setBase(canonical);
3057    specMaps.add(igm);
3058    if (!VersionUtilities.versionsCompatible(version, igm.getVersion())) {
3059      log("Version mismatch. This IG is for FHIR version "+version+", while the IG '"+pi.name()+"#"+pi.version()+"' is for FHIR version "+igm.getVersion()+" (will try to run anyway)");
3060    }
3061    
3062    loadFromPackage(name, canonical, pi, webref, igm);
3063    jsonDependencies .add(new JsonDependency(name, canonical, pi.name(), pi.version()));
3064  }

3066
3067  private NpmPackage resolveDependency(String canonical, String packageId, String igver) throws Exception {
3068    if (packageId != null) 
3069      return pcm.loadPackage(packageId, igver);
3070    
3071    JsonObject pl;
3072    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Fetch Package history from "+Utilities.pathURL(canonical, "package-list.json"));
3073    try {
3074      pl = JsonTrackingParser.fetchJson(Utilities.pathURL(canonical, "package-list.json"));
3075    } catch (Exception e) {
3076      return null;
3077    }
3078    if (!canonical.equals(pl.get("canonical").getAsString()))
3079      throw new Exception("Canonical mismatch fetching package list for "+canonical+"#"+igver+", package-list.json says "+pl.get("canonical"));
3080    for (JsonElement e : pl.getAsJsonArray("list")) {
3081      JsonObject o = (JsonObject) e;
3082      if (igver.equals(o.get("version").getAsString())) {
3083        InputStream src = fetchFromSource(pl.get("package-id").getAsString()+"-"+igver, Utilities.pathURL(o.get("path").getAsString(), "package.tgz"));
3084        return pcm.addPackageToCache(pl.get("package-id").getAsString(), igver, src, Utilities.pathURL(o.get("path").getAsString(), "package.tgz"));
3085      }
3086    }
3087    return null;
3088  }

3091  private String fetchFromURL(String source, String name) throws Exception {
3092    String filename = Utilities.path(vsCache, name+".cache");
3093    if (new File(filename).exists())
3094      return filename;
3095
3096    if (!source.endsWith("validator.pack"))
3097      source = Utilities.pathURL(source, "validator.pack");
3098    try {
3099      URL url = new URL(source+"?nocache=" + System.currentTimeMillis());
3100      URLConnection c = url.openConnection();
3101      byte[] cnt = IOUtils.toByteArray(c.getInputStream());
3102      TextFile.bytesToFile(cnt, filename);
3103      return filename;
3104    } catch (Exception e) {
3105      throw new Exception("Unable to load definitions from URL '"+source+"': "+e.getMessage(), e);
3106    }
3107  }

3119  
3120  private boolean checkDir(String dir, boolean emptyOk) throws Exception {
3121    FetchState state = fetcher.check(dir);
3122    if (state == FetchState.NOT_FOUND) {
3123      if (emptyOk)
3124        return false;
3125      throw new Exception(String.format("Error: folder %s not found", dir));
3126    } else if (state == FetchState.FILE)
3127      throw new Exception(String.format("Error: Output must be a folder (%s)", dir));
3128    return true;
3129  }
3130
3131  private void checkFile(String fn) throws Exception {
3132    FetchState state = fetcher.check(fn);
3133    if (state == FetchState.NOT_FOUND)
3134      throw new Exception(String.format("Error: file %s not found", fn));
3135    else if (state == FetchState.DIR)
3136      throw new Exception(String.format("Error: Output must be a file (%s)", fn));
3137  }

3139  private void forceDir(String dir) throws Exception {
3140    File f = new File(dir);
3141    if (!f.exists())
3142      Utilities.createDirectory(dir);
3143    else if (!f.isDirectory())
3144      throw new Exception(String.format("Error: Output must be a folder (%s)", dir));
3145  }

3147  private boolean checkMakeFile(byte[] bs, String path, Set<String> outputTracker) throws IOException {
3148    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.GENERATE, "Check Generate "+path);
3149    if (firstExecution) {
3150      String s = path.toLowerCase();
3151      if (allOutputs.contains(s))
3152        throw new Error("Error generating build: the file "+path+" is being generated more than once (may differ by case)");
3153      allOutputs.add(s);
3154    }
3155    outputTracker.add(path);
3156    File f = new CSFile(path);
3157    byte[] existing = null;
3158    if (f.exists())
3159      existing = TextFile.fileToBytes(path);
3160    if (!Arrays.equals(bs, existing)) {
3161      TextFile.bytesToFile(bs, path);
3162      return true;
3163    }
3164    return false;
3165  }

3167  private boolean needFile(String s) {
3168    if (s.endsWith(".css") && !isChild())
3169      return true;
3170    if (s.startsWith("tbl"))
3171      return true;
3172    if (s.endsWith(".js"))
3173      return true;
3174    if (s.startsWith("icon"))
3175      return true;
3176    if (Utilities.existsInList(s, "modifier.png", "mustsupport.png", "summary.png", "lock.png", "external.png", "cc0.png", "target.png", "link.svg"))
3177      return true;
3178    
3179    return false;
3180  }
3181
3182  public SpecMapManager loadSpecDetails(byte[] bs) throws IOException {
3183    SpecMapManager map = new SpecMapManager(bs, version);
3184    map.setBase(PackageHacker.fixPackageUrl(specPath));
3185    specMaps.add(map);
3186    return map;
3187  }
3188
3189
3190  private boolean load() throws Exception {
3191    validationFetcher.initOtherUrls();
3192    fileList.clear();
3193    changeList.clear();
3194    bndIds.clear();
3195    boolean needToBuild = false;
3196    FetchedFile igf = fetcher.fetch(igName);
3197    needToBuild = noteFile(IG_NAME, igf) || needToBuild;
3198    if (needToBuild) {
3199      if (sourceIg == null) // old JSON approach
3200        sourceIg = (ImplementationGuide) parse(igf);
3201      publishedIg = sourceIg.copy();
3202      FetchedResource igr = igf.addResource();
3203//      loadAsElementModel(igf, igr, null);
3204      igr.setResource(publishedIg);
3205      igr.setElement(convertToElement(publishedIg));
3206      igr.setId(sourceIg.getId()).setTitle(publishedIg.getName());
3207    } else {
3208      // special case; the source is updated during the build, so we track it differently
3209      publishedIg = sourceIg.copy();
3210      altMap.get(IG_NAME).getResources().get(0).setResource(publishedIg);
3211    }
3212    
3213    loadMappingSpaces(context.getBinaries().get("mappingSpaces.details"));
3214    validationFetcher.getMappingUrls().addAll(mappingSpaces.keySet());
3215    validationFetcher.getOtherUrls().add(publishedIg.getUrl());
3216    for (SpecMapManager s :  specMaps) {
3217      validationFetcher.getOtherUrls().add(s.getBase());
3218      if (s.getBase2() != null) {
3219        validationFetcher.getOtherUrls().add(s.getBase2());
3220      }
3221    }
3222
3223    if (npmName == null)
3224      throw new Exception("A package name (npm-name) is required to publish implementation guides. For further information, see http://wiki.hl7.org/index.php?title=FHIR_NPM_Package_Spec#Package_name");
3225    if (!publishedIg.hasLicense())
3226      publishedIg.setLicense(licenseAsEnum());
3227    if (!publishedIg.hasPackageId())
3228      publishedIg.setPackageId(npmName);
3229    if (!publishedIg.hasFhirVersion())
3230      publishedIg.addFhirVersion(FHIRVersion.fromCode(version));
3231    if (!publishedIg.hasVersion() && businessVersion != null)
3232      publishedIg.setVersion(businessVersion);
3233    
3234    String id = npmName;
3235    if (npmName.startsWith("hl7.")) {
3236      if (!id.matches("[A-Za-z0-9\\-\\.]{1,64}"))
3237        throw new FHIRException("The generated ID is '"+id+"' which is not valid");
3238      FetchedResource r = fetchByResource("ImplementationGuide", publishedIg.getId());
3239      publishedIg.setId(id);
3240      publishedIg.setUrl(igpkp.getCanonical()+"/ImplementationGuide/"+id);
3241      if (r != null) { // it better be....
3242        r.setId(id);
3243        r.getElement().getNamedChild("id").setValue(id);
3244        r.getElement().getNamedChild("url").setValue(publishedIg.getUrl());
3245      }        
3246    } else if (!id.equals(publishedIg.getId()))
3247      errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "ImplementationGuide.id", "The Implementation Guide Resource id should be "+id, IssueSeverity.WARNING));
3248      
3249    // Cql Compile
3250    cql = new CqlSubSystem(npmList, binaryPaths, new LibraryLoader(version), this, context.getUcumService(), publishedIg.getPackageId(), igpkp.getCanonical());
3251    if (binaryPaths.size() > 0) {
3252      cql.execute();
3253    }
3254    fetcher.setRootDir(rootDir);
3255    loadedIds = new HashSet<>();
3256    duplicateInputResourcesDetected = false;
3257    // load any bundles
3258    if (sourceDir != null || igpkp.isAutoPath())
3259      needToBuild = loadResources(needToBuild, igf);
3260    needToBuild = loadSpreadsheets(needToBuild, igf);
3261    needToBuild = loadMappings(needToBuild, igf);
3262    needToBuild = loadBundles(needToBuild, igf);
3263    int i = 0;
3264    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent res : publishedIg.getDefinition().getResource()) {
3265      if (!res.hasReference())
3266        throw new Exception("Missing source reference on a resource in the IG with the name '"+res.getName()+"' (index = "+i+")");
3267      i++;
3268      FetchedFile f = null;
3269      if (!bndIds.contains(res.getReference().getReference()) && !res.hasUserData("loaded.resource")) { // todo: this doesn't work for differential builds
3270        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Load "+res.getReference());
3271        f = fetcher.fetch(res.getReference(), igf);
3272        if (!f.hasTitle() && res.getName() != null)
3273          f.setTitle(res.getName());
3274        boolean rchanged = noteFile(res, f);        
3275        needToBuild = rchanged || needToBuild;
3276        if (rchanged) {
3277          if (res.hasExtension(ToolingExtensions.EXT_BINARY_FORMAT)) {
3278            loadAsBinaryResource(f, f.addResource(), res, res.getExtensionString(ToolingExtensions.EXT_BINARY_FORMAT));
3279          } else {
3280            loadAsElementModel(f, f.addResource(), res);
3281          }
3282        }
3283      }
3284      if (res.hasExampleCanonicalType()) {
3285        if (f != null && f.getResources().size()!=1)
3286          throw new Exception("Can't have an exampleFor unless the file has exactly one resource");
3287        FetchedResource r = res.hasUserData("loaded.resource") ? (FetchedResource) res.getUserData("loaded.resource") : f.getResources().get(0);
3288        if (r == null)
3289            throw new Exception("Unable to resolve example canonical " + res.getExampleCanonicalType().asStringValue());
3290        examples.add(r);
3291        String ref = res.getExampleCanonicalType().getValueAsString();
3292        if (Utilities.isAbsoluteUrl(ref)) {
3293          r.setExampleUri(ref);
3294        } else {
3295          r.setExampleUri(Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), ref));
3296        }
3297        // Redo this because we now have example information
3298        if (f!=null)
3299          igpkp.findConfiguration(f, r);
3300      }
3301    }
3302    if (duplicateInputResourcesDetected) {
3303      throw new Error("Unable to continue because duplicate input resources were identified");
3304    }
3305
3306    // load static pages
3307    needToBuild = loadPrePages() || needToBuild;
3308    needToBuild = loadPages() || needToBuild;
3309
3310    if (publishedIg.getDefinition().hasPage())
3311      loadIgPages(publishedIg.getDefinition().getPage(), igPages);
3312
3313    for (FetchedFile f: fileList) {
3314      for (FetchedResource r: f.getResources()) {
3315        resources.put(igpkp.doReplacements(igpkp.getLinkFor(r, false), r, null, null), r);
3316      }
3317    }
3318    
3319    for (JsonDependency dep : jsonDependencies) {
3320      ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent d = null;
3321      for (ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent t : publishedIg.getDependsOn()) {
3322        if (dep.getCanonical().equals(t.getUri()) || dep.getNpmId().equals(t.getPackageId())) {
3323          d = t;
3324          break;
3325        }
3326      }
3327      if (d == null) {
3328        d = publishedIg.addDependsOn();
3329        d.setUri(dep.getCanonical());
3330        d.setVersion(dep.getVersion());
3331        d.setPackageId(dep.getNpmId());
3332      } else {
3333        d.setVersion(dep.getVersion());
3334      }
3335    }
3336
3337    for (ImplementationGuideDependsOnComponent dep : publishedIg.getDependsOn()) {
3338      if (!dep.hasPackageId()) {
3339        dep.setPackageId(pcm.getPackageId(determineCanonical(dep.getUri(), null)));
3340      }
3341      if (!dep.hasPackageId()) 
3342        throw new FHIRException("Unknown package id for "+dep.getUri());
3343    }
3344    npm = new NPMPackageGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "package.tgz"), igpkp.getCanonical(), targetUrl(), PackageType.IG,  publishedIg, execTime.getTime(), !publishing);
3345    execTime = Calendar.getInstance();
3346
3347    rc = new RenderingContext(context, markdownEngine, ValidationOptions.defaults(), checkAppendSlash(specPath), "", null, ResourceRendererMode.TECHNICAL);
3348    rc.setTemplateProvider(templateProvider);
3349    rc.setResolver(this);    
3350    rc.setServices(validator.getExternalHostServices());
3351    rc.setDestDir(Utilities.path(tempDir));
3352    rc.setProfileUtilities(new ProfileUtilities(context, new ArrayList<ValidationMessage>(), igpkp));
3353    rc.setQuestionnaireMode(QuestionnaireRendererMode.TREE);
3354    rc.getCodeSystemPropList().addAll(codeSystemProps );
3355//    rc.setTargetVersion(pubVersion);
3356
3357    if (igMode) {
3358      boolean failed = false;
3359      CommaSeparatedStringBuilder b = new CommaSeparatedStringBuilder();
3360      // sanity check: every specified resource must be loaded, every loaded resource must be specified
3361      for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent r : publishedIg.getDefinition().getResource()) {
3362        b.append(r.getReference().getReference());
3363        if (!r.hasUserData("loaded.resource")) {
3364          log("Resource "+r.getReference().getReference()+" not loaded");
3365          failed = true;
3366        }
3367      }  
3368      for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
3369        for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
3370          ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent rg = findIGReference(r.fhirType(), r.getId());
3371          if (!"ImplementationGuide".equals(r.fhirType()) && rg == null) {
3372            log("Resource "+r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId()+" not defined");
3373            failed = true;
3374          }
3375          if (rg != null) {
3376            if (!rg.hasName()) {
3377              if (r.getElement().hasChild("title")) {
3378                rg.setName(r.getElement().getChildValue("title"));
3379              } else if (r.getElement().hasExtension("http://hl7.org/fhir/tools/StructureDefinition/extension-title")) {
3380                rg.setName(r.getElement().getExtensionValue("http://hl7.org/fhir/tools/StructureDefinition/extension-title").primitiveValue());                
3381              }
3382            }
3383            if (!rg.hasDescription()) {
3384              if (r.getElement().hasChild("description")) {
3385                Element descriptionElement = r.getElement().getNamedChild("description");
3386                if (descriptionElement.hasValue()) {
3387                  rg.setDescription(r.getElement().getChildValue("description").trim());
3388                }
3389                else {
3390                  if (descriptionElement.hasChild("text")) {
3391                    Element textElement = descriptionElement.getNamedChild("text");
3392                    if (textElement.hasValue()) {
3393                      rg.setDescription(textElement.getValue().trim());
3394                    }
3395                  }
3396                }
3397              }
3398            }
3399            if (!rg.hasExample()) {
3400              // If the instance declares a profile that's got the same canonical base as this IG, then the resource is an example of that profile
3401              Map<String, String> profiles = new HashMap<String, String>();
3402              if (r.getElement().hasChild("meta")) {
3403                for (Element p : r.getElement().getChildren("meta").get(0).getChildren("profile")) {
3404                  if (!profiles.containsKey(p.getValue()))
3405                    profiles.put(p.getValue(), p.getValue());
3406                }
3407              }
3408              if (r.getElement().getName().equals("Bundle")) {
3409                for (Element entry : r.getElement().getChildren("entry")) {
3410                  for (Element entres : entry.getChildren("resource")) {
3411                    if (entres.hasChild("meta")) {
3412                      for (Element p : entres.getChildren("meta").get(0).getChildren("profile")) {
3413                        if (!profiles.containsKey(p.getValue()))
3414                          profiles.put(p.getValue(), p.getValue());
3415                      }
3416                    }              
3417                  }
3418                }
3419              }
3420              for (String p : profiles.keySet()) {
3421                // Ideally we'd want to have *all* of the profiles listed as examples, but right now we can only have one, so we just overwrite and take the last.
3422                if (p.startsWith(igpkp.getCanonical()+"/StructureDefinition")) {
3423                  rg.setExample(new CanonicalType(p));
3424                  if (rg.getName()==null) {
3425                    String name = String.join(" - ", rg.getReference().getReference().split("/"));
3426                    rg.setName("Example " + name);
3427                  }
3428                  examples.add(r);
3429                  r.setExampleUri(p);
3430                  igpkp.findConfiguration(f, r);
3431                }
3432              }
3433            }            
3434          }
3435        }
3436      }
3437      if (failed) {
3438        log("Resources: "+b.toString());
3439        throw new Exception("Invalid - see reasons"); // if this ever happens, it's a programming issue....
3440      }
3441    }
3442    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "Loaded Files: "+fileList.size());
3443    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
3444      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "  "+f.getTitle()+" - "+f.getResources().size()+" Resources");
3445      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources())
3446        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "    "+r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());      
3447    }
3448    extensionTracker.scan(publishedIg);
3449    return needToBuild;
3450  }
3451
3452  private FetchedResource fetchByResource(String type, String id) {
3453    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
3454      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
3455        if (r.fhirType().equals(type) && r.getId().equals(id))
3456          return r;
3457      }
3458    }
3459    return null;
3460  }

3462
3463  private String targetUrl() {
3464    if (mode == null)
3465      return "file://"+outputDir;
3466    switch (mode) {
3467    case AUTOBUILD: return targetOutput == null ? "https://build.fhir.org/ig/[org]/[repo]" : targetOutput;
3468    case MANUAL: return "file://"+outputDir;
3469    case WEBSERVER: return "http://unknown";
3470    case PUBLICATION: return targetOutput;
3471    default: return igpkp.getCanonical();
3472    }
3473  }

3476  private void copyFiles(String base, String folder, String dest, List<String> files) throws IOException {
3477    for (File f : new File(folder).listFiles()) {
3478      if (f.isDirectory()) {
3479        copyFiles(base, f.getAbsolutePath(),  Utilities.path(dest, f.getName()), files);
3480      } else {
3481        String dst = Utilities.path(dest, f.getName());
3482        FileUtils.copyFile(f, new File(dst), true);
3483        files.add(f.getAbsolutePath().substring(base.length()+1));
3484      }
3485    } 
3486  }

3489  private void templateBeforeGenerate() throws IOException, FHIRException {
3490    if (template != null) {
3491      if (debug) {
3492        waitForInput("before OnGenerate");
3493      }
3494      Session tts = tt.start("template");
3495      List<String> newFileList = new ArrayList<String>();
3496      checkOutcomes(template.beforeGenerateEvent(publishedIg, tempDir, otherFilesRun, newFileList));
3497      for (String newFile: newFileList) {
3498        if (!newFile.isEmpty()) {
3499          try {
3500            FetchedFile f = fetcher.fetch(Utilities.path(repoRoot, newFile));
3501            String dir = Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(f.getPath());
3502            String relative = tempDir.length() > dir.length() ? "" : dir.substring(tempDir.length());
3503            if (relative.length() > 0)
3504              relative = relative.substring(1);
3505            f.setRelativePath(f.getPath().substring(dir.length()+1));
3506            PreProcessInfo ppinfo = new PreProcessInfo(null, relative);
3507            loadPrePage(f, ppinfo);
3508          } catch (Exception e) {
3509            throw new FHIRException(e.getMessage());
3510          }
3511        }
3512      }
3513      igPages.clear();
3514      if (publishedIg.getDefinition().hasPage()) {
3515        loadIgPages(publishedIg.getDefinition().getPage(), igPages);
3516      }
3517      tts.end();
3518      if (debug) {
3519        waitForInput("after OnGenerate");
3520      }
3521    }
3522    cleanUpExtensions(publishedIg);
3523  }
3524
3525  private void cleanUpExtensions(ImplementationGuide ig) {
3526   ToolingExtensions.removeExtension(ig, IGHelper.EXT_SPREADSHEET);
3527   ToolingExtensions.removeExtension(ig, IGHelper.EXT_BUNDLE);
3528   for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent r : ig.getDefinition().getResource())
3529     ToolingExtensions.removeExtension(r, IGHelper.EXT_RESOURCE_INFO);
3530  }

3533  private void checkOutcomes(Map<String, List<ValidationMessage>> outcomes) {
3534    if (outcomes == null)
3535      return;
3536    
3537    for (String s : outcomes.keySet()) {
3538      FetchedFile f = getFileForFile(s);
3539      if (f == null)
3540        errors.addAll(outcomes.get(s));
3541      else
3542        f.getErrors().addAll(outcomes.get(s));        
3543    }    
3544  }

3549      if (debug)
3550        waitForInput("before OnJekyll");
3551      Session tts = tt.start("template");
3552      List<String> newFileList = new ArrayList<String>();
3553      checkOutcomes(template.beforeJekyllEvent(publishedIg, newFileList));
3554      tts.end();
3555      if (debug)
3556        waitForInput("after OnJekyll");
3557    }
3558  }

3562      if (debug)
3563        waitForInput("before OnJekyll");
3564      Session tts = tt.start("template");
3565      checkOutcomes(template.onCheckEvent(publishedIg));
3566      tts.end();
3567      if (debug)
3568        waitForInput("after OnJekyll");
3569    }

3572  private void waitForInput(String string) throws IOException {
3573    System.out.print("At point '"+string+"' - press enter to continue: ");
3574    while (System.in.read() != 10) {};
3575  }

3578  private void loadIgPages(ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent page, HashMap<String, ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent> map) throws FHIRException {
3579    if (page.hasName() && page.hasNameUrlType())
3580      map.put(page.getNameUrlType().getValue(), page);
3581    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent childPage: page.getPage()) {
3582      loadIgPages(childPage, map);
3583    }
3584  }
3585
3586  private boolean loadPrePages() throws Exception {
3587    boolean changed = false;
3588    if (prePagesDirs.isEmpty())
3589      return false;
3590
3591    for (String prePagesDir : prePagesDirs) {
3592      FetchedFile dir = fetcher.fetch(prePagesDir);
3593      if (dir != null) {
3594        dir.setRelativePath("");
3595        if (!dir.isFolder())
3596          throw new Exception("pre-processed page reference is not a folder");
3597        if (loadPrePages(dir, dir.getStatedPath()))
3598          changed = true;
3599      }
3600    }
3601    return changed;
3602  }
3603
3604  private boolean loadPrePages(FetchedFile dir, String basePath) throws Exception {
3605    System.out.println("loadPrePages from " + dir+ " as "+basePath);
3606    boolean changed = false;
3607    PreProcessInfo ppinfo = preProcessInfo.get(basePath);
3608    if (ppinfo==null) {
3609      System.out.println("PreProcessInfo hash:" + preProcessInfo.toString());
3610      throw new Exception("Unable to find preProcessInfo for basePath: " + basePath);
3611    }
3612    if (!altMap.containsKey("pre-page/"+dir.getPath())) {
3613      changed = true;
3614      altMap.put("pre-page/"+dir.getPath(), dir);
3615      dir.setProcessMode(ppinfo.hasXslt() ? FetchedFile.PROCESS_XSLT : FetchedFile.PROCESS_NONE);
3616      dir.setXslt(ppinfo.getXslt());
3617      if (ppinfo.hasRelativePath()) {
3618        if (dir.getRelativePath().isEmpty())
3619          dir.setRelativePath(ppinfo.getRelativePath());
3620        else
3621          dir.setRelativePath(ppinfo.getRelativePath() + File.separator + dir.getRelativePath());
3622
3623      }
3624      addFile(dir);
3625    }
3626    for (String link : dir.getFiles()) {
3627      FetchedFile f = fetcher.fetch(link);
3628      System.out.println("find pre-page "+f.getPath()+" at "+link+" from "+basePath);
3629      f.setRelativePath(f.getPath().substring(basePath.length()+1));
3630      if (f.isFolder())
3631        changed = loadPrePages(f, basePath) || changed;
3632      else
3633        changed = loadPrePage(f, ppinfo) || changed;
3634    }
3635    return changed;
3636  }
3637
3638  private boolean loadPrePage(FetchedFile file, PreProcessInfo ppinfo) {
3639    FetchedFile existing = altMap.get("pre-page/"+file.getPath());
3640    if (existing == null || existing.getTime() != file.getTime() || existing.getHash() != file.getHash()) {
3641      file.setProcessMode(ppinfo.hasXslt() && !file.getPath().endsWith(".md") ? FetchedFile.PROCESS_XSLT : FetchedFile.PROCESS_NONE);
3642      file.setXslt(ppinfo.getXslt());
3643      if (ppinfo.hasRelativePath())
3644        file.setRelativePath(ppinfo.getRelativePath() + File.separator + file.getRelativePath());
3645      addFile(file);
3646      altMap.put("pre-page/"+file.getPath(), file);
3647      return true;
3648    } else {
3649      return false;
3650    }
3651  }
3652
3653  private boolean loadPages() throws Exception {
3654    boolean changed = false;
3655    for (String pagesDir: pagesDirs) {
3656      FetchedFile dir = fetcher.fetch(pagesDir);
3657      dir.setRelativePath("");
3658      if (!dir.isFolder())
3659        throw new Exception("page reference is not a folder");
3660      if (loadPages(dir, dir.getPath()))
3661        changed = true;
3662    }
3663    return changed;
3664  }
3665
3666  private boolean loadPages(FetchedFile dir, String basePath) throws Exception {
3667    boolean changed = false;
3668    if (!altMap.containsKey("page/"+dir.getPath())) {
3669      changed = true;
3670      altMap.put("page/"+dir.getPath(), dir);
3671      dir.setProcessMode(FetchedFile.PROCESS_NONE);
3672      addFile(dir);
3673    }
3674    for (String link : dir.getFiles()) {
3675      FetchedFile f = fetcher.fetch(link);
3676      f.setRelativePath(f.getPath().substring(basePath.length()+1));
3677      if (f.isFolder())
3678        changed = loadPages(f, basePath) || changed;
3679      else
3680        changed = loadPage(f) || changed;
3681    }
3682    return changed;
3683  }
3684
3685  private boolean loadPage(FetchedFile file) {
3686    FetchedFile existing = altMap.get("page/"+file.getPath());
3687    if (existing == null || existing.getTime() != file.getTime() || existing.getHash() != file.getHash()) {
3688      file.setProcessMode(FetchedFile.PROCESS_NONE);
3689      addFile(file);
3690      altMap.put("page/"+file.getPath(), file);
3691      return true;
3692    } else {
3693      return false;
3694    }
3695  }
3696
3697  private boolean loadBundles(boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile igf) throws Exception {
3698    for (String be : bundles) {
3699      needToBuild = loadBundle(be, needToBuild, igf);
3700    }
3701    return needToBuild;
3702  }
3703
3704  private boolean loadBundle(String name, boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile igf) throws Exception {
3705    FetchedFile f = fetcher.fetch(new Reference().setReference("Bundle/"+name), igf);
3706    boolean changed = noteFile("Bundle/"+name, f);
3707    if (changed) {
3708      f.setBundle(new FetchedResource());
3709      f.setBundleType(FetchedBundleType.NATIVE);
3710      loadAsElementModel(f, f.getBundle(), null);
3711      List<Element> entries = new ArrayList<Element>();
3712      f.getBundle().getElement().getNamedChildren("entry", entries);
3713      int i = -1;
3714      for (Element bnde : entries) {
3715        i++;
3716        Element res = bnde.getNamedChild("resource"); 
3717        if (res == null) {
3718          f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "Bundle.element["+i+"]", "All entries must have resources when loading a bundle", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
3719        } else {
3720          checkResourceUnique(res.fhirType()+"/"+res.getIdBase());
3721          FetchedResource r = f.addResource();
3722          r.setElement(res);
3723          r.setId(res.getIdBase());
3724          List<Element> profiles = new ArrayList<Element>();
3725          Element meta = res.getNamedChild("meta");
3726          if (meta != null)
3727            meta.getNamedChildren("profile", profiles);
3728          for (Element p : profiles)
3729            r.getStatedProfiles().add(p.primitiveValue());
3730          r.setTitle(r.getElement().getChildValue("name"));
3731          igpkp.findConfiguration(f, r);
3732        }
3733      }
3734    } else
3735      f = altMap.get("Bundle/"+name);
3736    ImplementationGuideDefinitionGroupingComponent pck = null;
3737    for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
3738      bndIds.add(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());
3739      ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent res = findIGReference(r.fhirType(), r.getId());
3740      if (res == null) {
3741        if (pck == null) {
3742          pck = publishedIg.getDefinition().addGrouping().setName(f.getTitle());
3743          pck.setId(name);
3744        }
3745        res = publishedIg.getDefinition().addResource();
3746        res.setGroupingId(pck.getId());
3747        if (!res.hasName())
3748          if (r.hasTitle())
3749            res.setName(r.getTitle());
3750          else
3751            res.setName(r.getId());
3752        if (!res.hasDescription() && r.getElement().hasChild("description")) {
3753          res.setDescription(r.getElement().getChildValue("description").trim());
3754        }
3755        res.setReference(new Reference().setReference(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId()));
3756      }
3757      res.setUserData("loaded.resource", r);
3758      r.setResEntry(res);
3759    }
3760    return changed || needToBuild;
3761  }
3762
3763  private boolean loadResources(boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile igf) throws Exception { // igf is not currently used, but it was about relative references? 
3764    List<FetchedFile> resources = fetcher.scan(sourceDir, context, igpkp.isAutoPath());
3765    for (FetchedFile ff : resources) {
3766      if (!ff.matches(igf))
3767        needToBuild = loadResource(needToBuild, ff);
3768    }
3769    return needToBuild;
3770  }
3771
3772  private boolean loadResource(boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile f) throws Exception {
3773    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "load "+f.getPath());
3774    boolean changed = noteFile(f.getPath(), f);
3775    if (changed) {
3776      loadAsElementModel(f, f.addResource(), null);
3777    }
3778    for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
3779      ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent res = findIGReference(r.fhirType(), r.getId());
3780      if (res == null) {
3781        res = publishedIg.getDefinition().addResource();
3782        if (!res.hasName())
3783          res.setName(r.getTitle());
3784        if (!res.hasDescription())
3785          res.setDescription(((CanonicalResource)r.getResource()).getDescription().trim());
3786        res.setReference(new Reference().setReference(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId()));
3787      }
3788      res.setUserData("loaded.resource", r);
3789      r.setResEntry(res);
3790    }
3791    return changed || needToBuild;
3792  }

3795  private boolean loadMappings(boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile igf) throws Exception {
3796    for (String s : mappings) {
3797      needToBuild = loadMapping(s, needToBuild, igf);
3798    }
3799    return needToBuild;

3802  private boolean loadMapping(String name, boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile igf) throws Exception {
3803    if (name.startsWith("!"))
3804      return false;
3805    FetchedFile f = fetcher.fetchResourceFile(name);
3806    boolean changed = noteFile("Mapping/"+name, f);
3807    if (changed) {
3808      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "load "+f.getPath());
3809      MappingSheetParser p = new MappingSheetParser();
3810      p.parse(new ByteArrayInputStream(f.getSource()), f.getRelativePath());
3811      ConceptMap cm = p.getConceptMap();
3812      FetchedResource r = f.addResource();
3813      r.setResource(cm);
3814      r.setId(cm.getId());
3815      r.setElement(convertToElement(cm));
3816      r.setTitle(r.getElement().getChildValue("name"));
3817      igpkp.findConfiguration(f, r);
3818    } else {
3819      f = altMap.get("Mapping/"+name);
3820    }
3821    return changed || needToBuild;
3822  }

3824  private boolean loadSpreadsheets(boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile igf) throws Exception {
3825    Set<String> knownValueSetIds = new HashSet<>();
3826    for (String s : spreadsheets) {
3827      needToBuild = loadSpreadsheet(s, needToBuild, igf, knownValueSetIds);
3828    }
3829    return needToBuild;
3830  }
3831
3832  private boolean loadSpreadsheet(String name, boolean needToBuild, FetchedFile igf, Set<String> knownValueSetIds) throws Exception {
3833    if (name.startsWith("!"))
3834      return false;
3835
3836    FetchedFile f = fetcher.fetchResourceFile(name);
3837    boolean changed = noteFile("Spreadsheet/"+name, f);
3838    if (changed) {
3839      f.getValuesetsToLoad().clear();
3840      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.INIT, "load "+f.getPath());
3841      Bundle bnd = new IgSpreadsheetParser(context, execTime, igpkp.getCanonical(), f.getValuesetsToLoad(), firstExecution, mappingSpaces, knownValueSetIds).parse(f);
3842      f.setBundle(new FetchedResource());
3843      f.setBundleType(FetchedBundleType.SPREADSHEET);
3844      f.getBundle().setResource(bnd);
3845      for (BundleEntryComponent b : bnd.getEntry()) {
3846        checkResourceUnique(b.getResource().fhirType()+"/"+b.getResource().getIdBase());
3847        FetchedResource r = f.addResource();
3848        r.setResource(b.getResource());
3849        r.setId(b.getResource().getId());
3850        r.setElement(convertToElement(r.getResource()));
3851        r.setTitle(r.getElement().getChildValue("name"));
3852        igpkp.findConfiguration(f, r);
3853      }
3854    } else {
3855      f = altMap.get("Spreadsheet/"+name);
3856    }
3857
3858    for (String id : f.getValuesetsToLoad().keySet()) {
3859      if (!knownValueSetIds.contains(id)) {
3860        String vr = f.getValuesetsToLoad().get(id);
3861        checkResourceUnique("ValueSet/"+id);
3862
3863        FetchedFile fv = fetcher.fetchFlexible(vr);
3864        boolean vrchanged = noteFile("sp-ValueSet/"+vr, fv);
3865        if (vrchanged) {
3866          loadAsElementModel(fv, fv.addResource(), null);
3867          checkImplicitResourceIdentity(id, fv);
3868        }
3869        knownValueSetIds.add(id);
3870        // ok, now look for an implicit code system with the same name
3871        boolean crchanged = false;
3872        String cr = vr.replace("valueset-", "codesystem-");
3873        if (!cr.equals(vr)) {
3874          if (fetcher.canFetchFlexible(cr)) {
3875            fv = fetcher.fetchFlexible(cr);
3876            crchanged = noteFile("sp-CodeSystem/"+vr, fv);
3877            if (crchanged) {
3878              loadAsElementModel(fv, fv.addResource(), null);
3879              checkImplicitResourceIdentity(id, fv);
3880            }
3881          }
3882        }
3883        changed = changed || vrchanged || crchanged;
3884      }
3885    }
3886    ImplementationGuideDefinitionGroupingComponent pck = null;
3887    for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
3888      bndIds.add(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());
3889      ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent res = findIGReference(r.fhirType(), r.getId()); 
3890      if (res == null) {
3891        if (pck == null) {
3892          pck = publishedIg.getDefinition().addGrouping().setName(f.getTitle());
3893          pck.setId(name);
3894        }
3895        res = publishedIg.getDefinition().addResource();
3896        res.setGroupingId(pck.getId());
3897        if (!res.hasName())
3898          res.setName(r.getTitle());
3899        if (!res.hasDescription())
3900          res.setDescription(((CanonicalResource)r.getResource()).getDescription().trim());
3901        res.setReference(new Reference().setReference(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId()));
3902      }
3903      res.setUserData("loaded.resource", r);
3904      r.setResEntry(res);
3905    }
3906    return changed || needToBuild;
3907  }
3908
3909
3910  private void checkImplicitResourceIdentity(String id, FetchedFile fv) throws Exception {
3911    // check the resource ids:
3912    String rid = fv.getResources().get(0).getId();
3913    String rurl = fv.getResources().get(0).getElement().getChildValue("url");
3914    if (Utilities.noString(rurl))
3915      throw new Exception("ValueSet has no canonical URL "+fv.getName());
3916    if (!id.equals(rid))
3917      throw new Exception("ValueSet has wrong id ("+rid+", expecting "+id+") in "+fv.getName());
3918    if (!tail(rurl).equals(rid))
3919      throw new Exception("resource id/url mismatch: "+id+" vs "+rurl+" for "+fv.getResources().get(0).getTitle()+" in "+fv.getName());
3920    if (!rurl.startsWith(igpkp.getCanonical()))
3921      throw new Exception("base/ resource url mismatch: "+igpkp.getCanonical()+" vs "+rurl);
3922  }
3923
3924
3925  private String tail(String url) {
3926    return url.substring(url.lastIndexOf("/")+1);
3927  }

3971  private void loadConformance() throws Exception {
3972    for (String s : metadataResourceNames()) 
3973      scan(s);
3974    loadInfo();
3975    for (String s : metadataResourceNames()) 
3976      load(s);
3977    log("Generating Snapshots");
3978    generateSnapshots();
3979    log("Generating Narratives");
3980    generateNarratives();
3981    if (!noValidation) {
3982      log("Validating Conformance Resources");
3983      for (String s : metadataResourceNames()) {
3984        validate(s);
3985      }
3986    }
3987    
3988    loadLists();
3989    checkConformanceResources();
3990    generateLogicalMaps();
3991//    load("StructureMap"); // todo: this is a problem...
3992    generateAdditionalExamples();
3993    executeTransforms();
3994    validateExpressions();
3995    errors.addAll(cql.getGeneralErrors());
3996    scanForUsageStats();
3997  }

3999  private void validate(String type) throws Exception {
4000    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4001      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4002        if (r.fhirType().equals(type)) {
4003          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "validate res: "+r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());
4004          if (!r.isValidated()) {
4005            validate(f, r);
4006          }
4007        }
4008      }
4009    }
4010  }

4012  private void loadInfo() {
4013    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4014      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4015        if (r.getResEntry() != null) {
4016          ToolingExtensions.setStringExtension(r.getResEntry(), IGHelper.EXT_RESOURCE_INFO, r.fhirType());
4017        }
4018      }
4019    }
4020  }

4022  private void scanForUsageStats() {
4023    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "scanForUsageStats");
4024    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4025      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4026        if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition")) 
4027          extensionTracker.scan((StructureDefinition) r.getResource());
4028        extensionTracker.scan(r.getElement(), f.getName());
4029      }
4030    }
4031  }

4033
4034  private void checkConformanceResources() throws IOException {
4035    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "check profiles & code systems");
4036    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4037      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4038        if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition")) {
4039          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "process profile: "+r.getId());
4040          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
4041          f.getErrors().addAll(pvalidator.validate(sd, false));
4042          checkJurisdiction(f, (CanonicalResource) r.getResource(), IssueSeverity.ERROR, "must");
4043        } else if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
4044          checkJurisdiction(f, (CanonicalResource) r.getResource(), IssueSeverity.WARNING, "should");
4045        }
4046        if (r.fhirType().equals("CodeSystem")) {
4047          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "process CodeSystem: "+r.getId());
4048          CodeSystem cs = (CodeSystem) r.getResource();
4049          f.getErrors().addAll(csvalidator.validate(cs, false));
4050        }
4051      }
4052    }
4053    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "check profiles & code systems");
4054    Session tts = tt.start("realm-rules");
4055    realmRules.startChecks(publishedIg);
4056    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4057      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4058        if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition")) {
4059          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
4060          realmRules.checkSD(f, sd);
4061        } else if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
4062          realmRules.checkCR(f, (CanonicalResource) r.getResource());
4063        }
4064        if (r.fhirType().equals("CodeSystem")) {
4065          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "process CodeSystem: "+r.getId());
4066          CodeSystem cs = (CodeSystem) r.getResource();
4067          f.getErrors().addAll(csvalidator.validate(cs, false));
4068        }
4069      }
4070    }
4071    realmRules.finishChecks();
4072    tts.end();
4073    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "check profiles & code systems");
4074    tts = tt.start("previous-version");
4075    previousVersionComparator.startChecks(publishedIg);
4076    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4077      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4078        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
4079          previousVersionComparator.check((CanonicalResource) r.getResource());
4080        }
4081      }
4082    }
4083    previousVersionComparator.finishChecks();
4084    tts.end();
4085  }

4087  private RealmBusinessRules makeRealmBusinessRules() {
4088    if (expectedJurisdiction != null && expectedJurisdiction.getCode().equals("US")) {
4089      return new USRealmBusinessRules(context, version, tempDir, igpkp.getCanonical(), igpkp);
4090    } else {
4091      return new NullRealmBusinessRules(igrealm);
4092    }
4093  }

4095  private PreviousVersionComparator makePreviousVersionComparator() throws IOException {
4096    if (isTemplate()) {
4097      return null;
4098    }
4099    if (comparisonVersions == null) {
4100      comparisonVersions = new ArrayList<>();
4101      comparisonVersions.add("{last}");
4102    }
4103    return new PreviousVersionComparator(context, version, rootDir, tempDir, igpkp.getCanonical(), igpkp, logger, comparisonVersions);
4104  }
4105
4106  private void checkJurisdiction(FetchedFile f, CanonicalResource resource, IssueSeverity error, String verb) {
4107    if (expectedJurisdiction != null) {
4108      boolean ok = false;
4109      for (CodeableConcept cc : resource.getJurisdiction()) {
4110        ok = ok || cc.hasCoding(expectedJurisdiction);
4111      }
4112      if (!ok) {
4113        f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, resource.fhirType()+".jurisdiction", "The resource "+verb+" declare its jurisdiction to match the package id ("+npmName+", jurisdiction = "+expectedJurisdiction.toString()+") (for FSH: 'jurisdiction: "+toFSH(expectedJurisdiction)+"')",
4114            error).setMessageId(I18nConstants.RESOURCE_JURISDICTION_MISMATCH));
4115      }
4116    }
4117  }
4118
4119  private String toFSH(Coding c) {
4120    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
4121    b.append(c.getSystem());
4122    b.append("#");
4123    b.append(c.getCode());
4124    b.append(" \"");
4125    b.append(c.getDisplay());
4126    b.append("\"");
4127    return b.toString();
4128  }
4129
4130  private void executeTransforms() throws FHIRException, Exception {
4131    if (doTransforms) {
4132      MappingServices services = new MappingServices(context, igpkp.getCanonical());
4133      StructureMapUtilities utils = new StructureMapUtilities(context, services, igpkp);
4134
4135      // ok, our first task is to generate the profiles
4136      for (FetchedFile f : changeList) {
4137        List<StructureMap> worklist = new ArrayList<StructureMap>();
4138        for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4139          if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition) {
4140            List<StructureMap> transforms = context.findTransformsforSource(((StructureDefinition) r.getResource()).getUrl());
4141            worklist.addAll(transforms);
4142          }
4143        }
4144
4145        for (StructureMap map : worklist) {
4146          StructureMapAnalysis analysis = utils.analyse(null, map);
4147          map.setUserData("analysis", analysis);
4148          for (StructureDefinition sd : analysis.getProfiles()) {
4149            FetchedResource nr = new FetchedResource();
4150            nr.setElement(convertToElement(sd));
4151            nr.setId(sd.getId());
4152            nr.setResource(sd);
4153            nr.setTitle("Generated Profile (by Transform)");
4154            f.getResources().add(nr);
4155            igpkp.findConfiguration(f, nr);
4156            sd.setUserData("path", igpkp.getLinkFor(nr, true));
4157            generateSnapshot(f, nr, sd, true);
4158          }
4159        }
4160      }
4161
4162      for (FetchedFile f : changeList) {
4163        Map<FetchedResource, List<StructureMap>> worklist = new HashMap<FetchedResource, List<StructureMap>>();
4164        for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4165          List<StructureMap> transforms = context.findTransformsforSource(r.getElement().getProperty().getStructure().getUrl());
4166          if (transforms.size() > 0) {
4167            worklist.put(r, transforms);
4168          }
4169        }
4170        for (Entry<FetchedResource, List<StructureMap>> t : worklist.entrySet()) {
4171          int i = 0;
4172          for (StructureMap map : t.getValue()) {
4173            boolean ok = true;
4174            String tgturl = null;
4175            for (StructureMapStructureComponent st : map.getStructure()) {
4176              if (st.getMode() == StructureMapModelMode.TARGET) {
4177                if (tgturl == null)
4178                  tgturl = st.getUrl();
4179                else
4180                  ok = false;
4181              }
4182            }
4183            if (ok) {
4184              Resource target = new Bundle().setType(BundleType.COLLECTION);
4185              if (tgturl != null) {
4186                StructureDefinition tsd = context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, tgturl);
4187                if (tsd == null)
4188                  throw new Exception("Unable to find definition "+tgturl);
4189                target = ResourceFactory.createResource(tsd.getType());
4190              }
4191              if (t.getValue().size() > 1)
4192                target.setId(t.getKey().getId()+"-map-"+Integer.toString(i));
4193              else
4194                target.setId(t.getKey().getId()+"-map");
4195              i++;
4196              services.reset();
4197              utils.transform(target, t.getKey().getElement(), map, target);
4198              FetchedResource nr = new FetchedResource();
4199              nr.setElement(convertToElement(target));
4200              nr.setId(target.getId());
4201              nr.setResource(target);
4202              nr.setTitle("Generated Example (by Transform)");
4203              nr.setValidateAsResource(true);
4204              f.getResources().add(nr);
4205              igpkp.findConfiguration(f, nr);
4206            }
4207          }
4208        }
4209      }
4210    }
4211  }

4213  private boolean noteFile(ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent key, FetchedFile file) {
4214    FetchedFile existing = fileMap.get(key);
4215    if (existing == null || existing.getTime() != file.getTime() || existing.getHash() != file.getHash()) {
4216      fileList.add(file);
4217      fileMap.put(key, file);
4218      addFile(file);
4219      return true;
4220    } else {
4221      fileList.add(existing); // this one is already parsed
4222      return false;
4223    }
4224  }
4225
4226  private boolean noteFile(String key, FetchedFile file) {
4227    FetchedFile existing = altMap.get(key);
4228    if (existing == null || existing.getTime() != file.getTime() || existing.getHash() != file.getHash()) {
4229      fileList.add(file);
4230      altMap.put(key, file);
4231      addFile(file);
4232      return true;
4233    } else {
4234      fileList.add(existing); // this one is already parsed
4235      return false;
4236    }
4237  }

4250  private void loadAsBinaryResource(FetchedFile file, FetchedResource r, ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent srcForLoad, String format) throws Exception {
4251    file.getErrors().clear();
4252    Binary bin = new Binary();
4253    String id = srcForLoad.getReference().getReference();
4254    if (id.startsWith("Binary/")) {
4255      bin.setId(id.substring(7));
4256    } else {
4257      throw new Exception("Unable to determine Resource id from reference: "+id);
4258    }
4259    bin.setContent(file.getSource());
4260    bin.setContentType(format);
4261    Element e = new ObjectConverter(context).convert(bin);
4262    checkResourceUnique(e.fhirType()+"/"+e.getIdBase());        
4263    r.setElement(e).setId(bin.getId());
4264    r.setResource(bin);
4265    r.setResEntry(srcForLoad);
4266    srcForLoad.setUserData("loaded.resource", r);
4267    r.setResEntry(srcForLoad);
4268    if (srcForLoad.hasExampleCanonicalType()) {
4269      r.getElement().setUserData("logical", srcForLoad.getExampleCanonicalType().getValue());
4270      r.setExampleUri(srcForLoad.getExampleCanonicalType().getValue());
4271    }
4272    igpkp.findConfiguration(file, r);
4273    srcForLoad.setUserData("loaded.resource", r);
4274  }
4275  
4276  private void loadAsElementModel(FetchedFile file, FetchedResource r, ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent srcForLoad) throws Exception {
4277    file.getErrors().clear();
4278    Element e = null;
4279
4280    try {        
4281      if (file.getContentType().contains("json")) {
4282        e = loadFromJson(file);
4283      } else if (file.getContentType().contains("xml")) {
4284        e = loadFromXml(file);
4285      } else
4286        throw new Exception("Unable to determine file type for "+file.getName());
4287    } catch (Exception ex) {
4288      throw new Exception("Unable to parse "+file.getName()+": " +ex.getMessage(), ex);
4289    }
4290    if (e == null)
4291      throw new Exception("Unable to parse "+file.getName()+": " +file.getErrors().get(0).summary());
4292    
4293    if (e != null) {
4294      try {
4295        if (!Utilities.noString(e.getIdBase())) {
4296          checkResourceUnique(e.fhirType()+"/"+e.getIdBase());
4297        }
4298        boolean altered = false;
4299
4300        String id = e.getChildValue("id");
4301        if (Utilities.noString(id)) {
4302          if (e.hasChild("url")) {
4303            String url = e.getChildValue("url");
4304            String prefix = Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), e.fhirType())+"/";
4305            if (url.startsWith(prefix)) {
4306              id = e.getChildValue("url").substring(prefix.length());
4307              e.setChildValue("id", id);
4308              altered = true;
4309            } 
4310            if (Utilities.noString(id)) {
4311              throw new Exception("Resource has no id in "+file.getPath()+" and canonical URL ("+url+") does not start with the IG canonical URL ("+prefix+")");
4312            }
4313          }
4314        }
4315        r.setElement(e).setId(id);
4316        igpkp.findConfiguration(file, r);
4317        if (srcForLoad == null)
4318          srcForLoad = findIGReference(r.fhirType(), r.getId());
4319        if (srcForLoad == null && !"ImplementationGuide".equals(r.fhirType())) {
4320          srcForLoad = publishedIg.getDefinition().addResource();
4321          srcForLoad.getReference().setReference(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());
4322        }
4323
4324        String ver = ToolingExtensions.readStringExtension(srcForLoad, ToolingExtensions.EXT_IGP_LOADVERSION); 
4325        if (ver == null)
4326          ver = r.getConfig() == null ? null : ostr(r.getConfig(), "version");
4327        if (ver == null)
4328          ver = version; // fall back to global version
4329
4330        // version check: for some conformance resources, they may be saved in a different vrsion from that stated for the IG. 
4331        // so we might need to convert them prior to loading. Note that this is different to the conversion below - we need to 
4332        // convert to the current version. Here, we need to convert to the stated version. Note that we need to do this after
4333        // the first load above because above, we didn't have enough data to get the configuration, but we do now. 
4334        if (!ver.equals(version)) {
4335          if (file.getContentType().contains("json"))
4336            e = loadFromJsonWithVersionChange(file, ver, version);
4337          else if (file.getContentType().contains("xml"))
4338            e = loadFromXmlWithVersionChange(file, ver, version);
4339          else
4340            throw new Exception("Unable to determine file type for "+file.getName());
4341          r.setElement(e);
4342        }
4343        if (srcForLoad != null) {
4344          srcForLoad.setUserData("loaded.resource", r);
4345          r.setResEntry(srcForLoad);
4346          if (srcForLoad.hasExampleCanonicalType()) {
4347            r.getElement().setUserData("profile", srcForLoad.getExampleCanonicalType().getValue());
4348            r.getStatedProfiles().add(srcForLoad.getExampleCanonicalType().getValue());
4349          }
4350        }
4351        
4352        r.setTitle(e.getChildValue("name"));
4353        Element m = e.getNamedChild("meta");
4354        if (m != null) {
4355          List<Element> profiles = m.getChildrenByName("profile");
4356          for (Element p : profiles)
4357            r.getStatedProfiles().add(p.getValue());
4358        }
4359        if ("1.0.1".equals(ver)) {
4360          file.getErrors().clear();
4361          org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.model.Resource res2 = null;
4362          if (file.getContentType().contains("json"))
4363            res2 = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser().parse(file.getSource());
4364          else if (file.getContentType().contains("xml"))
4365            res2 = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.XmlParser().parse(file.getSource());
4366          org.hl7.fhir.r5.model.Resource res = VersionConvertorFactory_10_50.convertResource(res2);
4367          e = convertToElement(res);
4368          r.setElement(e).setId(id).setTitle(e.getChildValue("name"));
4369          r.setResource(res);
4370        }
4371        if (new AdjunctFileLoader(binaryPaths, cql).replaceAttachments1(file, r, metadataResourceNames())) {
4372          altered = true;
4373        }
4374        if ((altered && r.getResource() != null) || (ver.equals(Constants.VERSION) && r.getResource() == null))
4375          r.setResource(new ObjectConverter(context).convert(r.getElement()));
4376        if ((altered && r.getResource() == null)) {
4377          if (file.getContentType().contains("json")) {
4378            saveToJson(file, e);
4379          } else if (file.getContentType().contains("xml")) {
4380            saveToXml(file, e);
4381          }
4382        }
4383      } catch ( Exception ex ) {
4384        throw new Exception("Unable to determine type for  "+file.getName()+": " +ex.getMessage(), ex);
4385      }
4386    }
4387  }
4388
4389  public void checkResourceUnique(String tid) throws Error {
4390    if (loadedIds.contains(tid)) {
4391      System.out.println("Duplicate Resource in IG: "+tid);
4392      duplicateInputResourcesDetected = true;
4393    }
4394    loadedIds.add(tid);
4395  }
