4397  private ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent findIGReference(String type, String id) {
4398    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent r : publishedIg.getDefinition().getResource()) {
4399      if (r.hasReference() && r.getReference().getReference().equals(type+"/"+id)) {
4400        return r;
4401      }
4402    }
4403    return null;
4404  }
4405
4406  private Element loadFromXml(FetchedFile file) throws Exception {
4407    org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser xp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser(context);
4408    xp.setAllowXsiLocation(true);
4409    xp.setupValidation(ValidationPolicy.EVERYTHING, file.getErrors());
4410    Element res = xp.parseSingle(new ByteArrayInputStream(file.getSource()));
4411    if (res == null) {
4412      throw new Exception("Unable to parse XML for "+file.getName());
4413    }
4414    return res;
4415  }
4416
4417  private Element loadFromJson(FetchedFile file) throws Exception {
4418    org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context);
4419    jp.setupValidation(ValidationPolicy.EVERYTHING, file.getErrors());
4420    jp.setAllowComments(true);
4421    return jp.parseSingle(new ByteArrayInputStream(file.getSource()));
4422  }
4423
4424  private void saveToXml(FetchedFile file, Element e) throws Exception {
4425    org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser xp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser(context);
4426    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
4427    xp.compose(e, bs, OutputStyle.PRETTY, null);
4428    file.setSource(bs.toByteArray());
4429  }
4430
4431  private void saveToJson(FetchedFile file, Element e) throws Exception {
4432    org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context);
4433    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
4434    jp.compose(e, bs, OutputStyle.PRETTY, null);
4435    file.setSource(bs.toByteArray());
4436  }
4437
4438  private Element loadFromXmlWithVersionChange(FetchedFile file, String srcV, String dstV) throws Exception {
4439    InputStream src = new ByteArrayInputStream(file.getSource());
4440    ByteArrayOutputStream dst = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
4441    if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(srcV) && VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(dstV)) {
4442      org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.model.Resource r3 = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.XmlParser().parse(src);
4443      org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.model.Resource r14 = VersionConvertorFactory_14_30.convertResource(r3);
4444      new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.XmlParser().compose(dst, r14);
4445    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(srcV) && Constants.VERSION.equals(dstV)) {
4446      org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.model.Resource r3 = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.XmlParser().parse(src);
4447      org.hl7.fhir.r5.model.Resource r5 = VersionConvertorFactory_30_50.convertResource(r3);
4448      new org.hl7.fhir.r5.formats.XmlParser().compose(dst, r5);
4449    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(srcV) && Constants.VERSION.equals(dstV)) {
4450      org.hl7.fhir.r4.model.Resource r4 = new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.XmlParser().parse(src);
4451      org.hl7.fhir.r5.model.Resource r5 = VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(r4);
4452      new org.hl7.fhir.r5.formats.XmlParser().compose(dst, r5);
4453    } else {
4454      throw new Exception("Conversion from "+srcV+" to "+dstV+" is not supported yet"); // because the only know reason to do this is 3.0.1 --> 1.40
4455    }
4456    org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser xp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser(context);
4457    xp.setAllowXsiLocation(true);
4458    xp.setupValidation(ValidationPolicy.EVERYTHING, file.getErrors());
4459    file.getErrors().clear();
4460    Element res = xp.parseSingle(new ByteArrayInputStream(dst.toByteArray()));
4461    if (res == null) {
4462      throw new Exception("Unable to parse XML for "+file.getName());
4463    }
4464    return res;
4465  }
4466
4467  private Element loadFromJsonWithVersionChange(FetchedFile file, String srcV, String dstV) throws Exception {
4468    throw new Exception("Version converting JSON resources is not supported yet"); // because the only know reason to do this is Forge, and it only works with XML
4469  }

4471  private void scan(String type) throws Exception {
4472    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "process type: "+type);
4473    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4474      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4475        if (r.fhirType().equals(type)) {
4476          String url = r.getElement().getChildValue("url");
4477          if (url != null) {
4478            validationFetcher.getOtherUrls().add(url);
4479          }
4480        }
4481      }
4482    }
4483  }

4486    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4487      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4488        if (r.fhirType().equals("List")) {
4489          ListResource l = (ListResource) convertFromElement(r.getElement());
4490          r.setResource(l);          
4491        }
4492      }
4493    }
4494  }
4495  
4496  private void load(String type) throws Exception {
4497    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4498      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4499        if (r.fhirType().equals(type)) {
4500          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "process res: "+r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());
4501          if (r.getResource() == null) {
4502            try {
4503              if (f.getBundleType() == FetchedBundleType.NATIVE) {
4504                r.setResource(parseInternal(f, r));
4505              } else {
4506                r.setResource(parse(f));
4507              }
4508              r.getResource().setUserData("element", r.getElement());
4509            } catch (Exception e) {
4510              throw new Exception("Error parsing "+f.getName()+": "+e.getMessage(), e);
4511            }
4512          }
4513          if (r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
4514            CanonicalResource bc = (CanonicalResource) r.getResource();
4515            if (bc == null) {
4516              throw new Exception("Error: conformance resource "+f.getPath()+" could not be loaded");
4517            }
4518            boolean altered = false;
4519            if (bc.hasUrl()) {
4520              if (adHocTmpDir == null && !listedURLExemptions.contains(bc.getUrl()) && !isExampleResource(bc) && !bc.getUrl().equals(Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), bc.fhirType(), bc.getId()))) {
4521                if (!bc.fhirType().equals("CapabilityStatement") || !bc.getUrl().contains("/Conformance/")) {
4522                  f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.ProfileValidator, IssueType.INVALID, bc.fhirType()+".where(url = '"+bc.getUrl()+"')", "Conformance resource "+f.getPath()+" - the canonical URL ("+Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), bc.fhirType(), 
4523                      bc.getId())+") does not match the URL ("+bc.getUrl()+")", IssueSeverity.ERROR).setMessageId(I18nConstants.RESOURCE_CANONICAL_MISMATCH));
4524                  // throw new Exception("Error: conformance resource "+f.getPath()+" canonical URL ("+Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), bc.fhirType(), bc.getId())+") does not match the URL ("+bc.getUrl()+")");
4525                }
4526              }
4527            } else if (bc.hasId()) {
4528              bc.setUrl(Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), bc.fhirType(), bc.getId()));
4529            } else {
4530              throw new Exception("Error: conformance resource "+f.getPath()+" has neither id nor url");
4531            }
4532            if (replaceLiquidTags(bc)) {
4533              altered = true;
4534            }
4535            if (bc.fhirType().equals("CodeSystem")) {
4536              context.clearTSCache(bc.getUrl());
4537            }
4538            if (businessVersion != null) {
4539              if (!bc.hasVersion()) {
4540                altered = true;
4541                bc.setVersion(businessVersion);
4542              } else if (!bc.getVersion().equals(businessVersion)) {
4543                altered = true;
4544                bc.setVersion(businessVersion);
4545              }
4546            }
4547            if (contacts != null && !contacts.isEmpty()) {
4548              altered = true;
4549              bc.getContact().clear();
4550              bc.getContact().addAll(contacts);
4551            }
4552            if (contexts != null && !contexts.isEmpty()) {
4553              altered = true;
4554              bc.getUseContext().clear();
4555              bc.getUseContext().addAll(contexts);
4556            }
4557            // Todo: Enable these
4558            if (copyright != null && !bc.hasCopyright() && bc.supportsCopyright()) {
4559             altered = true;
4560             bc.setCopyright(copyright);
4561            }
4562            if (bc.hasCopyright() && bc.getCopyright().contains("{{{year}}}")) {
4563              bc.setCopyright(bc.getCopyright().replace("{{{year}}}", Integer.toString(Calendar.getInstance().get(Calendar.YEAR))));
4564              altered = true;
4565            }
4566            if (jurisdictions != null && !jurisdictions.isEmpty()) {
4567              altered = true;
4568              bc.getJurisdiction().clear();
4569              bc.getJurisdiction().addAll(jurisdictions);
4570            }
4571            if (publisher != null) {
4572              altered = true;
4573              bc.setPublisher(publisher);
4574            }
4575
4576
4577            if (!bc.hasDate()) {
4578              altered = true;
4579              bc.setDateElement(new DateTimeType(execTime));
4580            }
4581            if (!bc.hasStatus()) {
4582              altered = true;
4583              bc.setStatus(PublicationStatus.DRAFT);
4584            }
4585            if (new AdjunctFileLoader(binaryPaths, cql).replaceAttachments2(f, r)) {
4586              altered = true;
4587            }
4588            if (altered) {
4589              r.setElement(convertToElement(bc));
4590            }
4591            igpkp.checkForPath(f, r, bc, false);
4592            try {
4593              context.cacheResourceFromPackage(bc, new PackageVersion(publishedIg.getPackageId(), publishedIg.getVersion()));
4594            } catch (Exception e) {
4595              throw new Exception("Exception loading "+bc.getUrl()+": "+e.getMessage(), e);
4596            }
4597          }
4598        } else if (r.fhirType().equals("Bundle")) {
4599          Bundle b = (Bundle) r.getResource();
4600          if (b == null) {
4601            try {
4602              b = (Bundle) convertFromElement(r.getElement());
4603              r.setResource(b);
4604            } catch (Exception e) { 
4605              logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Ignoring conformance resources in Bundle "+f.getName()+" because :"+e.getMessage());
4606            }
4607          }
4608          if (b != null) {
4609            for (BundleEntryComponent be : b.getEntry()) {
4610              if (be.hasResource() && be.getResource().fhirType().equals(type)) {
4611                CanonicalResource mr = (CanonicalResource) be.getResource();
4612                if (mr.hasUrl()) {
4613                  if (!mr.hasUserData("path")) {
4614                    igpkp.checkForPath(f,  r,  mr, true);
4615                  }
4616                  context.cacheResourceFromPackage(mr, new PackageVersion(publishedIg.getPackageId(), publishedIg.getVersion()));
4617                } else
4618                  logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Ignoring resource "+type+"/"+mr.getId()+" in Bundle "+f.getName()+" because it has no canonical URL");
4619
4620              }
4621            }
4622          }
4623        }
4624      }
4625    }
4626  }
4627
4628  private boolean replaceLiquidTags(DomainResource resource) {
4629    if (!resource.hasText() || !resource.getText().hasDiv()) {
4630      return false;
4631    }
4632    Map<String, String> vars = new HashMap<>();
4633    vars.put("{{site.data.fhir.path}}", igpkp.specPath()+"/");
4634    return new LiquidEngine(context, validator.getExternalHostServices()).replaceInHtml(resource.getText().getDiv(), vars);
4635  }

4639  private boolean isExampleResource(CanonicalResource mr) {
4640    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent ir : publishedIg.getDefinition().getResource()) {
4641      if (isSameResource(ir, mr)) {
4642        return ir.hasExample();
4643      }
4644    }
4645    return false;
4646  }

4649  private boolean isSameResource(ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent ir, CanonicalResource mr) {
4650    return ir.getReference().getReference().equals(mr.fhirType()+"/"+mr.getId());
4651  }

4654  private void generateAdditionalExamples() throws Exception {
4655    if (genExamples) {
4656      ProfileUtilities utils = new ProfileUtilities(context, null, null);
4657      for (FetchedFile f : changeList) {
4658        List<StructureDefinition> list = new ArrayList<StructureDefinition>();
4659        for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4660          if (r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition) {
4661            list.add((StructureDefinition) r.getResource());
4662          }
4663        }
4664        for (StructureDefinition sd : list) {
4665          for (Element e : utils.generateExamples(sd, false)) {
4666            FetchedResource nr = new FetchedResource();
4667            nr.setElement(e);
4668            nr.setId(e.getChildValue("id"));
4669            nr.setTitle("Generated Example");
4670            nr.getStatedProfiles().add(sd.getUrl());
4671            f.getResources().add(nr);
4672            igpkp.findConfiguration(f, nr);
4673          }
4674        }
4675      }
4676    }
4677  }
4678
4679  private void generateSnapshots() throws Exception {
4680    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Generate Snapshots");
4681    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4682      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4683        if (r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition) {
4684          if (r.getResEntry() != null) {
4685            ToolingExtensions.setStringExtension(r.getResEntry(), IGHelper.EXT_RESOURCE_INFO, r.fhirType()+":"+IGKnowledgeProvider.getSDType(r));
4686          }
4687
4688          if (!r.isSnapshotted()) {
4689            StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
4690            sd.setSnapshot(null); // make sure its clrared out so we do actually regenerate it at this point
4691            try {
4692              generateSnapshot(f, r, sd, false);
4693            } catch (Exception e) {
4694              throw new Exception("Error generating snapshot for "+f.getTitle()+(f.getResources().size() > 0 ? "("+r.getId()+")" : "")+": "+e.getMessage(), e);
4695            }
4696          }
4697        }
4698      }
4699    }
4700  }
4701
4702  private void generateSnapshot(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, StructureDefinition sd, boolean close) throws Exception {
4703    boolean changed = false;
4704    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Check Snapshot for "+sd.getUrl());
4705    sd.setFhirVersion(FHIRVersion.fromCode(version));
4706    ProfileUtilities utils = new ProfileUtilities(context, f.getErrors(), igpkp);
4707    StructureDefinition base = sd.hasBaseDefinition() ? fetchSnapshotted(sd.getBaseDefinition()) : null;
4708    utils.setIds(sd, true);
4709    utils.setXver(context.getXVer());
4710    if (base == null) {
4711      throw new Exception("Cannot find or generate snapshot for base definition ("+sd.getBaseDefinition()+" from "+sd.getUrl()+")");
4712    }
4713
4714    if (sd.getKind() != StructureDefinitionKind.LOGICAL || sd.getDerivation()==TypeDerivationRule.CONSTRAINT) {
4715      if (!sd.hasSnapshot()) {
4716        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Generate Snapshot for "+sd.getUrl());
4717        List<String> errors = new ArrayList<String>();
4718        if (close) {
4719          utils.closeDifferential(base, sd);
4720        } else {
4721            try {
4722            utils.sortDifferential(base, sd, "profile " + sd.getUrl(), errors, true);
4723          } catch (Exception e) {
4724            f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.ProfileValidator, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "Exception generating snapshot: "+e.getMessage(), IssueSeverity.ERROR));
4725            r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.ProfileValidator, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "Exception generating snapshot: "+e.getMessage(), IssueSeverity.ERROR));
4726          }
4727        }
4728        for (String s : errors) {
4729          f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.ProfileValidator, IssueType.INVALID, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", s, IssueSeverity.ERROR));
4730          r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.ProfileValidator, IssueType.INVALID, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", s, IssueSeverity.ERROR));
4731        }
4732        utils.setIds(sd, true);
4733
4734        String p = sd.getDifferential().hasElement() ? sd.getDifferential().getElement().get(0).getPath() : null;
4735        if (p == null || p.contains(".")) {
4736          changed = true;
4737          sd.getDifferential().getElement().add(0, new ElementDefinition().setPath(p == null ? sd.getType() : p.substring(0, p.indexOf("."))));
4738        }
4739        utils.setDefWebRoot(igpkp.getCanonical());
4740        try {
4741          utils.generateSnapshot(base, sd, sd.getUrl(), Utilities.extractBaseUrl(base.getUserString("path")), sd.getName());
4742        } catch (Exception e) { 
4743          throw new FHIRException("Unable to generate snapshot for "+sd.getUrl()+" in "+f.getName(), e);
4744        }
4745        changed = true;
4746      }
4747    } else { //sd.getKind() == StructureDefinitionKind.LOGICAL
4748      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Generate Snapshot for Logical Model or specialization"+sd.getUrl());
4749      if (!sd.hasSnapshot()) {
4750        utils.setDefWebRoot(igpkp.getCanonical());
4751        utils.generateSnapshot(base, sd, sd.getUrl(), Utilities.extractBaseUrl(base.getUserString("path")), sd.getName());
4752        changed = true;
4753      }
4754    }
4755    if (changed || (!r.getElement().hasChild("snapshot") && sd.hasSnapshot())) {
4756      r.setElement(convertToElement(sd));
4757    }
4758    r.setSnapshotted(true);
4759    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.CONTEXT, "Context.See "+sd.getUrl());
4760    context.cacheResourceFromPackage(sd, new PackageVersion(publishedIg.getPackageId(), publishedIg.getVersion()));
4761  }
4762
4763  private void validateExpressions() {
4764    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "validate Expressions");
4765    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4766      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4767        if (r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition && !r.isSnapshotted()) {
4768          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
4769          validateExpressions(f, sd, r);
4770        }
4771      }
4772    }
4773  }
4774
4775  private void validateExpressions(FetchedFile f, StructureDefinition sd, FetchedResource r) {
4776    FHIRPathEngine fpe = new FHIRPathEngine(context);
4777    for (ElementDefinition ed : sd.getSnapshot().getElement()) {
4778      for (ElementDefinitionConstraintComponent inv : ed.getConstraint()) {
4779        validateExpression(f, sd, fpe, ed, inv, r);
4780      }
4781    }
4782  }
4783
4784  private void validateExpression(FetchedFile f, StructureDefinition sd, FHIRPathEngine fpe, ElementDefinition ed, ElementDefinitionConstraintComponent inv, FetchedResource r) {
4785    if (inv.hasExpression()) {
4786      try {
4787        ExpressionNode n = (ExpressionNode) inv.getUserData("validator.expression.cache");
4788        if (n == null) {
4789          n = fpe.parse(inv.getExpression(), sd.getUrl()+"#"+ed.getId()+" / "+inv.getKey());
4790          inv.setUserData("validator.expression.cache", n);
4791        }
4792        fpe.check(null, sd, ed.getPath(), n);
4793      } catch (Exception e) {
4794        f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.ProfileValidator, IssueType.INVALID, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"').snapshot.element.where('path = '"+ed.getPath()+"').constraint.where(key = '"+inv.getKey()+"')", e.getMessage(), IssueSeverity.ERROR));
4795        r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.ProfileValidator, IssueType.INVALID, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"').snapshot.element.where('path = '"+ed.getPath()+"').constraint.where(key = '"+inv.getKey()+"')", e.getMessage(), IssueSeverity.ERROR));
4796      }
4797    }
4798  }
4799
4800  private StructureDefinition fetchSnapshotted(String url) throws Exception {
4801    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4802      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4803        if (r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition) {
4804          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
4805          if (sd.getUrl().equals(url)) {
4806            if (!r.isSnapshotted()) {
4807              generateSnapshot(f, r, sd, false);
4808            }
4809            return sd;
4810          }
4811        }
4812      }
4813    }
4814    // Special case for logical models:
4815    if ("http://hl7.org/fhir/StructureDefinition/Base".equals(url)) {
4816      return ProfileUtilities.makeBaseDefinition(FHIRVersion.fromCode(version));
4817    }
4818    return context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, url);
4819  }
4820
4821  private void generateLogicalMaps() throws Exception {
4822    StructureMapUtilities mu = new StructureMapUtilities(context, null, null);
4823    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4824      List<StructureMap> maps = new ArrayList<StructureMap>();
4825      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4826        if (r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition) {
4827          StructureMap map = mu.generateMapFromMappings((StructureDefinition) r.getResource());
4828          if (map != null) {
4829            maps.add(map);
4830          }
4831        }
4832      }
4833      for (StructureMap map : maps) {
4834        FetchedResource nr = f.addResource();
4835        nr.setResource(map);
4836        nr.setElement(convertToElement(map));
4837        nr.setId(map.getId());
4838        nr.setTitle(map.getName());
4839        igpkp.findConfiguration(f, nr);
4840      }
4841    }
4842  }
4843
4844  private Resource parseContent(String name, String contentType, String parseVersion, byte[] source) throws Exception {
4845    if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(parseVersion)) {
4846      org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.model.Resource res;
4847      if (contentType.contains("json")) {
4848        res = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser(true).parse(source);
4849      } else if (contentType.contains("xml")) {
4850        res = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.XmlParser(true).parse(source);
4851      } else {
4852        throw new Exception("Unable to determine file type for "+name);
4853      }
4854      return VersionConvertorFactory_30_50.convertResource(res);
4855    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(parseVersion)) {
4856      org.hl7.fhir.r4.model.Resource res;
4857      if (contentType.contains("json")) {
4858        res = new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.JsonParser(true, true).parse(source);
4859      } else if (contentType.contains("xml")) {
4860        res = new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.XmlParser(true).parse(source);
4861      } else {
4862        throw new Exception("Unable to determine file type for "+name);
4863      }
4864      return VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(res);
4865    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(parseVersion)) {
4866      org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.model.Resource res;
4867      if (contentType.contains("json")) {
4868        res = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.JsonParser(true).parse(source);
4869      } else if (contentType.contains("xml")) {
4870        res = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.XmlParser(true).parse(source);
4871      } else {
4872        throw new Exception("Unable to determine file type for "+name);
4873      }
4874      return VersionConvertorFactory_14_50.convertResource(res);
4875    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(parseVersion)) {
4876      org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.model.Resource res;
4877      if (contentType.contains("json")) {
4878        res = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser(true).parse(source);
4879      } else if (contentType.contains("xml")) {
4880        res = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.XmlParser(true).parse(source);
4881      } else {
4882        throw new Exception("Unable to determine file type for "+name);
4883      }
4884
4885      BaseAdvisor_10_50 advisor = new IGR2ConvertorAdvisor5();
4886      return VersionConvertorFactory_10_50.convertResource(res, advisor);
4887    } else if (parseVersion.equals(Constants.VERSION) || VersionUtilities.isR4BVer(parseVersion)) {
4888      if (contentType.contains("json")) {
4889        return new JsonParser(true, true).parse(source);
4890      } else if (contentType.contains("xml")) {
4891        return new XmlParser(true).parse(source);
4892      } else {
4893        throw new Exception("Unable to determine file type for "+name);
4894      }
4895    } else {
4896      throw new Exception("Unsupported version "+parseVersion);
4897    }    
4898  }
4899
4900  private Resource parseInternal(FetchedFile file, FetchedResource res) throws Exception {
4901    String parseVersion = version;
4902    if (!file.getResources().isEmpty()) {
4903      parseVersion = str(file.getResources().get(0).getConfig(), "version", version);
4904    }
4905    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
4906    new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser(context).compose(res.getElement(), bs, OutputStyle.NORMAL, null);
4907    return parseContent("Entry "+res.getId()+" in "+file.getName(), "xml", parseVersion, bs.toByteArray());
4908  }
4909  
4910  private Resource parse(FetchedFile file) throws Exception {
4911    String parseVersion = version;
4912    if (!file.getResources().isEmpty()) {
4913      parseVersion = str(file.getResources().get(0).getConfig(), "version", version);
4914    }
4915    return parseContent(file.getName(), file.getContentType(), parseVersion, file.getSource());
4916  }
4917
4918  private void validate() throws Exception {
4919    if (noValidation) {
4920      return;
4921    }
4922    
4923    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4924      logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, " .. validate "+f.getName());
4925      if (firstExecution) {
4926        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, " .. "+f.getName());
4927      }
4928      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4929        if (!r.isValidated()) {
4930          logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "     validating "+r.getTitle());
4931          validate(f, r);
4932        }
4933      }
4934    }
4935    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, " .. check Profile Examples");
4936    logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "gen narratives");
4937    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4938      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4939        if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition")) {
4940          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
4941          if (!sd.getAbstract()) {
4942            if (sd.getKind() == StructureDefinitionKind.RESOURCE) {
4943              int cE = countStatedExamples(sd.getUrl());
4944              int cI = countFoundExamples(sd.getUrl());
4945              if (cE + cI == 0) {
4946                f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no examples for this profile", IssueSeverity.WARNING));
4947                r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no examples for this profile", IssueSeverity.WARNING));
4948              } else if (cE == 0) {
4949                f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no explicitly linked examples for this profile", IssueSeverity.INFORMATION));
4950                r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no explicitly linked examples for this profile", IssueSeverity.INFORMATION));
4951              }
4952            } else if (sd.getKind() == StructureDefinitionKind.COMPLEXTYPE) {
4953              if (sd.getType().equals("Extension")) {
4954                int c = countUsages(getFixedUrl(sd));
4955                if (c == 0) {
4956                  f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no examples for this extension", IssueSeverity.WARNING));
4957                  r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no examples for this extension", IssueSeverity.WARNING));
4958                }
4959              } else {
4960                int cI = countFoundExamples(sd.getUrl());
4961                if (cI == 0) {
4962                  f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no examples for this data type profile", IssueSeverity.WARNING));
4963                  r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, "StructureDefinition.where(url = '"+sd.getUrl()+"')", "The Implementation Guide contains no examples for this data type profile", IssueSeverity.WARNING));
4964                }
4965              }
4966            }
4967          }
4968        }
4969      }        
4970    }
4971  }
4972
4973  private int countUsages(String fixedUrl) {
4974    int res = 0;
4975    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
4976      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
4977        res = res + countExtensionUsage(r.getElement(), fixedUrl);
4978      }
4979    }
4980    return res;
4981  }
4982
4983
4984
4985  private int countExtensionUsage(Element element, String url) {
4986    int res = 0;
4987    if (element.fhirType().equals("Extension") && url.equals(element.getChildValue("url"))) {
4988      res = res + 1;
4989    }
4990    for (Element child : element.getChildren()) {
4991      res = res + countExtensionUsage(child, url);
4992    }
4993    return res;
4994  }
4995

4997
4998  private String getFixedUrl(StructureDefinition sd) {
4999    for (ElementDefinition ed : sd.getSnapshot().getElement()) {
5000      if (ed.getPath().equals("Extension.url") && ed.hasFixed()) {
5001        return ed.getFixed().primitiveValue();
5002      }
5003    }
5004    return sd.getUrl();
5005  }

5009  private int countStatedExamples(String url) {
5010    int res = 0;
5011    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5012      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5013        for (String p : r.getStatedProfiles()) {
5014          if (url.equals(p)) {
5015            res++;
5016          }
5017        }
5018      }
5019    }
5020    return res;
5021  }
5022
5023  private int countFoundExamples(String url) {
5024    int res = 0;
5025    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5026      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5027        for (String p : r.getFoundProfiles()) {
5028          if (url.equals(p)) {
5029            res++;
5030          }
5031        }
5032      }
5033    }
5034    return res;
5035  }
5036
5037  private void validate(FetchedFile file, FetchedResource r) throws Exception {
5038    if (!passesValidationFilter(r)) {
5039      noValidateResources.add(r);
5040      return;
5041    }
5042    Session tts = tt.start("validation");
5043    List<ValidationMessage> errs = new ArrayList<ValidationMessage>();
5044    r.getElement().setUserData("igpub.context.file", file);
5045    r.getElement().setUserData("igpub.context.resource", r);
5046    if (r.isValidateAsResource()) { 
5047      Resource res = r.getResource();
5048      if (res instanceof Bundle) {
5049        validator.validate(r.getElement(), errs, null, r.getElement());
5050
5051        for (BundleEntryComponent be : ((Bundle) res).getEntry()) {
5052          Resource ber = be.getResource();
5053          if (ber.hasUserData("profile")) {
5054            validator.validate(r.getElement(), errs, ber, ber.getUserString("profile"));
5055          }
5056        }
5057
5058      } else if (res.hasUserData("profile")) {
5059        validator.validate(r.getElement(), errs, res, res.getUserString("profile"));
5060      }
5061    } else if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof Binary && r.getExampleUri() != null) {
5062      Binary bin = (Binary) r.getResource();
5063      validator.validate(r.getElement(), errs, new ByteArrayInputStream(bin.getContent()), getFhirFormatFromMimeType(bin.getContentType()));    
5064    } else {
5065      validator.setNoCheckAggregation(r.isExample() && ToolingExtensions.readBoolExtension(r.getResEntry(), "http://hl7.org/fhir/tools/StructureDefinition/igpublisher-no-check-aggregation"));
5066      if (r.getElement().hasUserData("profile")) {
5067        String ref = r.getElement().getUserString("profile");
5068        if (!Utilities.isAbsoluteUrl(ref)) {
5069          ref = Utilities.pathURL(igpkp.getCanonical(), ref);
5070        }
5071        validator.validate(r.getElement(), errs, null, r.getElement(), ref);
5072      } else {
5073        validator.validate(r.getElement(), errs, null, r.getElement());
5074      }
5075    }
5076    for (ValidationMessage vm : errs) {
5077      String loc = r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId();
5078      if (!vm.getLocation().startsWith(loc)) {
5079        vm.setLocation(loc+": "+vm.getLocation());
5080      }
5081      file.getErrors().add(vm);
5082      r.getErrors().add(vm);
5083    }
5084    r.setValidated(true);
5085    if (r.getConfig() == null) {
5086      igpkp.findConfiguration(file, r);
5087    }
5088    tts.end();
5089  }
5090
5091  public FhirFormat getFhirFormatFromMimeType(String mt) {
5092    if (mt.contains("/xml") || mt.contains("+xml")) {
5093      return FhirFormat.XML;
5094    }
5095    if (mt.contains("/json") || mt.contains("+json")) {
5096      return FhirFormat.JSON;
5097    }
5098    return null;
5099  }

5101  private void generate() throws Exception {
5102    forceDir(tempDir);
5103    forceDir(Utilities.path(tempDir, "_includes"));
5104    forceDir(Utilities.path(tempDir, "data"));
5105
5106    otherFilesRun.clear();
5107    otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(outputDir, "package.tgz"));
5108    otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(outputDir, "package.manifest.json"));
5109    for (String rg : regenList) {
5110      regenerate(rg);
5111    }
5112
5113    updateImplementationGuide();
5114    
5115    for (FetchedFile f : changeList) {
5116      generateNativeOutputs(f, false);
5117    }
5118    
5119    templateBeforeGenerate();
5120
5121    for (FetchedFile f : changeList) {
5122      generateHtmlOutputs(f, false);
5123    }
5124
5125    if (!changeList.isEmpty()) {
5126      generateSummaryOutputs();
5127    }
5128    TextFile.bytesToFile(extensionTracker.generate(), Utilities.path(tempDir, "usage-stats.json"));
5129    try {
5130      log("Sending Usage Stats to Server");
5131      extensionTracker.sendToServer("http://test.fhir.org/usage-stats");
5132    } catch (Exception e) {
5133      log("Submitting Usage Stats failed: "+e.getMessage());
5134    }
5135    
5136    realmRules.addOtherFiles(otherFilesRun, outputDir);
5137    previousVersionComparator.addOtherFiles(otherFilesRun, outputDir);
5138    otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "usage-stats.json"));
5139    
5140    printMemUsage();
5141    System.out.println("Reclaiming memory...");
5142    cleanOutput(tempDir);
5143    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5144      f.trim();
5145    }
5146    System.gc();
5147    printMemUsage();
5148        
5149    if (nestedIgConfig != null) {
5150      if (watch) {
5151        throw new Exception("Cannot run in watch mode when IG has a nested IG.");
5152      }
5153      if (nestedIgOutput == null || igArtifactsPage == null) {
5154        throw new Exception("If nestedIgConfig is specified, then nestedIgOutput and igArtifactsPage must also be specified.");
5155      }
5156      inspector.setAltRootFolder(nestedIgOutput);
5157      log("");
5158      log("**************************");
5159      log("Processing nested IG: " + nestedIgConfig);
5160      childPublisher = new Publisher();
5161      childPublisher.setConfigFile(Utilities.path(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(this.getConfigFile()), nestedIgConfig));
5162      childPublisher.setJekyllCommand(this.getJekyllCommand());
5163      childPublisher.setTxServer(this.getTxServer());
5164      childPublisher.setDebug(this.debug);
5165      childPublisher.setCacheOption(this.getCacheOption());
5166      childPublisher.setIsChild(true);
5167      childPublisher.setMode(this.getMode());
5168      childPublisher.setTargetOutput(this.getTargetOutputNested());
5169      
5170      try {
5171        childPublisher.execute();
5172        log("Done processing nested IG: " + nestedIgConfig);
5173        log("**************************");
5174        childPublisher.updateInspector(inspector, nestedIgOutput);
5175      } catch (Exception e) {
5176        log("Publishing Child IG Failed: " + nestedIgConfig);
5177        throw e;
5178      }
5179      createToc(childPublisher.getPublishedIg().getDefinition().getPage(), igArtifactsPage, nestedIgOutput);
5180    }
5181    fixSearchForm();
5182    if (!noGenerate) {
5183      templateBeforeJekyll();
5184    }
5185
5186    if (runTool()) {
5187      if (!noGenerate) {
5188        templateOnCheck();
5189      }
5190
5191      if (!changeList.isEmpty()) {
5192        File df = makeSpecFile();
5193        npm.addFile(Category.OTHER, "spec.internals", TextFile.fileToBytes(df.getAbsolutePath()));
5194        npm.addFile(Category.OTHER, "validation-summary.json", validationSummaryJson());
5195        npm.addFile(Category.OTHER, "validation-oo.json", validationSummaryOO());
5196        npm.finish();
5197        
5198        if (mode == null || mode == IGBuildMode.MANUAL) {
5199          if (cacheVersion) {
5200            pcm.addPackageToCache(publishedIg.getPackageId(), publishedIg.getVersion(), new FileInputStream(npm.filename()), "[output]");
5201          } else {
5202            pcm.addPackageToCache(publishedIg.getPackageId(), "dev", new FileInputStream(npm.filename()), "[output]");
5203          }
5204        } else if (mode == IGBuildMode.PUBLICATION) {
5205          pcm.addPackageToCache(publishedIg.getPackageId(), publishedIg.getVersion(), new FileInputStream(npm.filename()), "[output]");
5206        }
5207        for (String s : generateVersions) {
5208          generatePackageVersion(npm.filename(), s);
5209        }
5210        generateZips(df);
5211      }
5212    }
5213    
5214    if (childPublisher!=null) {
5215      // Combine list of files so that the validation report will include everything
5216      fileList.addAll(childPublisher.getFileList());
5217    }
5218    
5219    if (!isChild()) {
5220      log("Checking Output HTML");
5221      String statusMessage;
5222      if (mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD) { 
5223        statusMessage = Utilities.escapeXml(sourceIg.present())+", published by "+Utilities.escapeXml(sourceIg.getPublisher())+". This is not an authorized publication; it is the continuous build for version "+workingVersion()+"). This version is based on the current content of <a href=\""+gh()+"\">"+gh()+"</a> and changes regularly. See the <a href=\""+igpkp.getCanonical()+"/history.html\">Directory of published versions</a>"; 
5224      } else if (mode == IGBuildMode.PUBLICATION) { 
5225        statusMessage = "Publication Build: This will be filled in by the publication tooling"; 
5226      } else { 
5227        statusMessage = Utilities.escapeXml(sourceIg.present())+" - Local Development build (v"+workingVersion()+"). See the <a href=\""+igpkp.getCanonical()+"/history.html\">Directory of published versions</a>";
5228      }
5229              
5230      realmRules.addOtherFiles(inspector.getExceptions(), outputDir);
5231      previousVersionComparator.addOtherFiles(inspector.getExceptions(), outputDir);
5232      List<ValidationMessage> linkmsgs = noGenerate ? new ArrayList<ValidationMessage>() : inspector.check(statusMessage);
5233      int bl = 0;
5234      int lf = 0;
5235      for (ValidationMessage m : ValidationPresenter.filterMessages(linkmsgs, true, suppressedMessages)) {
5236        if (m.getLevel() == IssueSeverity.ERROR) {
5237          if (m.getType() == IssueType.NOTFOUND) {
5238            bl++;
5239          } else {
5240            lf++;
5241          }
5242        } else if (m.getLevel() == IssueSeverity.FATAL) {
5243          throw new Exception(m.getMessage());
5244        }
5245      }
5246      log("  ... "+Integer.toString(inspector.total())+" html "+checkPlural("file", inspector.total())+", "+Integer.toString(lf)+" "+checkPlural("page", lf)+" invalid xhtml ("+Integer.toString((lf*100)/(inspector.total() == 0 ? 1 : inspector.total()))+"%)");
5247      log("  ... "+Integer.toString(inspector.links())+" "+checkPlural("link", inspector.links())+", "+Integer.toString(bl)+" broken "+checkPlural("link", lf)+" ("+Integer.toString((bl*100)/(inspector.links() == 0 ? 1 : inspector.links()))+"%)");
5248      errors.addAll(linkmsgs);    
5249      if (brokenLinksError && linkmsgs.size() > 0) {
5250        throw new Error("Halting build because broken links have been found, and these are disallowed in the IG control file");
5251      }
5252      if (mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD && inspector.isMissingPublishBox()) {
5253        throw new FHIRException("The auto-build infrastructure does not publish IGs that contain HTML pages without the publish-box present ("+inspector.getMissingPublishboxSummary()+"). For further information, see note at http://wiki.hl7.org/index.php?title=FHIR_Implementation_Guide_Publishing_Requirements#HL7_HTML_Standards_considerations");
5254      }
5255
5256      log("Build final .zip");
5257      ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(tempDir, "full-ig.zip"));
5258      zip.addFolder(outputDir, "site/", false);
5259      zip.addFileSource("index.html", REDIRECT_SOURCE, false);
5260      zip.close();
5261      Utilities.copyFile(Utilities.path(tempDir, "full-ig.zip"), Utilities.path(outputDir, "full-ig.zip"));
5262      log("Final .zip built");
5263    }
5264  }
5265
5266  private byte[] validationSummaryOO() throws IOException {
5267    Bundle bnd = new Bundle();
5268    bnd.setType(BundleType.COLLECTION);
5269    bnd.setTimestamp(new Date());
5270    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5271      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5272        OperationOutcome oo = new OperationOutcome();
5273        oo.setId(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId());
5274        bnd.addEntry().setFullUrl(igpkp.getCanonical()+"/OperationOutcome/"+oo.getId()).setResource(oo);
5275        for (ValidationMessage vm : r.getErrors()) {
5276          if (!vm.getLevel().isHint())
5277          oo.addIssue(OperationOutcomeUtilities.convertToIssue(vm, oo));
5278        }
5279      }
5280    }
5281    return new JsonParser().composeBytes(bnd);
5282  }
5283
5284  private byte[] validationSummaryJson() throws UnsupportedEncodingException {
5285    JsonObject json = new JsonObject();
5286    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5287      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5288        JsonObject rd = new JsonObject();
5289        json.add(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId(), rd);
5290        createValidationSummary(rd, r);
5291      }
5292    }
5293    return JsonTrackingParser.write(json).getBytes("UTF-8");
5294  }
5295
5296  private void createValidationSummary(JsonObject fd, FetchedResource r) {
5297    int e = 0;
5298    int w = 0;
5299    int i = 0;
5300    for (ValidationMessage vm : r.getErrors()) {
5301      if (vm.getLevel() == IssueSeverity.INFORMATION) {
5302        i++;
5303      } else if (vm.getLevel() == IssueSeverity.WARNING) {
5304        w++;
5305      } else {
5306        e++;
5307      }
5308    }
5309    fd.addProperty("errors", e);
5310    fd.addProperty("warnings", w);
5311//    fd.addProperty("hints", i);
5312  }
5313
5314  private void fixSearchForm() throws IOException {
5315    
5316    String sfn = Utilities.path(tempDir, "searchform.html");
5317    if (new File(sfn).exists() ) {
5318      String sf = TextFile.fileToString(sfn);
5319      sf = sf.replace("{{title}}", publishedIg.present());
5320      sf = sf.replace("{{url}}", targetUrl());
5321      TextFile.stringToFile(sf, sfn);      
5322    }    
5323  }

5325  private void printMemUsage() {
5326    int mb = 1024*1024;
5327    Runtime runtime = Runtime.getRuntime();
5328    System.out.print("## Memory (MB): ");
5329    System.out.print("Use = " + (runtime.totalMemory() - runtime.freeMemory()) / mb);
5330    System.out.print(", Free = " + runtime.freeMemory() / mb);
5331    System.out.print(", Total = " + runtime.totalMemory() / mb);
5332    System.out.println(", Max =" + runtime.maxMemory() / mb);
5333  }

5335  private void generatePackageVersion(String filename, String ver) throws IOException {
5336    NpmPackageVersionConverter self = new NpmPackageVersionConverter(filename, Utilities.path(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(filename), publishedIg.getPackageId()+"."+ver+".tgz"), ver);
5337    self.execute();
5338    for (String s : self.getErrors()) {
5339      errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "ImplementationGuide", "Error creating "+ver+" package: "+s, IssueSeverity.ERROR));
5340    }
5341  }

5348  private void download(String address, String filename) throws IOException {
5349    URL url = new URL(address);
5350    URLConnection c = url.openConnection();
5351    InputStream s = c.getInputStream();
5352    FileOutputStream f = new FileOutputStream(filename);
5353    transfer(s, f, 1024);
5354    f.close();   
5355  }
5356  
5357  public static void transfer(InputStream in, OutputStream out, int buffer) throws IOException {
5358    byte[] read = new byte[buffer]; // Your buffer size.
5359    while (0 < (buffer = in.read(read))) {
5360      out.write(read, 0, buffer);
5361    }
5362}

5364  private void updateImplementationGuide() throws Exception {
5365    FetchedResource r = altMap.get(IG_NAME).getResources().get(0);
5366    if (!publishedIg.hasText() || !publishedIg.getText().hasDiv()) {
5367      publishedIg.setText(((ImplementationGuide)r.getResource()).getText());
5368    }
5369    r.setResource(publishedIg);
5370    r.setElement(convertToElement(publishedIg));
5371    
5372    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
5373    new JsonParser().setOutputStyle(OutputStyle.NORMAL).compose(bs, publishedIg);
5374    npm.addFile(Category.RESOURCE, "ig-r4.json", bs.toByteArray());
5375    
5376    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent res : publishedIg.getDefinition().getResource()) {
5377      FetchedResource rt = null;
5378      for (FetchedFile tf : fileList) {
5379        for (FetchedResource tr : tf.getResources()) {
5380          if (tr.getLocalRef().equals(res.getReference().getReference())) {
5381            rt = tr;
5382          }
5383        }
5384      }
5385      if (rt != null) {
5386        if (!rt.getProvenance()) {
5387          // Don't expose a page for a resource that is just provenance information
5388          String path = igpkp.doReplacements(igpkp.getLinkFor(rt, false), rt, null, null);
5389          res.addExtension().setUrl("http://hl7.org/fhir/StructureDefinition/implementationguide-page").setValue(new UriType(path));
5390          inspector.addLinkToCheck("Implementation Guide", path, "fake generated link");
5391        }
5392      }
5393    }
5394  }

5396  private String checkPlural(String word, int c) {
5397    return c == 1 ? word : Utilities.pluralizeMe(word);
5398  }
5399
5400  private void regenerate(String uri) throws Exception {
5401    Resource res ;
5402    if (uri.contains("/StructureDefinition/")) {
5403      res = context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, uri);
5404    } else {
5405      throw new Exception("Unable to process "+uri);
5406    }
5407
5408    if (res == null) {
5409      throw new Exception("Unable to find regeneration source for "+uri);
5410    }
5411
5412    CanonicalResource bc = (CanonicalResource) res;
5413
5414    FetchedFile f = new FetchedFile(bc.getUserString("path"));
5415    FetchedResource r = f.addResource();
5416    r.setResource(res);
5417    r.setId(bc.getId());
5418    r.setTitle(bc.getName());
5419    r.setValidated(true);
5420    r.setElement(convertToElement(bc));
5421    igpkp.findConfiguration(f, r);
5422    bc.setUserData("config", r.getConfig());
5423    generateNativeOutputs(f, true);
5424    generateHtmlOutputs(f, true);
5425  }
5426
5427  private Element convertToElement(Resource res) throws IOException, org.hl7.fhir.exceptions.FHIRException, FHIRFormatError, DefinitionException {
5428    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
5429    if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(version)) {
5430      org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser();
5431      jp.compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_30_50.convertResource(res));
5432    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(version)) {
5433      org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.JsonParser();
5434      jp.compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(res));
5435    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(version)) {
5436      org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.JsonParser();
5437      jp.compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_14_50.convertResource(res));
5438    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(version)) {
5439      org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser();
5440      jp.compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_10_50.convertResource(res, new IGR2ConvertorAdvisor5()));
5441    } else {
5442      org.hl7.fhir.r5.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.formats.JsonParser();
5443      jp.compose(bs, res);
5444    }
5445    ByteArrayInputStream bi = new ByteArrayInputStream(bs.toByteArray());
5446    return new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context).parseSingle(bi);
5447  }
5448
5449  private Resource convertFromElement(Element res) throws IOException, org.hl7.fhir.exceptions.FHIRException, FHIRFormatError, DefinitionException {
5450    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
5451    new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context).compose(res, bs, OutputStyle.NORMAL, null);
5452    ByteArrayInputStream bi = new ByteArrayInputStream(bs.toByteArray());
5453    if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(version)) {
5454      org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser();
5455      return  VersionConvertorFactory_30_50.convertResource(jp.parse(bi));
5456    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(version)) {
5457      org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.JsonParser();
5458      return  VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(jp.parse(bi));
5459    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(version)) {
5460      org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.JsonParser();
5461      return  VersionConvertorFactory_14_50.convertResource(jp.parse(bi));
5462    } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(version)) {
5463        org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser();
5464        return VersionConvertorFactory_10_50.convertResource(jp.parse(bi));
5465    } else { // if (version.equals(Constants.VERSION)) {
5466      org.hl7.fhir.r5.formats.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.formats.JsonParser();
5467      return jp.parse(bi);
5468    } 
5469  }

5478  public void cleanOutputFile(File f) {
5479 // Lloyd: this was changed from getPath to getCanonicalPath, but 
5480 // Grahame: changed it back because this was achange that broke everything, and with no reason provided

5488  private boolean isValidFile(String p) {
5489    if (otherFilesStartup.contains(p)) {
5490      return true;
5491    }
5492    if (otherFilesRun.contains(p)) {
5493      return true;
5494    }
5495    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5496      if (f.getOutputNames().contains(p)) {
5497        return true;
5498      }
5499    }
5500    for (FetchedFile f : altMap.values()) {
5501      if (f.getOutputNames().contains(p)) {
5502        return true;
5503      }
5504    }
5505    return false;
5506  }
5507
5508  private File makeSpecFile() throws Exception {
5509    SpecMapManager map = new SpecMapManager(npmName, version, Constants.VERSION, Integer.toString(ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION), execTime, igpkp.getCanonical());
5510    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5511      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5512        String u = igpkp.getCanonical()+r.getUrlTail();
5513        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
5514          String uc = ((CanonicalResource) r.getResource()).getUrl();
5515          if (uc != null && !u.equals(uc) && !isListedURLExemption(uc) && !isExampleResource((CanonicalResource) r.getResource()) && adHocTmpDir == null) {
5516            f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, f.getName(), "URL Mismatch "+u+" vs "+uc, IssueSeverity.ERROR));
5517            r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.BUSINESSRULE, f.getName(), "URL Mismatch "+u+" vs "+uc, IssueSeverity.ERROR));
5518          }
5519          if (uc != null && !u.equals(uc)) {
5520            map.path(uc, igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true));
5521          }
5522          String v = ((CanonicalResource) r.getResource()).getVersion();
5523          if (v != null) {
5524            map.path(uc + "|" + v, v + "/" + igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true));
5525          }
5526        }
5527        map.path(u, igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true));
5528      }
5529    }
5530    for (String s : new File(outputDir).list()) {
5531      if (s.endsWith(".html")) {
5532        map.target(s);
5533      }
5534    }
5535    File df = File.createTempFile("fhir", "tmp");
5536    df.deleteOnExit();
5537    map.save(df.getCanonicalPath());
5538    return df;
5539  }
5540  
5541  private void generateZips(File df) throws Exception {
5542    if (generateExampleZip(FhirFormat.XML)) {
5543      generateDefinitions(FhirFormat.XML, df.getCanonicalPath());
5544    }
5545    if (generateExampleZip(FhirFormat.JSON)) {
5546      generateDefinitions(FhirFormat.JSON, df.getCanonicalPath());
5547    }
5548    if (supportsTurtle() && generateExampleZip(FhirFormat.TURTLE)) {
5549      generateDefinitions(FhirFormat.TURTLE, df.getCanonicalPath());
5550    }
5551    generateExpansions();
5552    generateValidationPack(df.getCanonicalPath());
5553    // Create an IG-specific named igpack to make is easy to grab the igpacks for multiple igs without the names colliding (Talk to Lloyd before removing this)
5554    FileUtils.copyFile(new File(Utilities.path(outputDir, "validator.pack")),new File(Utilities.path(outputDir, "validator-" + sourceIg.getId() + ".pack")));
5555    generateCsvZip();
5556    generateExcelZip();
5557//    generateRegistryUploadZip(df.getCanonicalPath());
5558  }

5560  private boolean supportsTurtle() {
5561    return !Utilities.existsInList(version, "1.0.2", "1.4.0");
5562  }

5565  private void generateExpansions() throws FileNotFoundException, IOException {
5566    Bundle exp = new Bundle();
5567    exp.setType(BundleType.COLLECTION);
5568    exp.setId(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
5569    exp.getMeta().setLastUpdated(execTime.getTime());
5570    for (ValueSet vs : expansions) {
5571      exp.addEntry().setResource(vs).setFullUrl(vs.getUrl());
5572    }
5573    
5574    new JsonParser().setOutputStyle(OutputStyle.PRETTY).compose(new FileOutputStream(Utilities.path(outputDir, "expansions.json")), exp);
5575    new XmlParser().setOutputStyle(OutputStyle.PRETTY).compose(new FileOutputStream(Utilities.path(outputDir, "expansions.xml")), exp);
5576    ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "expansions.json.zip"));
5577    zip.addFileName("expansions.json", Utilities.path(outputDir, "expansions.json"), false);
5578    zip.close();
5579    zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "expansions.xml.zip"));
5580    zip.addFileName("expansions.xml", Utilities.path(outputDir, "expansions.xml"), false);
5581    zip.close();
5582  }

5589  private void generateDefinitions(FhirFormat fmt, String specFile)  throws Exception {
5590    // public definitions
5591    Set<FetchedResource> files = new HashSet<FetchedResource>();
5592    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5593      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5594        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
5595          files.add(r);
5596        }
5597      }
5598    }
5599    if (!files.isEmpty()) {
5600      ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "definitions."+fmt.getExtension()+".zip"));
5601      for (FetchedResource r : files) {
5602        ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
5603        if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(version)) {
5604          org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.model.Resource r3 = VersionConvertorFactory_30_50.convertResource(r.getResource());
5605          if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.JSON)) {
5606            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, r3);
5607          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.XML)) {
5608            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.XmlParser().compose(bs, r3);
5609          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.TURTLE)) {
5610            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.RdfParser().compose(bs, r3);
5611          }
5612        } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(version)) {
5613          org.hl7.fhir.r4.model.Resource r4 = VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(r.getResource());
5614          if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.JSON)) {
5615            new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, r4);
5616          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.XML)) {
5617            new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.XmlParser().compose(bs, r4);
5618          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.TURTLE)) {
5619            new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.RdfParser().compose(bs, r4);
5620          }
5621        } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(version)) {
5622          org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.model.Resource r14 = VersionConvertorFactory_14_50.convertResource(r.getResource());
5623          if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.JSON)) {
5624            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, r14);
5625          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.XML)) {
5626            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.XmlParser().compose(bs, r14);
5627          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.TURTLE)) {
5628            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.RdfParser().compose(bs, r14);
5629          }
5630        } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(version)) {
5631          BaseAdvisor_10_50 advisor = new IGR2ConvertorAdvisor5();
5632          org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.model.Resource r14 = VersionConvertorFactory_10_50.convertResource(r.getResource(), advisor);
5633          if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.JSON)) {
5634            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, r14);
5635          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.XML)) {
5636            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.XmlParser().compose(bs, r14);
5637          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.TURTLE)) {
5638            throw new Exception("Turtle is not supported for releases < 3");
5639          }
5640        } else {
5641          if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.JSON)) {
5642            new JsonParser().compose(bs, r.getResource());
5643          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.XML)) {
5644            new XmlParser().compose(bs, r.getResource());
5645          } else if (fmt.equals(FhirFormat.TURTLE)) {
5646            new RdfParser().compose(bs, r.getResource());
5647          }
5648        }
5649        zip.addBytes(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"."+fmt.getExtension(), bs.toByteArray(), false);
5650      }
5651      zip.addFileName("spec.internals", specFile, false);
5652      zip.close();
5653    }
5654  }

5664  private void generateRegistryUploadZip(String specFile)  throws Exception {
5665    ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "registry.fhir.org.zip"));
5666    zip.addFileName("spec.internals", specFile, false);
5667    StringBuilder ri = new StringBuilder();
5668    ri.append("[registry]\r\n");
5669    ri.append("toolversion="+getToolingVersion()+"\r\n");
5670    ri.append("fhirversion="+version+"\r\n");
5671    int i = 0;
5672    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5673      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5674        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
5675          try {
5676            ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
5677            org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.model.Resource r3 = VersionConvertorFactory_30_50.convertResource(r.getResource());
5678            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, r3);
5679            zip.addBytes(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".json", bs.toByteArray(), false);
5680          } catch (Exception e) {
5681            log("Can't store "+r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+" in R3 format for registry.fhir.org");
5682            e.printStackTrace();
5683          }
5684          i++;
5685        }
5686      }
5687    }
5688    ri.append("resourcecount="+Integer.toString(i)+"\r\n");
5689    zip.addBytes("registry.info",TextFile.stringToBytes(ri.toString(), false), false);
5690    zip.close();
5691  }
5692
5693  private void generateValidationPack(String specFile)  throws Exception {
5694    String sch = makeTempZip(".sch");
5695    String js = makeTempZip(".schema.json");
5696    String shex = makeTempZip(".shex");
5697
5698    ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "validator.pack"));
5699    zip.addBytes("version.info", makeNewVersionInfo(version), false);
5700    zip.addFileName("spec.internals", specFile, false);
5701    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5702      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5703        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
5704          ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
5705          if (VersionUtilities.isR3Ver(version)) {
5706            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu3.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_30_50.convertResource(r.getResource()));
5707          } else if (VersionUtilities.isR4Ver(version)) {
5708            new org.hl7.fhir.r4.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_40_50.convertResource(r.getResource()));
5709          } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2BVer(version)) {
5710            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2016may.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_14_50.convertResource(r.getResource()));
5711          } else if (VersionUtilities.isR2Ver(version)) {
5712            BaseAdvisor_10_50 advisor = new IGR2ConvertorAdvisor5();
5713            new org.hl7.fhir.dstu2.formats.JsonParser().compose(bs, VersionConvertorFactory_10_50.convertResource(r.getResource(), advisor));
5714          } else if (version.equals(Constants.VERSION) || VersionUtilities.isR4BVer(version)) {
5715            new JsonParser().compose(bs, r.getResource());
5716          } else {
5717            throw new Exception("Unsupported version "+version);
5718          }
5719          zip.addBytes(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".json", bs.toByteArray(), false);
5720        }
5721      }
5722    }
5723    if (sch != null) {
5724      zip.addFileName("schematron.zip", sch, false);
5725    }
5726    if (js != null) {
5727      zip.addFileName("json.schema.zip", sch, false);
5728    }
5729    if (shex != null) {
5730      zip.addFileName("shex.zip", sch, false);
5731    }
5732    zip.close();
5733  }
5734
5735  private byte[] makeNewVersionInfo(String version) throws IOException {
5736    String is = "[FHIR]\r\nversion="+version+"\r\n";
5737    IniFile ini = new IniFile(new ByteArrayInputStream(TextFile.stringToBytes(is, false)));
5738    ini.setStringProperty("IG", "version", version, null);
5739    ini.setStringProperty("IG", "date",  new SimpleDateFormat("yyyyMMddhhmmssZ", new Locale("en", "US")).format(execTime.getTime()), null);
5740    ByteArrayOutputStream b = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
5741    ini.save(b);
5742    return b.toByteArray();
5743  }

5746  private String makeTempZip(String ext) throws IOException {
5747    File tmp = File.createTempFile("fhir", "zip");
5748    tmp.deleteOnExit();
5749    if (generateZipByExtension(tmp.getCanonicalPath(), ext)) {
5750      return tmp.getCanonicalPath();
5751    } else {
5752      return null;
5753    }
5754  }
5755
5756  private boolean generateZipByExtension(String path, String ext) throws IOException {
5757    Set<String> files = new HashSet<String>();
5758    for (String s : new File(outputDir).list()) {
5759      if (s.endsWith(ext)) {
5760        files.add(s);
5761      }
5762    }
5763    if (files.size() == 0) {
5764      return false;
5765    }
5766    ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(path);
5767    for (String fn : files) {
5768      zip.addFileName(fn, Utilities.path(outputDir, fn), false);
5769    }
5770    zip.close();
5771    return true;
5772  }
5773  
5774  private boolean generateExampleZip(FhirFormat fmt) throws Exception {
5775    Set<String> files = new HashSet<String>();
5776    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5777      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5778        String fn = Utilities.path(outputDir, r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"."+fmt.getExtension());
5779        if (new File(fn).exists()) {
5780          files.add(fn);
5781        }
5782      }
5783    }
5784    if (!files.isEmpty()) {
5785      ZipGenerator zip = new ZipGenerator(Utilities.path(outputDir, "examples."+fmt.getExtension()+".zip"));
5786      for (String fn : files) {
5787        zip.addFileName(fn.substring(fn.lastIndexOf(File.separator)+1), fn, false);
5788      }
5789      zip.close();
5790    }
5791       
5792    return !files.isEmpty();
5793  }
5794
5795  private boolean runTool() throws Exception {
5796    if (noGenerate) {
5797      FileUtils.copyDirectory(new File(tempDir), new File(outputDir));
5798      return true;
5799    }
5800    switch (tool) {
5801    case Jekyll: return runJekyll();
5802    default:
5803      throw new Exception("unimplemented tool");
5804    }
5805  }
5806
5807  public class MyFilterHandler extends OutputStream {
5808
5809    private byte[] buffer;
5810    private int length;
5811    private boolean observedToSucceed = false;
5812
5813    public MyFilterHandler() {
5814      buffer = new byte[256];
5815    }
5816
5817    public String getBufferString() {
5818        return new String(this.buffer, 0, length);
5819    }
5820
5821    private boolean passJekyllFilter(String s) {
5822      if (Utilities.noString(s)) {
5823        return false;
5824      }
5825      if (s.contains("Source:")) {
5826        return true;
5827      }
5828      if (s.contains("Liquid Exception:")) {
5829          return true;
5830      }
5831      if (s.contains("Destination:")) {
5832        return false;
5833      }
5834      if (s.contains("Configuration")) {
5835        return false;
5836      }
5837      if (s.contains("Incremental build:")) {
5838        return false;
5839      }
5840      if (s.contains("Auto-regeneration:")) {
5841        return false;
5842      }
5843      if (s.contains("done in")) {
5844        observedToSucceed = true;
5845      }
5846      return true;
5847    }
5848
5849    @Override
5850    public void write(int b) throws IOException {
5851      buffer[length] = (byte) b;
5852      length++;
5853      if (b == 10) { // eoln
5854        String s = new String(buffer, 0, length);
5855        if (passJekyllFilter(s)) {
5856          log("Jekyll: "+s.trim());
5857        }
5858        length = 0;
5859      }
5860    }
5861  }
5862
5863  private boolean runJekyll() throws IOException, InterruptedException {
5864    Session tts = tt.start("jekyll");
5865
5866    DefaultExecutor exec = new DefaultExecutor();
5867    exec.setExitValue(0);
5868    MyFilterHandler pumpHandler = new MyFilterHandler();
5869    PumpStreamHandler pump = new PumpStreamHandler(pumpHandler, pumpHandler);
5870    exec.setStreamHandler(pump);
5871    exec.setWorkingDirectory(new File(tempDir));
5872    ExecuteWatchdog watchdog = new ExecuteWatchdog(JEKYLL_TIMEOUT);
5873    exec.setWatchdog(watchdog);
5874
5875    try {
5876            if (SystemUtils.IS_OS_WINDOWS) {
5877              exec.execute(org.apache.commons.exec.CommandLine.parse("cmd /C "+jekyllCommand+" build --destination \""+outputDir+"\""));
5878            } else {
5879              exec.execute(org.apache.commons.exec.CommandLine.parse(jekyllCommand+" build --destination \""+outputDir+"\""));
5880            }
5881            tts.end();
5882    } catch (IOException ioex) {
5883      tts.end();
5884      if (pumpHandler.observedToSucceed) {
5885        log("Jekyll claimed to succeed, but returned an error. Proceeding anyway");
5886      } else {
5887        log("Jekyll has failed. Complete output from running Jekyll: " + pumpHandler.getBufferString());
5888        log("Note: Check that Jekyll is installed correctly");
5889        throw ioex;
5890      }
5891    }
5892    return true;
5893  }
5894
5895  private void dumpVars() {
5896    log("---- Props -------------");
5897    Properties properties = System.getProperties();
5898    properties.forEach((k, v) -> log((String) k + ": "+ v));
5899    log("---- Vars -------------");
5900    System.getenv().forEach((k, v) -> {
5901      log(k + ":" + v);
5902    });
5903    log("-----------------------");
5904  }

5927    JsonObject data = new JsonObject();
5928    int i = 0;
5929    JsonObject maturities = new JsonObject();
5930    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
5931      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
5932        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource) {
5933          String fmm = ToolingExtensions.readStringExtension((DomainResource) r.getResource(), ToolingExtensions.EXT_FMM_LEVEL);
5934          if (fmm != null) {

5936          }

5947          item.addProperty("path", sd.getUserString("path"));
5948          item.addProperty("kind", sd.getKind().toCode());
5949          item.addProperty("type", sd.getType());
5950          item.addProperty("base", sd.getBaseDefinition());
5951          StructureDefinition base = sd.hasBaseDefinition() ? context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, sd.getBaseDefinition()) : null;
5952          if (base != null) {
5953            item.addProperty("basename", base.getName());
5954            item.addProperty("basepath", Utilities.escapeXml(base.getUserString("path")));
5955          } else if ("http://hl7.org/fhir/StructureDefinition/Base".equals(sd.getBaseDefinition())) {
5956            item.addProperty("basename", "Base");
5957            item.addProperty("basepath", "http://hl7.org/fhir/StructureDefinition/Element");            
5958          }
5959          item.addProperty("status", sd.getStatus().toCode());
5960          item.addProperty("date", sd.getDate().toString());
5961          item.addProperty("abstract", sd.getAbstract());
5962          if (sd.hasDerivation()) {
5963            item.addProperty("derivation", sd.getDerivation().toCode());
5964          }
5965          item.addProperty("publisher", sd.getPublisher());
5966          item.addProperty("copyright", sd.getCopyright());
5967          item.addProperty("description", sd.getDescription());
5968          if (sd.hasContext()) {
5969            JsonArray contexts = new JsonArray();

5973              contexts.add(citem);
5974              citem.addProperty("type", ec.getType().getDisplay());
5975              citem.addProperty("type", ec.getExpression());
5976            }
5977          }
5978          i++;
5979        }
5980      }
5981    }
5982    if (maturities.keySet().size() > 0) {
5983      data.add("maturities", maturities);
5984    }
5985
5986    for (FetchedResource r: examples) {
5987      FetchedResource baseRes = getResourceForUri(r.getExampleUri());
5988      if (baseRes == null) {
5989        // We only yell if the resource doesn't exist, not only if it doesn't exist in the current IG.
5990        if (context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, r.getExampleUri())==null)
5991          errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.NOTFOUND, r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId(), "Unable to find profile " + r.getExampleUri() + " nominated as the profile for which resource " + r.getUrlTail()+" is an example", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
5992      } else {
5993        baseRes.addStatedExample(r);
5994      }
5995    }
5996
5997    Gson gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
5998    String json = gson.toJson(data);
5999    TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "structuredefinitions.json"), false);
6000
6001    // now, list the profiles - all the profiles
6002    data = new JsonObject();
6003    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6004      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6005        if (r.fhirType().equals("Questionnaire")) {
6006          Questionnaire q = (Questionnaire) r.getResource();
6007
6008          JsonObject item = new JsonObject();
6009          data.add(q.getId(), item);
6010          item.addProperty("index", i);
6011          item.addProperty("url", q.getUrl());
6012          item.addProperty("name", q.getName());
6013          item.addProperty("path", q.getUserString("path"));
6014          item.addProperty("status", q.getStatus().toCode());
6015          item.addProperty("date", q.getDate().toString());
6016          item.addProperty("publisher", q.getPublisher());
6017          item.addProperty("copyright", q.getCopyright());
6018          item.addProperty("description", q.getDescription());
6019          i++;
6020        }
6021      }
6022    }
6023    
6024    gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
6025    json = gson.toJson(data);
6026    TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "questionnaires.json"), false);
6027
6028    // now, list the profiles - all the profiles
6029    data = new JsonObject();
6030    i = 0;
6031    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6032      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6033        JsonObject item = new JsonObject();
6034        data.add(r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId(), item);
6035        item.addProperty("history", r.hasHistory());
6036        item.addProperty("index", i);
6037        item.addProperty("source", f.getStatedPath());
6038        item.addProperty("path", r.getElement().getUserString("path"));
6039        if (r.getResource() != null) {
6040          if (r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
6041            CanonicalResource cr = (CanonicalResource) r.getResource();
6042            item.addProperty("url", cr.getUrl());
6043            if (cr.hasName()) {
6044              item.addProperty("name", cr.getName());
6045            }
6046            if (cr.hasTitle()) {
6047              item.addProperty("title", cr.getTitle());
6048            }
6049            if (cr.hasVersion()) {
6050              item.addProperty("version", cr.getVersion());
6051            }
6052            if (cr.hasDate()) {
6053              item.addProperty("date", cr.getDateElement().primitiveValue());
6054            }
6055            if (cr.hasStatus()) {
6056              item.addProperty("status", cr.getStatus().toCode());
6057            }
6058          }
6059          if (r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource) {
6060            org.hl7.fhir.igtools.renderers.StatusRenderer.ResourceStatusInformation info = StatusRenderer.analyse((DomainResource) r.getResource());
6061            JsonObject jo = new JsonObject();
6062            if (info.getColorClass() != null) {
6063              jo.addProperty("class", info.getColorClass());
6064            }
6065            if (info.getFmm() != null) {
6066              jo.addProperty("fmm", info.getFmm());
6067            }
6068            if (info.getOwner() != null) {
6069              jo.addProperty("owner", info.getOwner());
6070            }
6071            if (info.getOwnerLink() != null) {
6072              jo.addProperty("link", info.getOwnerLink());
6073            }
6074            if (info.getSstatus() != null) {
6075              jo.addProperty("standards-status", info.getSstatus());
6076            }
6077            if (info.getStatus() != null) {
6078              jo.addProperty("status", info.getStatus());
6079            }

6081              item.add("status", jo);
6082            }
6083          }
6084        }
6085        i++;
6086      }
6087    }
6088
6089    json = gson.toJson(data);
6090    TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "resources.json"), false);
6091

6093      JsonObject pages = new JsonObject();
6094      addPageData(pages, publishedIg.getDefinition().getPage(), "0", "");
6095      //   gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
6096      //   json = gson.toJson(pages);
6097      Entry<String, JsonElement> priorEntry = null;
6098      for (Entry<String, JsonElement> entry: pages.entrySet()) {
6099        if (priorEntry!=null) {
6100          String priorPageUrl = priorEntry.getKey();
6101          String currentPageUrl = entry.getKey();
6102          JsonObject priorPageData = priorEntry.getValue().getAsJsonObject();
6103          JsonObject currentPageData = entry.getValue().getAsJsonObject();
6104          priorPageData.addProperty("next", currentPageUrl);
6105          currentPageData.addProperty("previous", priorPageUrl);
6106        }
6107        priorEntry = entry;
6108      }
6109      json = pages.toString();

6111
