6120  private void generateCanonicalSummary() throws IOException {
6121    List<CanonicalResource> crlist = new ArrayList<>();
6122    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6123      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6124        if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
6125          crlist.add((CanonicalResource) r.getResource());
6126        }
6127      }
6128    }
6129    Collections.sort(crlist, new ResourceSorters.CanonicalResourceSortByUrl());
6130    JsonArray list = new JsonArray();
6131    for (CanonicalResource cr : crlist) {
6132      JsonObject obj = new JsonObject();
6133      obj.addProperty("id", cr.getId());
6134      obj.addProperty("type", cr.fhirType());
6135      if (cr.hasUrl()) {
6136        obj.addProperty("url", cr.getUrl());
6137      }
6138      if (cr.hasVersion()) {
6139        obj.addProperty("version", cr.getVersion());
6140      }
6141      if (cr.hasName()) {
6142        obj.addProperty("name", cr.getName());
6143      }
6144      JsonArray oids = new JsonArray();
6145      JsonArray urls = new JsonArray();
6146      for (Identifier id : cr.getIdentifier()) {
6147        if (id != null) {
6148          if("urn:ietf:rfc:3986".equals(id.getSystem()) && id.hasValue()) {
6149            if (id.getValue().startsWith("urn:oid:")) {
6150              oids.add(id.getValue().substring(8));
6151            } else {
6152              urls.add(id.getValue());
6153            }
6154          }
6155        }
6156      }
6157      if (oids.size() > 0) {
6158        obj.add("oids", oids);
6159      }
6160      if (urls.size() > 0) {
6161        obj.add("alt-urls", urls);
6162      }
6163      list.add(obj);
6164    }
6165    Gson gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
6166    String json = gson.toJson(list);
6167    TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "canonicals.json"), false);
6168    TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(tempDir, "canonicals.json"), false);
6169    otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, "canonicals.json"));
6170    
6171    Collections.sort(crlist, new ResourceSorters.CanonicalResourceSortByTypeId());    
6172    XhtmlNode tbl = new XhtmlNode(NodeType.Element, "table").setAttribute("class", "grid");
6173    XhtmlNode tr = tbl.tr();
6174    tr.td().b().tx("Canonical");
6175    tr.td().b().tx("Id");
6176    tr.td().b().tx("Version");
6177    tr.td().b().tx("Oids");
6178    tr.td().b().tx("Other URLS");
6179    String type = "";
6180    for (CanonicalResource cr : crlist) {
6181      CommaSeparatedStringBuilder bu = new CommaSeparatedStringBuilder(); 
6182      CommaSeparatedStringBuilder bo = new CommaSeparatedStringBuilder(); 
6183      for (Identifier id : cr.getIdentifier()) {
6184        if (id != null) {
6185          if ("urn:ietf:rfc:3986".equals(id.getSystem()) && id.hasValue()) {
6186            if (id.getValue().startsWith("urn:oid:")) {
6187              bo.append(id.getValue().substring(8));
6188            } else {
6189              bu.append(id.getValue());
6190            }
6191          }
6192        }
6193      }
6194      if (!type.equals(cr.fhirType())) {
6195        type = cr.fhirType();
6196        XhtmlNode h = tbl.tr().style("background-color: #eeeeee").td().colspan("5").h3();
6197        h.an(type);
6198        h.tx(type);
6199      }
6200      tr = tbl.tr();
6201      tr.td().ah(cr.getUserString("path")).tx(cr.getUrl());
6202      tr.td().tx(cr.getId());
6203      tr.td().tx(cr.getVersion());
6204      tr.td().tx(bo.toString());
6205      tr.td().tx(bu.toString());      
6206    }
6207    String xhtml = new XhtmlComposer(true).compose(tbl);
6208    fragment("canonical-index", xhtml, otherFilesRun);
6209  }

6211  public String license() throws Exception {
6212    if (Utilities.noString(license)) {
6213      throw new Exception("A license is required in the configuration file, and it must be a SPDX license identifier (see https://spdx.org/licenses/), or \"not-open-source\"");
6214    }
6215    return license;
6216  }

6218  public SPDXLicense licenseAsEnum() throws Exception {
6219    return SPDXLicense.fromCode(license());

6228    return null;

6241  private void applyPageTemplate(String htmlTemplate, String mdTemplate, ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent page) throws Exception {
6242    String p = page.getNameUrlType().getValue();
6243    String sourceName = null;
6244    String template = null;
6245    if (htmlTemplate != null && page.getGeneration() == GuidePageGeneration.HTML  && !relativeNames.keySet().contains(p) && p.endsWith(".html")) {
6246      sourceName = p.substring(0, p.indexOf(".html")) + ".xml";
6247      template = htmlTemplate;
6248    } else if (mdTemplate != null && page.getGeneration() == GuidePageGeneration.MARKDOWN  && !relativeNames.keySet().contains(p) && p.endsWith(".html")) {
6249      sourceName = p.substring(0, p.indexOf(".html")) + ".md";
6250      template = mdTemplate;
6251    }
6252    if (sourceName!=null) {
6253      String sourcePath = Utilities.path("_includes", sourceName);
6254      if (!relativeNames.keySet().contains(sourcePath) && !sourceName.equals("toc.xml")) {
6255        throw new Exception("Template based HTML file " + p + " is missing source file " + sourceName);
6256      }
6257      FetchedFile f = relativeNames.get(sourcePath);
6258      String s = "---\r\n---\r\n{% include " + template + "%}";
6259      String targetPath = Utilities.path(tempDir, p);
6260      TextFile.stringToFile(s, targetPath, false);
6261      if (f==null) { // toc.xml
6262        checkMakeFile(s.getBytes(), targetPath, otherFilesRun);
6263      } else {
6264        checkMakeFile(s.getBytes(), targetPath, f.getOutputNames());
6265      }
6266    }
6267
6268    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent childPage : page.getPage()) {
6269      applyPageTemplate(htmlTemplate, mdTemplate, childPage);
6270    }
6271  }
6272
6273  private String breadCrumbForPage(ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent page, boolean withLink) throws FHIRException {
6274    if (withLink) {
6275      return "<li><a href='" + page.getNameUrlType().getValue() + "'><b>" + Utilities.escapeXml(page.getTitle()) + "</b></a></li>";
6276    } else {
6277      return "<li><b>" + Utilities.escapeXml(page.getTitle()) + "</b></li>";
6278    }
6279  }
6280
6281  private void addPageData(JsonObject pages, ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent page, String label, String breadcrumb) throws FHIRException {
6282    if (!page.hasNameUrlType()) {
6283      errors.add(new ValidationMessage(Source.Publisher, IssueType.REQUIRED, "Base IG resource", "The page \""+page.getTitle()+"\" is missing a name/source element", IssueSeverity.ERROR));
6284    } else {
6285      addPageData(pages, page, page.getNameUrlType().getValue(), page.getTitle(), label, breadcrumb);
6286    }
6287  }
6288
6289  private void addPageData(JsonObject pages, ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent page, String source, String title, String label, String breadcrumb) throws FHIRException {
6290    FetchedResource r = resources.get(source);
6291    if (r==null) {
6292      addPageDataRow(pages, source, title, label + (page.hasPage() ? ".0" : ""), breadcrumb + breadCrumbForPage(page, false), null);
6293//      addPageDataRow(pages, source, title, label + (page.hasPage() ? ".0" : ""), breadcrumb + breadCrumbForPage(page, false), null);
6294    } else {
6295      Map<String, String> vars = makeVars(r);
6296      String outputName = determineOutputName(igpkp.getProperty(r, "base"), r, vars, null, "");
6297      addPageDataRow(pages, outputName, title, label, breadcrumb + breadCrumbForPage(page, false), r.getStatedExamples());
6298//      addPageDataRow(pages, source, title, label, breadcrumb + breadCrumbForPage(page, false), r.getStatedExamples());
6299      for (String templateName: extraTemplateList) {
6300        if (r.getConfig() !=null && r.getConfig().get("template-"+templateName)!=null && !r.getConfig().get("template-"+templateName).getAsString().isEmpty()) {
6301          if (templateName.equals("format")) {
6302            String templateDesc = extraTemplates.get(templateName);
6303            for (String format: template.getFormats()) {
6304              String formatTemplateDesc = templateDesc.replace("FMT", format.toUpperCase());
6305              if (igpkp.wantGen(r, format)) {
6306                outputName = determineOutputName(igpkp.getProperty(r, "format"), r, vars, format, "");
6307                addPageDataRow(pages, outputName, page.getTitle() + " - " + formatTemplateDesc, label, breadcrumb + breadCrumbForPage(page, false), null);
6308              }
6309            }
6310          } else if (page.hasGeneration() && page.getGeneration().equals(GuidePageGeneration.GENERATED) /*page.getKind().equals(ImplementationGuide.GuidePageKind.RESOURCE) */) {
6311            boolean showPage = true;
6312            if (historyTemplates.contains(templateName) && r.getAudits().isEmpty())
6313              showPage = false;
6314            if (exampleTemplates.contains(templateName) && r.getStatedExamples().isEmpty())
6315              showPage = false;
6316            if (showPage) {
6317              String templateDesc = extraTemplates.get(templateName);
6318              outputName = igpkp.getProperty(r, templateName);
6319              if (outputName==null)
6320                throw new FHIRException("Error in publisher template.  Unable to find file-path property " + templateName + " for resource type " + r.fhirType() + " when property template-" + templateName + " is defined.");
6321              outputName = igpkp.doReplacements(outputName, r, vars, "");
6322              addPageDataRow(pages, outputName, page.getTitle() + " - " + templateDesc, label, breadcrumb + breadCrumbForPage(page, false), null);
6323            }
6324          }          
6325        }
6326      }
6327    }
6328
6329    int i = 1;
6330    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent childPage : page.getPage()) {
6331      addPageData(pages, childPage, (label.equals("0") ? "" : label+".") + Integer.toString(i), breadcrumb + breadCrumbForPage(page, true));
6332      i++;
6333    }
6334  }

6337  private void addPageDataRow(JsonObject pages, String url, String title, String label, String breadcrumb, Set<FetchedResource> examples) throws FHIRException {
6338    JsonObject jsonPage = new JsonObject();
6339    pages.add(url, jsonPage);
6340    jsonPage.addProperty("title", title);
6341    jsonPage.addProperty("label", label);
6342    jsonPage.addProperty("breadcrumb", breadcrumb);
6343
6344    String baseUrl = url;
6345
6346    if (baseUrl.indexOf(".html") > 0) {
6347        baseUrl = baseUrl.substring(0, baseUrl.indexOf(".html"));
6348    }
6349
6350    for (String pagesDir: pagesDirs) {
6351      String contentFile = pagesDir + File.separator + "_includes" + File.separator + baseUrl + "-intro.xml";
6352      if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6353        jsonPage.addProperty("intro", baseUrl+"-intro.xml");
6354        jsonPage.addProperty("intro-type", "xml");
6355      } else {
6356        contentFile = pagesDir + File.separator + "_includes" + File.separator + baseUrl + "-intro.md";
6357        if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6358          jsonPage.addProperty("intro", baseUrl+"-intro.md");
6359          jsonPage.addProperty("intro-type", "md");
6360        }
6361      }
6362
6363      contentFile = pagesDir + File.separator + "_includes" + File.separator + baseUrl + "-notes.xml";
6364      if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6365        jsonPage.addProperty("notes", baseUrl+"-notes.xml");
6366        jsonPage.addProperty("notes-type", "xml");
6367      } else {
6368        contentFile = pagesDir + File.separator + "_includes" + File.separator + baseUrl + "-notes.md";
6369        if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6370          jsonPage.addProperty("notes", baseUrl+"-notes.md");
6371          jsonPage.addProperty("notes-type", "md");
6372        }
6373      }
6374    }
6375
6376    for (String prePagesDir: prePagesDirs) {
6377      PreProcessInfo ppinfo = preProcessInfo.get(prePagesDir);
6378      String baseFile = prePagesDir + File.separator;
6379      if (ppinfo.relativePath.equals("")) {
6380        baseFile = baseFile + "_includes" + File.separator;
6381      } else if (!ppinfo.relativePath.equals("_includes")) {
6382        continue;
6383      }
6384      baseFile = baseFile + baseUrl;
6385      String contentFile = baseFile + "-intro.xml";
6386      if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6387        jsonPage.addProperty("intro", baseUrl+"-intro.xml");
6388        jsonPage.addProperty("intro-type", "xml");
6389      } else {
6390        contentFile = baseFile + "-intro.md";
6391        if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6392          jsonPage.addProperty("intro", baseUrl+"-intro.md");
6393          jsonPage.addProperty("intro-type", "md");
6394        }
6395      }
6396  
6397      contentFile = baseFile + "-notes.xml";
6398      if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6399        jsonPage.addProperty("notes", baseUrl+"-notes.xml");
6400        jsonPage.addProperty("notes-type", "xml");
6401      } else {
6402        contentFile = baseFile + "-notes.md";
6403        if (new File(contentFile).exists()) {
6404          jsonPage.addProperty("notes", baseUrl+"-notes.md");
6405          jsonPage.addProperty("notes-type", "md");
6406        }        
6407      }
6408    }
6409    
6410    if (examples != null) {
6411      JsonArray exampleArray = new JsonArray();
6412      jsonPage.add("examples", exampleArray);
6413
6414      TreeSet<ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent> examplePages = new TreeSet<ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent>(new ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponentComparator());
6415      for (FetchedResource exampleResource: examples) {
6416        ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent page = pageForFetchedResource(exampleResource);
6417        if (page!=null)
6418          examplePages.add(page);
6419        // else
6420        //   throw new Error("Unable to find page for resource "+ exampleResource.getId());
6421      }
6422      for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent examplePage : examplePages) {
6423        JsonObject exampleItem = new JsonObject();
6424        exampleArray.add(exampleItem);
6425        exampleItem.addProperty("url", examplePage.getNameUrlType().getValue());
6426        exampleItem.addProperty("title", examplePage.getTitle());
6427      }
6428    }
6429  }

6432  private void createToc() throws IOException, FHIRException {
6433    createToc(null, null, null);
6434  }
6435  
6436  private void createToc(ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent insertPage, String insertAfterName, String insertOffset) throws IOException, FHIRException {
6437    String s = "<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?><div style=\"col-12\"><table style=\"border:0px;font-size:11px;font-family:verdana;vertical-align:top;\" cellpadding=\"0\" border=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\"><tbody>";
6438    s = s + createTocPage(publishedIg.getDefinition().getPage(), insertPage, insertAfterName, insertOffset, null, "", "0", false);
6439    s = s + "</tbody></table></div>";
6440    TextFile.stringToFile(s, Utilities.path(tempDir, "_includes", "toc.xml"), false);
6441  }
6442
6443  private String createTocPage(ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent page, ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent insertPage, String insertAfterName, String insertOffset, String currentOffset, String indents, String label, boolean last) throws FHIRException {
6444    String s = "<tr style=\"border:0px;padding:0px;vertical-align:top;background-color:white;\">";
6445    s = s + "<td style=\"vertical-align:top;text-align:left;background-color:white;padding:0px 4px 0px 4px;white-space:nowrap;background-image:url(tbl_bck0.png)\" class=\"hierarchy\">";
6446    s = s + "<img style=\"background-color:inherit\" alt=\".\" class=\"hierarchy\" src=\"tbl_spacer.png\"/>";
6447    s = s + indents;
6448    if (!label.equals("0")) {
6449      if (last)
6450        s = s + "<img style=\"background-color:inherit\" alt=\".\" class=\"hierarchy\" src=\"tbl_vjoin_end.png\"/>";
6451      else
6452        s = s + "<img style=\"background-color:inherit\" alt=\".\" class=\"hierarchy\" src=\"tbl_vjoin.png\"/>";
6453    }
6454    s = s + "<img style=\"background-color:white;background-color:inherit\" alt=\".\" class=\"hierarchy\" src=\"icon_page.gif\"/>";
6455    s = s + "<a title=\"" + Utilities.escapeXml(page.getTitle()) + "\" href=\"" + (currentOffset!=null ? currentOffset + "/" : "") + (page.hasNameUrlType() ? page.getNameUrlType().getValue() : "?name?") +"\">" + label + " " + Utilities.escapeXml(page.getTitle()) + "</a></td></tr>";
6456
6457    int total = page.getPage().size();
6458    int i = 1;
6459    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent childPage : page.getPage()) {
6460      String newIndents = indents;
6461      if (!label.equals("0")) {
6462        if (last)
6463          newIndents = newIndents + "<img style=\"background-color:inherit\" alt=\".\" class=\"hierarchy\" src=\"tbl_blank.png\"/>";
6464        else
6465          newIndents = newIndents + "<img style=\"background-color:inherit\" alt=\".\" class=\"hierarchy\" src=\"tbl_vline.png\"/>";
6466      }
6467      if (insertAfterName!=null && childPage.getNameUrlType().getValue().equals(insertAfterName)) {
6468        total++;
6469      }
6470      
6471      s = s + createTocPage(childPage, insertPage, insertAfterName, insertOffset, currentOffset, newIndents, (label.equals("0") ? "" : label+".") + Integer.toString(i), i==total);
6472      i++;
6473      if (insertAfterName!=null && childPage.getNameUrlType().getValue().equals(insertAfterName)) {
6474        s = s + createTocPage(insertPage, null, null, "", insertOffset, newIndents, (label.equals("0") ? "" : label+".") + Integer.toString(i), i==total);
6475        i++;
6476      }
6477    }
6478    return s;
6479  }
6480
6481  private ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent pageForFetchedResource(FetchedResource r) throws FHIRException {
6482    String key = igpkp.doReplacements(igpkp.getLinkFor(r, false), r, null, null);
6483    return igPages.get(key);
6484  }

6486  private class ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponentComparator implements Comparator<ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent> {
6487    @Override
6488    public int compare(ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent x, ImplementationGuideDefinitionPageComponent y) {
6489      try {
6490        return x.getNameUrlType().getValue().compareTo(y.getNameUrlType().getValue());
6491      } catch (FHIRException e) {
6492        // TODO Auto-generated catch block
6493        e.printStackTrace();
6494        return 0;
6495      }
6496    }
6497  }

6499  private void generateDataFile() throws IOException, FHIRException {
6500    JsonObject data = new JsonObject();
6501    data.addProperty("path", checkAppendSlash(specPath));
6502    data.addProperty("canonical", igpkp.getCanonical());
6503    data.addProperty("igId", publishedIg.getId());
6504    data.addProperty("igName", publishedIg.getName());
6505    data.addProperty("packageId", npmName);
6506    data.addProperty("igVer", workingVersion());
6507    data.addProperty("errorCount", getErrorCount());
6508    data.addProperty("version", version);
6509    data.addProperty("revision", specMaps.get(0).getBuild());
6510    data.addProperty("versionFull", version+"-"+specMaps.get(0).getBuild());
6511    data.addProperty("toolingVersion", Constants.VERSION);
6512    data.addProperty("toolingRevision", ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION_STR);
6513    data.addProperty("toolingVersionFull", Constants.VERSION+" ("+ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION_STR+")");
6514    data.addProperty("totalFiles", fileList.size());
6515    data.addProperty("processedFiles", changeList.size());
6516    data.addProperty("genDate", genTime());
6517    data.addProperty("genDay", genDate());
6518    JsonObject ig = new JsonObject();
6519    data.add("ig", ig);
6520    ig.addProperty("id", publishedIg.getId());
6521    ig.addProperty("name", publishedIg.getName());
6522    ig.addProperty("title", publishedIg.getTitle());
6523    ig.addProperty("url", publishedIg.getUrl());
6524    ig.addProperty("version", workingVersion());
6525    ig.addProperty("status", publishedIg.getStatusElement().asStringValue());
6526    ig.addProperty("experimental", publishedIg.getExperimental());
6527    ig.addProperty("publisher", publishedIg.getPublisher());
6528    ig.addProperty("gitstatus", getGitStatus());
6529    if (previousVersionComparator != null && previousVersionComparator.hasLast() && !targetUrl().startsWith("file:")) {
6530      JsonObject diff = new JsonObject();
6531      data.add("diff", diff);
6532      diff.addProperty("name", Utilities.encodeUri(previousVersionComparator.getLastName()));
6533      diff.addProperty("current", Utilities.encodeUri(targetUrl()));
6534      diff.addProperty("previous", Utilities.encodeUri(previousVersionComparator.getLastUrl()));
6535    }
6536    
6537    if (publishedIg.hasContact()) {
6538      JsonArray jc = new JsonArray();
6539      ig.add("contact", jc);
6540      for (ContactDetail c : publishedIg.getContact()) {
6541        JsonObject jco = new JsonObject();
6542        jc.add(jco);
6543        jco.addProperty("name", c.getName());
6544        if (c.hasTelecom()) {
6545          JsonArray jct = new JsonArray();
6546          jco.add("telecom", jct);
6547          for (ContactPoint cc : c.getTelecom()) {
6548            jct.add(new JsonPrimitive(cc.getValue()));
6549          }
6550        }
6551      }
6552    }
6553    ig.addProperty("date", publishedIg.getDateElement().asStringValue());
6554    ig.addProperty("description", publishedIg.getDescription());
6555    ig.addProperty("copyright", publishedIg.getCopyright());
6556    for (Enumeration<FHIRVersion> v : publishedIg.getFhirVersion()) {
6557      ig.addProperty("fhirVersion", v.asStringValue());
6558      break;
6559    }
6560
6561    for (SpecMapManager sm : specMaps) {
6562      if (sm.getName() != null) {
6563        data.addProperty(sm.getName(), appendTrailingSlashInDataFile ? sm.getBase() : Utilities.appendForwardSlash(sm.getBase()));
6564        if (!data.has("ver")) {
6565          data.add("ver", new JsonObject());
6566        }
6567        data.getAsJsonObject("ver").addProperty(sm.getName(), appendTrailingSlashInDataFile ? sm.getBase2() : Utilities.appendForwardSlash(sm.getBase2()));
6568      }
6569    }
6570    Gson gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
6571    String json = gson.toJson(data);
6572    TextFile.stringToFile(json, Utilities.path(tempDir, "_data", "fhir.json"), false);
6573  }
6574
6575  public String workingVersion() {
6576    return businessVersion == null ? publishedIg.getVersion() : businessVersion;
6577  }
6578
6579  private String getGitStatus() throws IOException {
6580    File gitDir = new File(Utilities.path(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(configFile), ".git"));
6581    if (!gitDir.exists()) {
6582      return "";      
6583    }
6584    String head = TextFile.fileToString(Utilities.path(gitDir.getAbsolutePath(), "HEAD")).trim();
6585    return head.substring(head.lastIndexOf("/")+1);
6586  }
6587
6588  private void generateResourceReferences() throws Exception {
6589    Set<String> resourceTypes = new HashSet<>();
6590    for (StructureDefinition sd : context.allStructures()) {
6591      if (sd.getDerivation() == TypeDerivationRule.SPECIALIZATION && sd.getKind() == StructureDefinitionKind.RESOURCE) {
6592        resourceTypes.add(sd.getType());
6593      }
6594    }
6595    for (String rt : resourceTypes) {
6596      generateResourceReferences(rt);
6597    }
6598    generateProfiles();
6599    generateExtensions();
6600    generateLogicals();
6601  }

6603  private class Item {
6604    public Item(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, String sort) {
6605      this.f= f;
6606      this.r = r;
6607      this.sort = sort;
6608    }
6609    public Item() {
6610      // TODO Auto-generated constructor stub
6611    }
6612    private String sort;
6613    private FetchedFile f;
6614    private FetchedResource r;
6615  }
6616  private class ItemSorter implements Comparator<Item> {
6617
6618    @Override
6619    public int compare(Item a0, Item a1) {
6620      return a0.sort.compareTo(a1.sort);
6621    }
6622  }
6623
6624  private void generateProfiles() throws Exception {
6625    List<Item> items = new ArrayList<Item>();
6626    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6627      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6628        if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition")) {
6629          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
6630          if (sd.getDerivation() == TypeDerivationRule.CONSTRAINT && sd.getKind() == StructureDefinitionKind.RESOURCE) {
6631            items.add(new Item(f, r, sd.hasTitle() ? sd.getTitle() : sd.hasName() ? sd.getName() : r.getTitle()));
6632          }
6633        }
6634      }
6635    }
6636    if (items.size() > 0) {
6637      Collections.sort(items, new ItemSorter());
6638      StringBuilder list = new StringBuilder();
6639      StringBuilder lists = new StringBuilder();
6640      StringBuilder table = new StringBuilder();
6641      StringBuilder listMM = new StringBuilder();
6642      StringBuilder listsMM = new StringBuilder();
6643      StringBuilder tableMM = new StringBuilder();
6644      for (Item i : items) {
6645        StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) i.r.getResource();
6646        genEntryItem(list, lists, table, listMM, listsMM, tableMM, i.f, i.r, i.sort, null);
6647      }
6648      fragment("list-profiles", list.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6649      fragment("list-simple-profiles", lists.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6650      fragment("table-profiles", table.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6651      fragment("list-profiles-mm", listMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6652      fragment("list-simple-profiles-mm", listsMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6653      fragment("table-profiles-mm", tableMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6654    }
6655  }
6656
6657  private void generateExtensions() throws Exception {
6658    List<Item> items = new ArrayList<Item>();
6659    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6660      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6661        if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition")) {
6662          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
6663          if (sd.getDerivation() == TypeDerivationRule.CONSTRAINT && sd.getType().equals("Extension")) {
6664            items.add(new Item(f, r, sd.hasTitle() ? sd.getTitle() : sd.hasName() ? sd.getName() : r.getTitle()));
6665          }
6666        }
6667      }
6668    }
6669
6670    StringBuilder list = new StringBuilder();
6671    StringBuilder lists = new StringBuilder();
6672    StringBuilder table = new StringBuilder();
6673    StringBuilder listMM = new StringBuilder();
6674    StringBuilder listsMM = new StringBuilder();
6675    StringBuilder tableMM = new StringBuilder();
6676    for (Item i : items) {
6677      StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) i.r.getResource();
6678      genEntryItem(list, lists, table, listMM, listsMM, tableMM, i.f, i.r, i.sort, null);
6679    }
6680    fragment("list-extensions", list.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6681    fragment("list-simple-extensions", lists.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6682    fragment("table-extensions", table.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6683    fragment("list-extensions-mm", listMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6684    fragment("list-simple-extensions-mm", listsMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6685    fragment("table-extensions-mm", tableMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6686  }

6688  private void generateLogicals() throws Exception {
6689    List<Item> items = new ArrayList<Item>();
6690    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6691      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6692        if (r.fhirType().equals("StructureDefinition")) {
6693          StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
6694          if (sd.getKind() == StructureDefinitionKind.LOGICAL) {
6695            items.add(new Item(f, r, sd.hasTitle() ? sd.getTitle() : sd.hasName() ? sd.getName() : r.getTitle()));
6696          }
6697        }
6698      }
6699    }
6700
6701    StringBuilder list = new StringBuilder();
6702    StringBuilder lists = new StringBuilder();
6703    StringBuilder table = new StringBuilder();
6704    StringBuilder listMM = new StringBuilder();
6705    StringBuilder listsMM = new StringBuilder();
6706    StringBuilder tableMM = new StringBuilder();
6707    for (Item i : items) {
6708      StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) i.r.getResource();
6709      genEntryItem(list, lists, table, listMM, listsMM, tableMM, i.f, i.r, i.sort, null);
6710    }
6711    fragment("list-logicals", list.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6712    fragment("list-simple-logicals", lists.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6713    fragment("table-logicals", table.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6714    fragment("list-logicals-mm", listMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6715    fragment("list-simple-logicals-mm", listsMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6716    fragment("table-logicals-mm", tableMM.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6717  }
6718
6719  private void genEntryItem(StringBuilder list, StringBuilder lists, StringBuilder table, StringBuilder listMM, StringBuilder listsMM, StringBuilder tableMM, FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, String name, String prefixType) throws Exception {
6720    String ref = igpkp.doReplacements(igpkp.getLinkFor(r, false), r, null, null);
6721    if (Utilities.noString(ref))
6722      throw new Exception("No reference found for "+r.getId());
6723    if (prefixType != null)
6724      if (ref.contains("."))
6725        ref = ref.substring(0, ref.lastIndexOf("."))+"."+prefixType+ref.substring(ref.lastIndexOf("."));
6726      else
6727        ref = ref+"."+prefixType;
6728    String desc = r.getTitle();
6729    String descSrc = "Resource Title";
6730    if (!r.hasTitle()) {
6731      desc = f.getTitle();
6732      descSrc = "File Title";
6733    }
6734    if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
6735      name = ((CanonicalResource) r.getResource()).present();
6736      String d = getDesc((CanonicalResource) r.getResource());
6737      if (d != null) {
6738        desc = markdownEngine.process(d, descSrc);
6739        descSrc = "Canonical Resource";
6740      }
6741    } else if (r.getElement() != null && r.getElement().hasChild("description")) {
6742      String d = new StringType(r.getElement().getChildValue("description")).asStringValue();
6743      if (d != null) {
6744        desc = markdownEngine.process(d, descSrc);
6745        // new BaseRenderer(context, null, igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, rc).processMarkdown("description", desc )
6746        descSrc = "Canonical Resource Source";
6747      }
6748    }
6749    list.append(" <li><a href=\""+ref+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(name)+"</a> "+desc+"</li>\r\n");
6750    lists.append(" <li><a href=\""+ref+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(name)+"</a></li>\r\n");
6751    table.append(" <tr><td><a href=\""+ref+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(name)+"</a> </td><td>"+desc+"</td></tr>\r\n");
6752    
6753    if (listMM != null) {
6754      String mm = "";
6755      if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource) {
6756        String fmm = ToolingExtensions.readStringExtension((DomainResource) r.getResource(), ToolingExtensions.EXT_FMM_LEVEL);
6757        if (fmm != null) {
6758          // Use hard-coded spec link to point to current spec because DSTU2 had maturity listed on a different page
6759          mm = " <a class=\"fmm\" href=\"http://hl7.org/fhir/versions.html#maturity\" title=\"Maturity Level\">"+fmm+"</a>";
6760        }
6761      }
6762      listMM.append(" <li><a href=\""+ref+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(name)+"</a>"+mm+" "+desc+"</li>\r\n");
6763      listsMM.append(" <li><a href=\""+ref+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(name)+"</a>"+mm+"</li>\r\n");
6764      tableMM.append(" <tr><td><a href=\""+ref+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(name)+"</a> </td><td>"+desc+"</td><td>"+mm+"</td></tr>\r\n");
6765    }
6766  }
6767
6768  private void generateResourceReferences(String rt) throws Exception {
6769    List<Item> items = new ArrayList<Item>();
6770    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6771      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6772        if (r.fhirType().equals(rt)) {
6773            if (r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
6774              CanonicalResource md = (CanonicalResource) r.getResource();
6775              items.add(new Item(f, r, md.hasTitle() ? md.getTitle() : md.hasName() ? md.getName() : r.getTitle()));
6776            } else
6777              items.add(new Item(f, r, Utilities.noString(r.getTitle()) ? r.getId() : r.getTitle()));
6778        }
6779      }
6780    }
6781
6782    genResourceReferencesList(rt, items, "");
6783    Collections.sort(items, new ItemSorterById());
6784    genResourceReferencesList(rt, items, "byid-");
6785    Collections.sort(items, new ItemSorterByName());
6786    genResourceReferencesList(rt, items, "name-");
6787  }

6789
6790  public class ItemSorterById implements Comparator<Item> {
6791    @Override
6792    public int compare(Item arg0, Item arg1) {
6793      String l = arg0.r == null ? null : arg0.r.getId();
6794      String r = arg1.r == null ? null : arg1.r.getId();
6795      return l == null ? 0 : l.compareTo(r);
6796    }
6797  }
6798
6799  public class ItemSorterByName implements Comparator<Item> {
6800    @Override
6801    public int compare(Item arg0, Item arg1) {
6802      String l = arg0.r == null ? null : arg0.r.getTitle();
6803      String r = arg1.r == null ? null : arg1.r.getTitle();
6804      return l == null ? 0 : l.compareTo(r);
6805    }
6806  }
6807
6808  public void genResourceReferencesList(String rt, List<Item> items, String ext) throws Exception, IOException {
6809    StringBuilder list = new StringBuilder();
6810    StringBuilder lists = new StringBuilder();
6811    StringBuilder table = new StringBuilder();
6812    StringBuilder listMM = new StringBuilder();
6813    StringBuilder listsMM = new StringBuilder();
6814    StringBuilder tableMM = new StringBuilder();
6815    StringBuilder listJ = new StringBuilder();
6816    StringBuilder listsJ = new StringBuilder();
6817    StringBuilder tableJ = new StringBuilder();
6818    StringBuilder listX = new StringBuilder();
6819    StringBuilder listsX = new StringBuilder();
6820    StringBuilder tableX = new StringBuilder();
6821    if (items.size() > 0) {
6822      for (Item i : items) {
6823        String name = i.r.getTitle();
6824        if (Utilities.noString(name))
6825          name = rt;
6826        genEntryItem(list, lists, table, listMM, listsMM, tableMM, i.f, i.r, i.sort, null);
6827        genEntryItem(listJ, listsJ, tableJ, null, null, null, i.f, i.r, i.sort, "json");
6828        genEntryItem(listX, listsX, tableX, null, null, null, i.f, i.r, i.sort, "xml");
6829      }
6830    }
6831    String pm = Utilities.pluralizeMe(rt.toLowerCase());
6832    fragment("list-"+ext+pm, list.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6833    fragment("list-simple-"+ext+pm, lists.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6834    fragment("table-"+ext+pm, table.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6835    fragment("list-"+ext+pm+"-json", listJ.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6836    fragment("list-simple-"+ext+pm+"-json", listsJ.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6837    fragment("table-"+ext+pm+"-json", tableJ.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6838    fragment("list-"+ext+pm+"-xml", listX.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6839    fragment("list-simple-"+ext+pm+"-xml", listsX.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6840    fragment("table-"+ext+pm+"-xml", tableX.toString(), otherFilesRun);
6841  }

6843  @SuppressWarnings("rawtypes")
6844  private String getDesc(CanonicalResource r) {
6845    if (r.hasDescriptionElement()) {
6846      return r.getDescriptionElement().asStringValue();
6847    }
6848    return null;
6849  }

6851  private Number getErrorCount() {
6852    int result = countErrs(errors);
6853    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
6854      result = result + countErrs(f.getErrors());
6855    }
6856    return result;
6857  }
6858
6859  private int countErrs(List<ValidationMessage> list) {
6860    int i = 0;
6861    for (ValidationMessage vm : list) {
6862      if (vm.getLevel() == IssueSeverity.ERROR || vm.getLevel() == IssueSeverity.FATAL)
6863        i++;
6864    }
6865    return i;
6866  }

6868  private void log(String s) {
6869    logger.logMessage(s);
6870  }

6872  private void generateNativeOutputs(FetchedFile f, boolean regen) throws IOException, FHIRException {
6873    for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6874        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Produce resources for "+r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());
6875        saveNativeResourceOutputs(f, r);
6876    }    
6877  }
6878  private void generateHtmlOutputs(FetchedFile f, boolean regen) throws Exception {
6879    if (noGenerate) {
6880      return;
6881    }
6882    
6883    if (f.getProcessMode() == FetchedFile.PROCESS_NONE) {
6884      String dst = tempDir;
6885      if (f.getRelativePath().startsWith(File.separator))
6886        dst = dst + f.getRelativePath();
6887      else
6888        dst = dst + File.separator + f.getRelativePath();
6889      try {
6890        if (f.isFolder()) {
6891          f.getOutputNames().add(dst);
6892          Utilities.createDirectory(dst);
6893        } else
6894          checkMakeFile(f.getSource(), dst, f.getOutputNames());
6895      } catch (IOException e) {
6896        log("Exception generating page "+dst+" for "+f.getRelativePath()+" in "+tempDir+": "+e.getMessage());
6897         
6898      }
6899    } else if (f.getProcessMode() == FetchedFile.PROCESS_XSLT) {
6900//      String dst = tempDir + f.getPath().substring(prePagesDir.length());
6901      String dst = tempDir;
6902      if (f.getRelativePath().startsWith(File.separator))
6903        dst = dst + f.getRelativePath();
6904      else
6905        dst = dst + File.separator + f.getRelativePath();
6906      try {
6907        if (f.isFolder()) {
6908          f.getOutputNames().add(dst);
6909          Utilities.createDirectory(dst);
6910        } else
6911          checkMakeFile(transform(f.getSource(), f.getXslt()), dst, f.getOutputNames());
6912      } catch (Exception e) {
6913        log("Exception generating xslt page "+dst+" for "+f.getRelativePath()+" in "+tempDir+": "+e.getMessage());
6914      }
6915    } else {
6916      saveFileOutputs(f);
6917      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
6918        logDebugMessage(LogCategory.PROGRESS, "Produce outputs for "+r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId());
6919        Map<String, String> vars = makeVars(r);
6920        makeTemplates(f, r, vars);
6921        saveDirectResourceOutputs(f, r, r.getResource(), vars);
6922        if (r.getResource() != null) {
6923          generateResourceHtml(f, regen, r, r.getResource(), vars, "");
6924          if (r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
6925            CanonicalResource container = (CanonicalResource) r.getResource();
6926            for (Resource contained : container.getContained()) {              
6927              String prefixForContained = r.getResource().getId()+"_";
6928              makeTemplatesContained(f, r, contained, vars, prefixForContained);
6929              saveDirectResourceOutputsContained(f, r, contained, vars, prefixForContained);
6930              if (contained instanceof CanonicalResource) {
6931                CanonicalResource cr = ((CanonicalResource) contained).copy();
6932                cr.copyUserData(container);
6933                if (!cr.hasUrl()) {
6934                  cr.setUrl(container.getUrl()+"#"+contained.getId());
6935                }
6936                if (!cr.hasVersion()) {
6937                  cr.setVersion(container.getVersion());
6938                }
6939                generateResourceHtml(f, regen, r, cr, vars, prefixForContained);                  
6940              } else {
6941                generateResourceHtml(f, regen, r, contained, vars, prefixForContained);                
6942              }
6943            }
6944          }
6945        } else {
6946          if ("QuestionnaireResponse".equals(r.fhirType())) {
6947            String prefixForContained = "";
6948            generateOutputsQuestionnaireResponse(f, r, vars, prefixForContained);
6949          }
6950        }
6951      }
6952    }
6953  }
6954
6955  public boolean generateResourceHtml(FetchedFile f, boolean regen, FetchedResource r, Resource res, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContainer) {
6956    boolean result = true;
6957    try {
6958
6959      // now, start generating resource type specific stuff
6960      switch (res.getResourceType()) {
6961      case CodeSystem:
6962        generateOutputsCodeSystem(f, r, (CodeSystem) res, vars, prefixForContainer);
6963        break;
6964      case ValueSet:
6965        generateOutputsValueSet(f, r, (ValueSet) res, vars, prefixForContainer);
6966        break;
6967      case ConceptMap:
6968        generateOutputsConceptMap(f, r, (ConceptMap) res, vars, prefixForContainer);
6969        break;
6970
6971      case List:
6972        generateOutputsList(f, r, (ListResource) res, vars, prefixForContainer);      
6973        break;
6974        
6975      case CapabilityStatement:
6976        generateOutputsCapabilityStatement(f, r, (CapabilityStatement) res, vars, prefixForContainer);
6977        break;
6978      case StructureDefinition:
6979        generateOutputsStructureDefinition(f, r, (StructureDefinition) res, vars, regen, prefixForContainer);
6980        break;
6981      case OperationDefinition:
6982        generateOutputsOperationDefinition(f, r, (OperationDefinition) res, vars, regen, prefixForContainer);
6983        break;
6984      case StructureMap:
6985        generateOutputsStructureMap(f, r, (StructureMap) res, vars, prefixForContainer);
6986        break;
6987      case Questionnaire:
6988        generateOutputsQuestionnaire(f, r, (Questionnaire) res, vars, prefixForContainer);
6989        break;
6990      case Library:
6991        generateOutputsLibrary(f, r, (Library) res, vars, prefixForContainer);
6992        break;
6993      default:
6994        if (res instanceof CanonicalResource) {
6995          generateOutputsCanonical(f, r, (CanonicalResource) res, vars, prefixForContainer);          
6996        }
6997        // nothing to do...
6998        result = false;
6999      }
7000    } catch (Exception e) {
7001      log("Exception generating resource "+f.getName()+"::"+r.fhirType()+"/"+r.getId()+(!Utilities.noString(prefixForContainer) ? "#"+res.getId() : "")+": "+e.getMessage());
7002      e.printStackTrace();
7003      for (StackTraceElement m : e.getStackTrace()) {
7004          log("   "+m.toString());
7005      }
7006    }
7007    return result;
7008  }
7009
7010
7011  private void generateOutputsOperationDefinition(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, OperationDefinition od, Map<String, String> vars, boolean regen, String prefixForContainer) throws FHIRException, IOException {
7012    OperationDefinitionRenderer odr = new OperationDefinitionRenderer(context, checkAppendSlash(specPath), od, Utilities.path(tempDir), igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, fileList, rc);
7013    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary")) {
7014      fragment("OperationDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+od.getId()+"-summary", odr.summary(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7015    }
7016    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary-table")) {
7017      fragment("OperationDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+od.getId()+"-summary-table", odr.summary(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7018    }
7019    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "idempotence")) {
7020      fragment("OperationDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+od.getId()+"-idempotence", odr.idempotence(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7021    }
7022  }

7024  public class ListItemEntry {
7025
7026    private String id;
7027    private String link;
7028    private String name;
7029    private String desc;
7030    private String type;
7031    private Element element;
7032
7033    public ListItemEntry(String type, String id, String link, String name, String desc, Element element) {
7034      super();
7035      this.type = type;
7036      this.id = id;
7037      this.link = link;
7038      this.name = name;
7039      this.desc = desc;
7040      this.element = element;
7041    }
7042
7043    public String getId() {
7044      return id;
7045    }
7046
7047    public String getLink() {
7048      return link;
7049    }
7050
7051    public String getName() {
7052      return name;
7053    }
7054
7055    public String getDesc() {
7056      return desc;
7057    }
7058
7059    public String getType() {
7060      return type;
7061    }
7062    
7063  }
7064
7065  public class ListViewSorterById implements Comparator<ListItemEntry> {
7066    @Override
7067    public int compare(ListItemEntry arg0, ListItemEntry arg1) {
7068      return arg0.getId().compareTo(arg1.getId());
7069    }
7070  }
7071
7072  public class ListViewSorterByName implements Comparator<ListItemEntry> {
7073    @Override
7074    public int compare(ListItemEntry arg0, ListItemEntry arg1) {
7075      return arg0.getName().toLowerCase().compareTo(arg1.getName().toLowerCase());
7076    }
7077  }
7078
7079
7080  private void generateOutputsList(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, ListResource resource, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws IOException, FHIRException {
7081    // we have 4 kinds of outputs:
7082    //  * list: a series of <li><a href="{{link}}">{{name}}</a> {{desc}}</li>
7083    //  * list-simple: a series of <li><a href="{{link}}">{{name}}]</a></li>
7084    //  * table: a series of <tr><td><a href="{{link}}">{{name}}]</a></td><td>{{desc}}</td></tr>
7085    //  * scripted: in format as provided by config, using liquid variables {{link}}, {{name}}, {{desc}} as desired
7086    // not all resources have a description. Name might be generated
7087    //
7088    // each list is produced 3 times: 
7089    //  * in order provided by the list
7090    //  * in alphabetical order by link
7091    //  * in allhpbetical order by name
7092    // and if there is more than one resource type in the list, 
7093    
7094    List<ListItemEntry> list = new ArrayList<>();
7095    
7096    for (ListResourceEntryComponent li : resource.getEntry()) {
7097      if (!li.getDeleted() && li.hasItem() && li.getItem().hasReference()) {
7098        String ref = li.getItem().getReference();
7099        FetchedResource lr = getResourceForUri(f, ref);
7100        if (lr == null)
7101          lr = getResourceForRef(f, ref);
7102        if (lr != null) {
7103          list.add(new ListItemEntry(lr.fhirType(), getListId(lr), getListLink(lr), getListName(lr), getListDesc(lr), lr.getElement()));          
7104        } else {
7105          // ok, we'll see if we can resolve it from another spec 
7106          Resource l = context.fetchResource(null, ref);
7107          if (l== null && ref.matches(Constants.LOCAL_REF_REGEX)) {
7108            String[] p = ref.split("\\/");
7109            l = context.fetchResourceById(p[0], p[1]);
7110          }
7111          if (l != null)
7112            list.add(new ListItemEntry(l.fhirType(), getListId(l), getListLink(l), getListName(l), getListDesc(l), null));          
7113        }
7114      }
7115    }
7116    String script = igpkp.getProperty(r, "list-script");
7117    String types = igpkp.getProperty(r, "list-types"); 
7118    genListViews(f, r, resource, list, script, "no", null);
7119    if (types != null) {
7120      for (String t : types.split("\\|")) {
7121        genListViews(f, r, resource, list, script, "no", t.trim());
7122      }
7123    }
7124    Collections.sort(list, new ListViewSorterById());
7125    genListViews(f, r, resource, list, script, "id", null);
7126    if (types != null) {
7127      for (String t : types.split("\\|")) {
7128        genListViews(f, r, resource, list, script, "id", t.trim());
7129      }
7130    }
7131    Collections.sort(list, new ListViewSorterByName());
7132    genListViews(f, r, resource, list, script, "name", null);
7133    if (types != null) {
7134      for (String t : types.split("\\|")) {
7135        genListViews(f, r, resource, list, script, "name", t.trim());
7136      }
7137    }
7138    
7139    // now, if the list has a package-id extension, generate the package for the list
7140    if (resource.hasExtension(ToolingExtensions.EXT_LIST_PACKAGE)) {
7141      Extension ext = resource.getExtensionByUrl(ToolingExtensions.EXT_LIST_PACKAGE);
7142      String id = ToolingExtensions.readStringExtension(ext, "id");
7143      String name = ToolingExtensions.readStringExtension(ext, "name");
7144      String dfn = Utilities.path(tempDir, id+".tgz");
7145      NPMPackageGenerator gen = NPMPackageGenerator.subset(npm, dfn, id, name, execTime.getTime(), !publishing);
7146      for (ListItemEntry i : list) {
7147        if (i.element != null) {
7148          ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
7149          new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context).compose(i.element, bs, OutputStyle.NORMAL, igpkp.getCanonical());
7150          gen.addFile(Category.RESOURCE, i.element.fhirType()+"-"+i.element.getIdBase()+".json", bs.toByteArray());
7151        }
7152      }
7153      gen.finish();
7154      otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, id+".tgz"));
7155    }
7156    
7157  }
7158
7159
7160  public void genListViews(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, ListResource resource, List<ListItemEntry> list, String script, String id, String type) throws IOException, FHIRException {
7161    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "list-list"))
7162      fragmentIfNN("List-"+resource.getId()+"-list-"+id+(type == null ? "" : "-"+type), genListView(list, "<li><a href=\"{{link}}\">{{name}}</a> {{desc}}</li>\r\n", type), f.getOutputNames());
7163    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "list-list-simple"))
7164      fragmentIfNN("List-"+resource.getId()+"-list-"+id+"-simple"+(type == null ? "" : "-"+type), genListView(list, "<li><a href=\"{{link}}\">{{name}}</a></li>\r\n", type), f.getOutputNames());
7165    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "list-list-table"))
7166      fragmentIfNN("List-"+resource.getId()+"-list-"+id+"-table"+(type == null ? "" : "-"+type), genListView(list, "<tr><td><a href=\"{{link}}\">{{name}}</a></td><td>{{desc}}</td></tr>\r\n", type), f.getOutputNames());
7167    if (script != null)
7168      fragmentIfNN("List-"+resource.getId()+"-list-"+id+"-script"+(type == null ? "" : "-"+type), genListView(list, script, type), f.getOutputNames());
7169  }
7170
7171  private String genListView(List<ListItemEntry> list, String template, String type) {
7172    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
7173    for (ListItemEntry i : list) {
7174      if (type == null || type.equals(i.getType())) {
7175        String s = template;
7176        if (s.contains("{{link}}")) {
7177          s = s.replace("{{link}}", i.getLink());
7178        }
7179        if (s.contains("{{name}}"))
7180          s = s.replace("{{name}}", i.getName());
7181        if (s.contains("{{desc}}"))
7182          s = s.replace("{{desc}}", i.getDesc() == null ? "" : trimPara(markdownEngine.process(i.getDesc(), "List reference description")));
7183        b.append(s);
7184      }
7185    }
7186    return b.toString();
7187  }
7188
7189  private String trimPara(String output) {
7190    if (output.startsWith("<p>") && output.endsWith("</p>\n") && !output.substring(3).contains("<p>"))
7191      return output.substring(0, output.length()-5).substring(3);
7192    else
7193      return output;
7194  }

7201  private String getListLink(FetchedResource lr) {

7204      res = lr.getResource().getUserString("path");
7205    else
7206      res = igpkp.getLinkFor(lr, true);
7207    return res;
7208  }

7210  private String getListName(FetchedResource lr) {

7214      return lr.getResource().fhirType()+"/"+lr.getResource().getId();
7215    }
7216    else {
7217      // well, as a non-metadata resource, we don't really have a name. We'll use the link
7218      return getListLink(lr);
7219    }
7220  }

7252  private byte[] transform(byte[] source, byte[] xslt) throws TransformerException {
7253    TransformerFactory f = TransformerFactory.newInstance();
7254    StreamSource xsrc = new StreamSource(new ByteArrayInputStream(xslt));
7255    Transformer t = f.newTransformer(xsrc);
7256
7257    StreamSource src = new StreamSource(new ByteArrayInputStream(source));
7258    ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
7259    StreamResult res = new StreamResult(out);
7260    t.transform(src, res);
7261    return out.toByteArray();
7262  }
7263
7264  private Map<String, String> makeVars(FetchedResource r) {
7265    Map<String, String> map = new HashMap<String, String>();
7266    if (r.getResource() != null) {
7267      switch (r.getResource().getResourceType()) {
7268      case StructureDefinition:
7269        StructureDefinition sd = (StructureDefinition) r.getResource();
7270        String url = sd.getBaseDefinition();
7271        StructureDefinition base = context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, url);
7272        if (base != null) {
7273          map.put("parent-name", base.getName());
7274          map.put("parent-link", base.getUserString("path"));
7275        } else {
7276          map.put("parent-name", "?? Unknown reference");
7277          map.put("parent-link", "??");
7278        }
7279        map.put("sd.Type", sd.getType());
7280        map.put("sd.Type-plural", Utilities.pluralize(sd.getType(), 2));
7281        map.put("sd.type", !sd.hasType() ? "" : sd.getType().toLowerCase());
7282        map.put("sd.type-plural", !sd.hasType() ? "" : Utilities.pluralize(sd.getType(), 2).toLowerCase());
7283        return map;
7284      default: return null;
7285      }
7286    } else
7287      return null;
7288  }
7289
7290  /**
7291   * saves the resource as XML, JSON, Turtle,
7292   * then all 3 of those as html with embedded links to the definitions
7293   * then the narrative as html
7294   *
7295   * @param r
7296   * @throws IOException 
7297   * @throws FHIRException 
7298   * @throws FileNotFoundException
7299   * @throws Exception
7300   */
7301  private void saveNativeResourceOutputs(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) throws FHIRException, IOException {
7302    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
7303    new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context).compose(r.getElement(), bs, OutputStyle.NORMAL, igpkp.getCanonical());
7304    npm.addFile(isExample(f,r ) ? Category.EXAMPLE : Category.RESOURCE, r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".json", bs.toByteArray());
7305    String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, "_includes", r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".json");
7306    String json = new String(bs.toByteArray());
7307    TextFile.stringToFile(json, path);
7308    path = Utilities.path(tempDir, "_includes", r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".escaped.json");
7309    json = Utilities.escapeXml(json);
7310    TextFile.stringToFile(json, path);
7311    
7312    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml") || forHL7orFHIR()) {
7313      path = Utilities.path(tempDir, r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".xml");
7314      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
7315      FileOutputStream stream = new FileOutputStream(path);
7316      new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser(context).compose(r.getElement(), stream, OutputStyle.PRETTY, igpkp.getCanonical());
7317      stream.close();
7318    }
7319    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "json") || forHL7orFHIR()) {
7320      path = Utilities.path(tempDir, r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".json");
7321      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
7322      FileOutputStream stream = new FileOutputStream(path);
7323      new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context).compose(r.getElement(), stream, OutputStyle.PRETTY, igpkp.getCanonical());
7324      stream.close();
7325    } 
7326    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl")) {
7327      path = Utilities.path(tempDir, r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+".ttl");
7328      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
7329      FileOutputStream stream = new FileOutputStream(path);
7330      new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.TurtleParser(context).compose(r.getElement(), stream, OutputStyle.PRETTY, igpkp.getCanonical());
7331      stream.close();
7332    }    
7333  }
7334
7335  private boolean isExample(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) {
7336    ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent igr = findIGReference(r.fhirType(), r.getId());
7337    if (igr == null)
7338      return false;
7339    else if (!igr.hasExample())
7340      return false;
7341    else if (igr.hasExampleCanonicalType())
7342      return true;
7343    else
7344      return igr.getExampleBooleanType().booleanValue();
7345  }
7346
7347
7348  private boolean forHL7orFHIR() {
7349    return igpkp.getCanonical().contains("hl7.org") || igpkp.getCanonical().contains("fhir.org") ;
7350  }
7351
7352
7353  private void saveFileOutputs(FetchedFile f) throws IOException, FHIRException {
7354    if (f.getResources().size() == 1) {
7355      Map<String, String> vars = new HashMap<>();
7356      FetchedResource r = f.getResources().get(0);
7357      StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
7358      b.append("<table class=\"grid\">\r\n");
7359      b.append("<tr><td><b>Level</b></td><td><b>Type</b></td><td><b>Location</b></td><td><b>Message</b></td></tr>\r\n");
7360      genVMessage(b, f.getErrors(), IssueSeverity.FATAL);
7361      genVMessage(b, f.getErrors(), IssueSeverity.ERROR);
7362      genVMessage(b, f.getErrors(), IssueSeverity.WARNING);
7363      genVMessage(b, f.getErrors(), IssueSeverity.INFORMATION);
7364      b.append("</table>\r\n");
7365      fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-validation", b.toString(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7366    }
7367  }
7368
7369  public void genVMessage(StringBuilder b, List<ValidationMessage> vms, IssueSeverity lvl) {
7370    for (ValidationMessage vm : vms) {
7371      if (vm.getLevel() == lvl) {
7372        b.append("<tr><td>");
7373        b.append(vm.getLevel().toCode());
7374        b.append("</td><td>");
7375        b.append(vm.getType().toCode());
7376        b.append("</td><td>");
7377        b.append(vm.getLocation());
7378        b.append("</td><td>");
7379        b.append(vm.getHtml());
7380        b.append("</td><td>");
7381        b.append("</td></tr>\r\n");
7382      }
7383    }
7384  }
7385
7386  private void makeTemplatesContained(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Resource res, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContained) throws FileNotFoundException, Exception {
7387    String baseName = igpkp.getPropertyContained(r, "base", res);
7388    if (res != null && res instanceof StructureDefinition) {
7389      if (igpkp.hasProperty(r, "template-base-"+((StructureDefinition) res).getKind().toCode().toLowerCase(), res))
7390        genWrapperContained(f, r, res, igpkp.getPropertyContained(r, "template-base-"+((StructureDefinition) res).getKind().toCode().toLowerCase(), res), baseName, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "", prefixForContained);
7391      else
7392        genWrapperContained(f, r, res, igpkp.getPropertyContained(r, "template-base", res), baseName, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "", prefixForContained);
7393    } else
7394      genWrapperContained(f, r, res, igpkp.getPropertyContained(r, "template-base", res), baseName, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "", prefixForContained);
7395    genWrapperContained(null, r, res, igpkp.getPropertyContained(r, "template-defns", res), igpkp.getPropertyContained(r, "defns", res), f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "definitions", prefixForContained);
7396    for (String templateName : extraTemplates.keySet()) {
7397      if (!templateName.equals("format") && !templateName.equals("defns")) {
7398        String output = igpkp.getProperty(r, templateName);
7399         if (output == null)
7400          output = r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"_"+res.getId()+"-"+templateName+".html";
7401        genWrapperContained(null, r, res, igpkp.getPropertyContained(r, "template-"+templateName, res), output, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, templateName, prefixForContained);
7402      }
7403    }
7404  }
7405  
7406  private void makeTemplates(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Map<String, String> vars) throws FileNotFoundException, Exception {
7407    String baseName = igpkp.getProperty(r, "base");
7408    if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition) {
7409      if (igpkp.hasProperty(r, "template-base-"+((StructureDefinition) r.getResource()).getKind().toCode().toLowerCase(), null))
7410        genWrapper(f, r, igpkp.getProperty(r, "template-base-"+((StructureDefinition) r.getResource()).getKind().toCode().toLowerCase()), baseName, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "", true);
7411      else
7412        genWrapper(f, r, igpkp.getProperty(r, "template-base"), baseName, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "", true);
7413    } else
7414      genWrapper(f, r, igpkp.getProperty(r, "template-base"), baseName, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "", true);
7415    genWrapper(null, r, igpkp.getProperty(r, "template-defns"), igpkp.getProperty(r, "defns"), f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, "definitions", false);
7416    for (String templateName : extraTemplates.keySet()) {
7417      if (!templateName.equals("format") && !templateName.equals("defns")) {
7418        String output = igpkp.getProperty(r, templateName);
7419         if (output == null)
7420          output = r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-"+templateName+".html";
7421        genWrapper(null, r, igpkp.getProperty(r, "template-"+templateName), output, f.getOutputNames(), vars, null, templateName, false);
7422      }
7423    }
7424  }

7426  private void saveDirectResourceOutputs(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Resource res, Map<String, String> vars) throws FileNotFoundException, Exception {
7427    boolean example = r.isExample();
7428    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "maturity") && res != null) {
7429      fragment(res.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-maturity",  genFmmBanner(r), f.getOutputNames());
7430    }
7431    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "ip-statements") && res != null) {
7432      fragment(res.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-ip-statements",  genIpStatements(r, example), f.getOutputNames());
7433    }
7434    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "validate")) {
7435      fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-validate",  genValidation(f, r), f.getOutputNames());
7436    }
7437
7438    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "status") && res instanceof DomainResource) {
7439      fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-status",  genStatus(f, r, res), f.getOutputNames());
7440    }
7441
7442    String template = igpkp.getProperty(r, "template-format");
7443    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml")) {
7444      if (tool == GenerationTool.Jekyll)
7445        genWrapper(null, r, template, igpkp.getProperty(r, "format"), f.getOutputNames(), vars, "xml", "", false);
7446    }
7447    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "json")) {
7448      if (tool == GenerationTool.Jekyll)
7449        genWrapper(null, r, template, igpkp.getProperty(r, "format"), f.getOutputNames(), vars, "json", "", false);
7450    } 
7451
7452    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl")) {
7453      if (tool == GenerationTool.Jekyll)
7454        genWrapper(null, r, template, igpkp.getProperty(r, "format"), f.getOutputNames(), vars, "ttl", "", false);
7455    }
7456
7457    org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser xp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.XmlParser(context);
7458    ByteArrayOutputStream bs = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
7459    xp.compose(r.getElement(), bs, OutputStyle.NORMAL, null);
7460    int size = bs.size();
7461    
7462    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml-html")) {
7463      XmlXHtmlRenderer x = new XmlXHtmlRenderer();
7464      x.setPrism(size < PRISM_SIZE_LIMIT);
7465      xp.setLinkResolver(igpkp);
7466      xp.setShowDecorations(false);
7467      xp.compose(r.getElement(), x);
7468      fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-xml-html", x.toString(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, "xml");
7469    }
7470    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "json-html")) {
7471      JsonXhtmlRenderer j = new JsonXhtmlRenderer();
7472      j.setPrism(size < PRISM_SIZE_LIMIT);
7473      org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser jp = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.JsonParser(context);
7474      jp.setLinkResolver(igpkp);
7475      jp.compose(r.getElement(), j);
7476      fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-json-html", j.toString(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, "json");
7477    }
7478
7479    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl-html")) {
7480      org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.TurtleParser ttl = new org.hl7.fhir.r5.elementmodel.TurtleParser(context);
7481      ttl.setLinkResolver(igpkp);
7482      Turtle rdf = new Turtle();
7483      ttl.compose(r.getElement(), rdf, "");
7484      fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-ttl-html", rdf.asHtml(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, "ttl");
7485    }
7486
7487    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "html")) {
7488      XhtmlNode xhtml = getXhtml(f, r);
7489      if (xhtml == null && HistoryGenerator.allEntriesAreHistoryProvenance(r.getElement())) {
7490        RenderingContext ctxt = rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f, r));
7491        List<ProvenanceDetails> entries = loadProvenanceForBundle(igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true), r.getElement(), f);
7492        xhtml = new HistoryGenerator(ctxt).generateForBundle(entries); 
7493        fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-html", new XhtmlComposer(XhtmlComposer.XML).compose(xhtml), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7494      } else if (r.getResource() instanceof Binary) {
7495        String pfx = "";
7496        if (r.getExampleUri() != null) {
7497          StructureDefinition sd = context.fetchResource(StructureDefinition.class, r.getExampleUri());
7498          if (sd != null && sd.getKind() == StructureDefinitionKind.LOGICAL) {
7499            pfx = "<p>This content is an example of the <a href=\""+Utilities.escapeXml(sd.getUserString("path"))+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(sd.present())+"</a> Logical Model and is not a FHIR Resource</p>\r\n";
7500          }          
7501        }
7502        BinaryRenderer br = new BinaryRenderer(tempDir);
7503        String html = pfx+br.display((Binary) r.getResource());
7504        for (String fn : br.getFilenames()) {
7505          otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, fn));
7506        }
7507        fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-html", html, f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7508      } else {
7509        String html = xhtml == null ? "" : new XhtmlComposer(XhtmlComposer.XML).compose(xhtml);
7510        fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-html", html, f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7511      }
7512    }
7513
7514    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "history")) {
7515      XhtmlNode xhtml = new HistoryGenerator(rc).generate(r);
7516      String html = xhtml == null ? "" : new XhtmlComposer(XhtmlComposer.XML).compose(xhtml);
7517      fragment(r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"-history", html, f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7518    }
7519   
7520    //  NarrativeGenerator gen = new NarrativeGenerator(null, null, context);
7521    //  gen.generate(f.getElement(), false);
7522    //  xhtml = getXhtml(f);
7523    //  html = xhtml == null ? "" : new XhtmlComposer().compose(xhtml);
7524    //  fragment(f.getId()+"-gen-html", html);
7525  }
7526
7527  private List<ProvenanceDetails> loadProvenanceForBundle(String path, Element bnd, FetchedFile f) throws Exception {
7528    List<ProvenanceDetails> ret = new ArrayList<>();
7529    List<Element> entries = bnd.getChildrenByName("entry");
7530    for (int i = 0; i < entries.size(); i++) {
7531      Element entry = entries.get(i);
7532      Element res = entry.getNamedChild("resource");
7533      if (res != null && "Provenance".equals(res.fhirType())) {
7534        ret.add(processProvenanceForBundle(f, path, res));
7535      }
7536    }
7537    return ret;
7538  }

7540  private void saveDirectResourceOutputsContained(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Resource res, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContained) throws FileNotFoundException, Exception {
7541    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "history")) {
7542      String html = "";
7543      fragment(res.fhirType()+"-"+prefixForContained+res.getId()+"-history", html, f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7544    }
7545    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "html")) {
7546      XhtmlNode xhtml = getXhtml(f, r, res);
7547      if (xhtml == null && HistoryGenerator.allEntriesAreHistoryProvenance(r.getElement())) {
7548        RenderingContext ctxt = rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f, r));
7549        List<ProvenanceDetails> entries = loadProvenanceForBundle(igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true), r.getElement(), f);
7550        xhtml = new HistoryGenerator(ctxt).generateForBundle(entries); 
7551        fragment(res.fhirType()+"-"+prefixForContained+res.getId()+"-html", new XhtmlComposer(XhtmlComposer.XML).compose(xhtml), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, prefixForContained);
7552      } else {
7553        String html = xhtml == null ? "" : new XhtmlComposer(XhtmlComposer.XML).compose(xhtml);
7554        fragment(res.fhirType()+"-"+prefixForContained+res.getId()+"-html", html, f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, prefixForContained);
7555      }
7556    }
7557  }
7558
7559  private String genIpStatements(List<FetchedFile> files) throws FHIRException {
7560    Set<String> systems = new HashSet<String>();
7561    for (FetchedFile f : files) {
7562      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
7563        listAllCodeSystems(systems, r.getElement());        
7564      }
7565    }
7566    
7567    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
7568    boolean first = true;
7569    for (String system : systems) {
7570      CopyRightUsageStatement stmt = getCopyRightStatement(system);
7571      if (stmt != null) {
7572        if (first) {
7573          b.append("<ul>\r\n");
7574        }
7575        first = false;
7576        b.append("<li>This publication includes IP from "+stmt.getSystemName()+". "+stmt.getHtml()+"</li>\r\n");
7577      }
7578    }
7579    if (!first) {
7580      b.append("</ul>\r\n");
7581    }
7582    return b.toString();     
7583  }
7584  
7585  private String genIpStatements(FetchedResource r, boolean example) throws FHIRException {
7586    Set<String> systems = listAllCodeSystems(r.getElement());
7587    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
7588    boolean first = true;
7589    for (String system : systems) {
7590      CopyRightUsageStatement stmt = getCopyRightStatement(system);
7591      if (stmt != null) {
7592        if (first) {
7593          b.append("<ul>\r\n");
7594        }
7595        first = false;
7596        b.append("<li>This "+(example ? "example" : describeResource(r.getElement()))+" includes IP from "+stmt.getSystemName()+". "+stmt.getHtml()+"</li>\r\n");
7597      }
7598    }
7599    if (!first) {
7600      b.append("</ul>\r\n");
7601    }
7602    return b.toString(); 
7603  }
7604
7605  private String describeResource(Element element) {
7606    String t = element.fhirType();
7607    if ("StructureDefinition".equals(t)) {
7608      String s = element.getChildValue("type");
7609      if ("Extension".equals(s)) {
7610        return "extension";
7611      } else {
7612        s = element.getChildValue("kind");
7613        if ("logical".equals(s)) {
7614          return "logical model";
7615        } else {
7616          return "profile";
7617        }       
7618      }
7619    } else {
7620      return t;
7621    }
7622  }
7623
7624  // todo - hook this up to the
7625  private CopyRightUsageStatement getCopyRightStatement(String system) {
7626    if ("http://snomed.info/sct".equals(system)) {
7627      return new CopyRightUsageStatement("SNOMED Clinical TermsÂ® (SNOMED CTÂ®)", "This content from  which is copyright of SNOMED International. Implementers of these specifications must have the appropriate SNOMED CT Affiliate license - "+
7628       "for more information contact <a href=\"http://www.snomed.org/snomed-ct/get-snomed-ct\">http://www.snomed.org/snomed-ct/get-snomed-ct</a> or <a href=\"mailto:info@snomed.org\">info@snomed.org</a>.");
7629    }
7630    if ("http://loinc.org".equals(system)) {
7631      return new CopyRightUsageStatement("LOINC", "This material contains content from <a href=\"http://loinc.org\">LOINC</a. LOINC is copyright Â© 1995-2020, Regenstrief Institute, Inc. and the Logical Observation Identifiers Names and Codes (LOINC) "+
7632         "Committee and is available at no cost under the <a href=\"http://loinc.org/license\">license</a>. LOINCÂ® is a registered United States trademark of Regenstrief Institute, Inc.");
7633    }
7634    if (system != null) {
7635      CodeSystem cs = context.fetchCodeSystem(system);
7636      if (cs != null && cs.hasCopyright()) {
7637        return new CopyRightUsageStatement(cs.present(), stripPara(markdownEngine.process(cs.getCopyright(), "Copyright")));        
7638      }
7639    }
7640    return null;
7641  }
7642
7643  private String stripPara(String p) {
7644    if (Utilities.noString(p)) {
7645      return "";
7646    }
7647    if (p.startsWith("<p>")) {
7648      p = p.substring(3);
7649    }
7650    if (p.endsWith("</p>")) {
7651      p = p.substring(0, p.length()-4);
7652    }
7653    return p;
7654  }
7655
7656  private Set<String> listAllCodeSystems(Element element) {
7657    Set<String> set = new HashSet<String>();
7658    listAllCodeSystems(set, element);
7659    return set;
7660  }
7661
7662  private void listAllCodeSystems(Set<String> set, Element element) {
7663    if ("Coding".equals(element.fhirType())) {
7664      set.add(element.getChildValue("system"));
7665    }
7666    for (Element child : element.getChildren()) {
7667      listAllCodeSystems(set, child);
7668    }    
7669  }

7671  private String genFmmBanner(FetchedResource r) throws FHIRException {
7672    String fmm = null;
7673    StandardsStatus ss = null;
7674    if (r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource) {
7675      fmm = ToolingExtensions.readStringExtension((DomainResource) r.getResource(), ToolingExtensions.EXT_FMM_LEVEL);
7676      ss = ToolingExtensions.getStandardsStatus((DomainResource) r.getResource());
7677    }
7678    if (ss == null)
7679      ss = StandardsStatus.TRIAL_USE;
7680    if (fmm != null)
7681      return "<table class=\"cols\"><tbody><tr>"+
7682        "<td><a href=\"http://hl7.org/fhir/versions.html#maturity\">Maturity Level</a>: "+fmm+"</td>"+
7683        "<td>&nbsp;<a href=\""+checkAppendSlash(specPath)+"versions.html#std-process\" title=\"Standard Status\">"+ss.toDisplay()+"</a></td>"+
7684        "</tr></tbody></table>";
7685    else
7686      return "";
7687  }
7688
7689  private String genStatus(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Resource resource) throws FHIRException {
7690    org.hl7.fhir.igtools.renderers.StatusRenderer.ResourceStatusInformation info = StatusRenderer.analyse((DomainResource) resource);
7691    return StatusRenderer.render(igpkp.specPath(), info);
7692  }
