7694  private String genValidation(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) throws FHIRException {
7695    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
7696    String version = mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD ? "current" : mode == IGBuildMode.PUBLICATION ? publishedIg.getVersion() : "dev";
7697    if (isExample(f, r)) {
7698      // we're going to use javascript to determine the relative path of this for the user.
7699      b.append("<p><b>Validation Links:</b></p><ul><li><a href=\"https://confluence.hl7.org/display/FHIR/Using+the+FHIR+Validator\">Validate using FHIR Validator</a> (Java): <code id=\"vl-"+r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"\">$cmd$</code></li></ul>\r\n");  
7700      b.append("<script type=\"text/javascript\">\r\n");
7701      b.append("  var x = window.location.href;\r\n");
7702      b.append("  document.getElementById(\"vl-"+r.fhirType()+"-"+r.getId()+"\").innerHTML = \"java -jar [path]/org.hl7.fhir.validator.jar -ig "+publishedIg.getPackageId()+"#"+version+" \"+x.substr(0, x.lastIndexOf(\".\")).replace(\"file:///\", \"\") + \".json\";\r\n");
7703      b.append("</script>\r\n");
7704    } else if (r.getResource() instanceof StructureDefinition) {
7705      b.append("<p>Validate this resource:</b></p><ul><li><a href=\"https://confluence.hl7.org/display/FHIR/Using+the+FHIR+Validator\">Validate using FHIR Validator</a> (Java): <code>"+
7706          "java -jar [path]/org.hl7.fhir.validator.jar -ig "+publishedIg.getPackageId()+"#"+version+" -profile "+((StructureDefinition) r.getResource()).getUrl()+" [resource-to-validate]"+
7707          "</code></li></ul>\r\n");        
7708    } else {
7709    } 
7710    return b.toString();
7711  }
7712
7713  private void genWrapper(FetchedFile ff, FetchedResource r, String template, String outputName, Set<String> outputTracker, Map<String, String> vars, String format, String extension, boolean recordPath) throws FileNotFoundException, IOException, FHIRException {
7714    if (template != null && !template.isEmpty()) {
7715      boolean existsAsPage = false;
7716      if (ff != null) {
7717        String fn = igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true);
7718        for (String pagesDir: pagesDirs) {
7719          if (altMap.containsKey("page/"+Utilities.path(pagesDir, fn))) {
7720            existsAsPage = true;
7721            break;
7722          }
7723        }
7724        if (!existsAsPage && !prePagesDirs.isEmpty()) {
7725          for (String prePagesDir : prePagesDirs) {
7726            if (altMap.containsKey("page/"+Utilities.path(prePagesDir, fn))) {
7727              existsAsPage = true;
7728              break;
7729            }
7730          }
7731        }
7732      }
7733      if (!existsAsPage) {
7734         template = fetcher.openAsString(Utilities.path(fetcher.pathForFile(configFile), template));
7735        template = igpkp.doReplacements(template, r, vars, format);
7736
7737        outputName = determineOutputName(outputName, r, vars, format, extension);
7738        if (!outputName.contains("#")) {
7739          String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, outputName);
7740          if (recordPath)
7741            r.setPath(outputName);
7742          checkMakeFile(TextFile.stringToBytes(template, false), path, outputTracker);
7743        }
7744      }
7745    }
7746  }
7747
7748  private void genWrapperContained(FetchedFile ff, FetchedResource r, Resource res, String template, String outputName, Set<String> outputTracker, Map<String, String> vars, String format, String extension, String prefixForContained) throws FileNotFoundException, IOException, FHIRException {
7749    if (template != null && !template.isEmpty()) {
7750      boolean existsAsPage = false;
7751      if (ff != null) {
7752        String fn = igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true, res);
7753        for (String pagesDir: pagesDirs) {
7754          if (altMap.containsKey("page/"+Utilities.path(pagesDir, fn))) {
7755            existsAsPage = true;
7756            break;
7757          }
7758        }
7759        if (!existsAsPage && !prePagesDirs.isEmpty()) {
7760          for (String prePagesDir : prePagesDirs) {
7761            if (altMap.containsKey("page/"+Utilities.path(prePagesDir, fn))) {
7762              existsAsPage = true;
7763              break;
7764            }
7765          }
7766        }
7767      }
7768      if (!existsAsPage) {
7769        template = fetcher.openAsString(Utilities.path(fetcher.pathForFile(configFile), template));
7770        template = igpkp.doReplacements(template, r, res, vars, format, prefixForContained);
7771
7772        outputName = determineOutputName(outputName, r, res, vars, format, extension, prefixForContained);
7773        if (!outputName.contains("#")) {
7774          String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, outputName);
7775          checkMakeFile(TextFile.stringToBytes(template, false), path, outputTracker);
7776        }
7777      }
7778    }
7779  }
7780
7781  private String determineOutputName(String outputName, FetchedResource r, Map<String, String> vars, String format, String extension) throws FHIRException {
7782    if (outputName == null)
7783      outputName = "{{[type]}}-{{[id]}}"+(extension.equals("")? "":"-"+extension)+(format==null? "": ".{{[fmt]}}")+".html";
7784    if (outputName.contains("{{["))
7785      outputName = igpkp.doReplacements(outputName, r, vars, format);
7786    return outputName;
7787  }
7788
7789  private String determineOutputName(String outputName, FetchedResource r, Resource res, Map<String, String> vars, String format, String extension, String prefixForContained) throws FHIRException {
7790    if (outputName == null)
7791      outputName = "{{[type]}}-{{[id]}}"+(extension.equals("")? "":"-"+extension)+(format==null? "": ".{{[fmt]}}")+".html";
7792    if (outputName.contains("{{["))
7793      outputName = igpkp.doReplacements(outputName, r, res, vars, format, prefixForContained);
7794    return outputName;
7795  }
7796
7797  /**
7798   * Generate:
7799   *   summary
7800   *   content as html
7801   *   xref
7802   * @throws org.hl7.fhir.exceptions.FHIRException
7803   * @throws Exception
7804   */
7805  private void generateOutputsCodeSystem(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource fr, CodeSystem cs, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
7806    CodeSystemRenderer csr = new CodeSystemRenderer(context, specPath, cs, igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, rc);
7807    if (igpkp.wantGen(fr, "summary")) {
7808      fragment("CodeSystem-"+prefixForContainer+cs.getId()+"-summary", csr.summaryTable(fr, igpkp.wantGen(fr, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(fr, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(fr, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), fr, vars, null);
7809    }
7810    if (igpkp.wantGen(fr, "summary-table")) {
7811      fragment("CodeSystem-"+prefixForContainer+cs.getId()+"-summary-table", csr.summaryTable(fr, igpkp.wantGen(fr, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(fr, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(fr, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), fr, vars, null);
7812    }
7813    if (igpkp.wantGen(fr, "content")) {
7814      fragment("CodeSystem-"+prefixForContainer+cs.getId()+"-content", csr.content(otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), fr, vars, null);
7815    }
7816    if (igpkp.wantGen(fr, "xref")) {
7817      fragment("CodeSystem-"+prefixForContainer+cs.getId()+"-xref", csr.xref(), f.getOutputNames(), fr, vars, null);
7818    }
7819    
7820    CodeSystemSpreadsheetGenerator vsg = new CodeSystemSpreadsheetGenerator(context);
7821    if (igpkp.wantGen(fr, "xlsx") && vsg.canGenerate(cs)) {
7822      String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, "CodeSystem-"+prefixForContainer + cs.getId()+".xlsx");
7823      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
7824      vsg.renderCodeSystem(cs);
7825      vsg.finish(new FileOutputStream(path));
7826    }
7827  }
7828
7829  /**
7830   * Genrate:
7831   *   summary
7832   *   Content logical definition
7833   *   cross-reference
7834   *
7835   * and save the expansion as html. todo: should we save it as a resource too? at this time, no: it's not safe to do that; encourages abuse
7836   * @param vs
7837   * @throws org.hl7.fhir.exceptions.FHIRException
7838   * @throws Exception
7839   */
7840  private void generateOutputsValueSet(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, ValueSet vs, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
7841    ValueSetRenderer vsr = new ValueSetRenderer(context, specPath, vs, igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, rc);
7842    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary")) {
7843      fragment("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-summary", vsr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7844    }
7845    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary-table")) {
7846      fragment("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-summary-table", vsr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7847    }
7848    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "cld")) {
7849      try {
7850        fragment("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-cld", vsr.cld(otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7851      } catch (Exception e) {
7852        fragmentError(vs.getId()+"-cld", e.getMessage(), null, f.getOutputNames());
7853      }
7854    }
7855    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xref")) {
7856      fragment("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-xref", vsr.xref(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7857    }
7858    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "expansion")) {
7859      if (vs.getStatus() == PublicationStatus.RETIRED) {
7860        String html = "<p style=\"color: maroon\">Expansions are not generated for retired value sets</p>";
7861        fragment("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-expansion", html, f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7862      } else {
7863        ValueSetExpansionOutcome exp = context.expandVS(vs, true, true);
7864        if (exp.getValueset() != null) {
7865          expansions.add(exp.getValueset());
7866
7867          RenderingContext lrc = rc.copy();
7868          lrc.setTooCostlyNoteNotEmpty("This value set has >1000 codes in it. In order to keep the publication size manageable, only a selection (1000 codes) of the whole set of codes is shown");
7869          lrc.setTooCostlyNoteEmpty("This value set cannot be expanded because of the way it is defined - it has an infinite number of members");
7870          lrc.setTooCostlyNoteNotEmptyDependent("One of this value set's dependencies has >1000 codes in it. In order to keep the publication size manageable, only a selection of the whole set of codes is shown");
7871          lrc.setTooCostlyNoteEmptyDependent("This value set cannot be expanded because of the way it is defined - one of it's dependents has an infinite number of members");
7872          exp.getValueset().setCompose(null);
7873          exp.getValueset().setText(null);  
7874          RendererFactory.factory(exp.getValueset(), lrc).render(exp.getValueset());
7875          String html = new XhtmlComposer(XhtmlComposer.XML).compose(exp.getValueset().getText().getDiv());
7876          fragment("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-expansion", html, f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7877        } else {
7878          if (exp.getError() != null) { 
7879            if (exp.getError().contains("Unable to provide support")) {
7880              fragmentErrorHtml("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-expansion", "No Expansion for this valueset (Unknown Code System<!-- "+Utilities.escapeXml(exp.getAllErrors().toString())+" -->)", "Publication Tooling Error: "+Utilities.escapeXml(exp.getAllErrors().toString()), f.getOutputNames());
7881              f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.TerminologyEngine, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "ValueSet.where(id = '"+vs.getId()+"')", exp.getError(), IssueSeverity.WARNING).setTxLink(exp.getTxLink()));
7882              r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.TerminologyEngine, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "ValueSet.where(id = '"+vs.getId()+"')", exp.getError(), IssueSeverity.WARNING).setTxLink(exp.getTxLink()));
7883            } else {
7884              fragmentErrorHtml("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-expansion", "No Expansion for this valueset (not supported by Publication Tooling<!-- "+Utilities.escapeXml(exp.getAllErrors().toString())+" -->)", "Publication Tooling Error: "+Utilities.escapeXml(exp.getAllErrors().toString()), f.getOutputNames());
7885              f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.TerminologyEngine, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "ValueSet.where(id = '"+vs.getId()+"')", exp.getError(), IssueSeverity.ERROR).setTxLink(exp.getTxLink()));
7886              r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.TerminologyEngine, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "ValueSet.where(id = '"+vs.getId()+"')", exp.getError(), IssueSeverity.ERROR).setTxLink(exp.getTxLink()));
7887            }
7888          } else {
7889            fragmentError("ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer+vs.getId()+"-expansion", "No Expansion for this valueset (not supported by Publication Tooling)", "Unknown Error", f.getOutputNames());
7890            f.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.TerminologyEngine, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "ValueSet.where(id = '"+vs.getId()+"')", "Unknown Error expanding ValueSet", IssueSeverity.ERROR).setTxLink(exp.getTxLink()));
7891            r.getErrors().add(new ValidationMessage(Source.TerminologyEngine, IssueType.EXCEPTION, "ValueSet.where(id = '"+vs.getId()+"')", "Unknown Error expanding ValueSet", IssueSeverity.ERROR).setTxLink(exp.getTxLink()));
7892          }
7893        }
7894      }
7895    }
7896    ValueSetSpreadsheetGenerator vsg = new ValueSetSpreadsheetGenerator(context);
7897    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xlsx") && vsg.canGenerate(vs)) {
7898      String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, "ValueSet-"+prefixForContainer + r.getId()+".xlsx");
7899      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
7900      vsg.renderValueSet(vs);
7901      vsg.finish(new FileOutputStream(path));
7902    }
7903
7904  }
7905
7906  private void fragmentError(String name, String error, String overlay, Set<String> outputTracker) throws IOException, FHIRException {
7907    if (Utilities.noString(overlay))
7908      fragment(name, "<p><span style=\"color: maroon; font-weight: bold\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(error)+"</span></p>\r\n", outputTracker);
7909    else
7910      fragment(name, "<p><span style=\"color: maroon; font-weight: bold\" title=\""+Utilities.escapeXml(overlay)+"\">"+Utilities.escapeXml(error)+"</span></p>\r\n", outputTracker);
7911  }
7912
7913  private void fragmentErrorHtml(String name, String error, String overlay, Set<String> outputTracker) throws IOException, FHIRException {
7914    if (Utilities.noString(overlay))
7915      fragment(name, "<p><span style=\"color: maroon; font-weight: bold\">"+error+"</span></p>\r\n", outputTracker);
7916    else
7917      fragment(name, "<p><span style=\"color: maroon; font-weight: bold\" title=\""+overlay+"\">"+error+"</span></p>\r\n", outputTracker);
7918  }

7920  /**
7921   * Generate:
7922   *   summary
7923   *   content as html
7924   *   xref
7925   * @throws IOException
7926   */
7927  private void generateOutputsConceptMap(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, ConceptMap cm, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws IOException, FHIRException {
7928    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary")) {
7929      fragmentError("ConceptMap-"+prefixForContainer+cm.getId()+"-summary", "yet to be done: concept map summary", null, f.getOutputNames());
7930    }
7931    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary-table")) {
7932      fragmentError("ConceptMap-"+prefixForContainer+cm.getId()+"-summary-table", "yet to be done: concept map summary", null, f.getOutputNames());
7933    }
7934    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "content")) {
7935      fragmentError("ConceptMap-"+prefixForContainer+cm.getId()+"-content", "yet to be done: table presentation of the concept map", null, f.getOutputNames());
7936    }
7937    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xref")) {
7938      fragmentError("ConceptMap-"+prefixForContainer+cm.getId()+"-xref", "yet to be done: list of all places where concept map is used", null, f.getOutputNames());
7939    }
7940    MappingSheetParser p = new MappingSheetParser();
7941    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "sheet") && p.isSheet(cm)) {
7942      fragment("ConceptMap-"+prefixForContainer+cm.getId()+"-sheet", p.genSheet(cm), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7943    }
7944    ConceptMapSpreadsheetGenerator cmg = new ConceptMapSpreadsheetGenerator(context);
7945    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xlsx") && cmg.canGenerate(cm)) {
7946      String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, prefixForContainer + r.getId()+".xlsx");
7947      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
7948      cmg.renderConceptMap(cm);
7949      cmg.finish(new FileOutputStream(path));
7950    }
7951  }
7952
7953  private void generateOutputsCapabilityStatement(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, CapabilityStatement cpbs, Map<String, String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
7954    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "swagger") || igpkp.wantGen(r, "openapi")) {
7955      Writer oa = null;
7956      if (openApiTemplate != null) 
7957        oa = new Writer(new FileOutputStream(Utilities.path(tempDir, cpbs.getId()+ ".openapi.json")), new FileInputStream(Utilities.path(Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(configFile), openApiTemplate)));
7958      else
7959        oa = new Writer(new FileOutputStream(Utilities.path(tempDir, cpbs.getId()+ ".openapi.json")));
7960      String lic = license();
7961      String displ = context.validateCode(new ValidationOptions("en-US"), new Coding("http://hl7.org/fhir/spdx-license",  lic, null), null).getDisplay();
7962      new OpenApiGenerator(context, cpbs, oa).generate(displ, "http://spdx.org/licenses/"+lic+".html");
7963      oa.commit();
7964      otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, cpbs.getId()+ ".openapi.json"));
7965      npm.addFile(Category.OPENAPI, cpbs.getId()+ ".openapi.json", TextFile.fileToBytes(Utilities.path(tempDir, cpbs.getId()+ ".openapi.json")));
7966    }
7967  }

7969  private void generateOutputsStructureDefinition(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, StructureDefinition sd, Map<String, String> vars, boolean regen, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
7970    // todo : generate shex itself
7971    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "shex"))
7972      fragmentError("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-shex", "yet to be done: shex as html", null, f.getOutputNames());
7973
7974    // todo : generate json schema itself. JSON Schema generator
7975//    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, ".schema.json")) {
7976//      String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, r.getId()+".sch");
7977//      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
7978//      new ProfileUtilities(context, errors, igpkp).generateSchematrons(new FileOutputStream(path), sd);
7979//    }
7980    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "json-schema"))
7981      fragmentError("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-json-schema", "yet to be done: json schema as html", null, f.getOutputNames());
7982
7983    StructureDefinitionRenderer sdr = new StructureDefinitionRenderer(context, checkAppendSlash(specPath), sd, Utilities.path(tempDir), igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, fileList, rc, allInvariants);
7984    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary")) {
7985      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-summary", sdr.summary(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7986    }
7987    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary-table")) {
7988      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-summary-table", sdr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7989    }
7990    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "header"))
7991      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-header", sdr.header(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7992    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "uses"))
7993      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-uses", sdr.uses(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7994    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "diff"))
7995      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-diff", sdr.diff(igpkp.getDefinitionsName(r), otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7996    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "snapshot"))
7997      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-snapshot", sdr.snapshot(igpkp.getDefinitionsName(r), otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
7998    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "snapshot-by-mustsupport"))
7999      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-snapshot-by-mustsupport", sdr.byMustSupport(igpkp.getDefinitionsName(r), otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8000    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "grid"))
8001      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-grid", sdr.grid(igpkp.getDefinitionsName(r), otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8002    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "pseudo-xml"))
8003      fragmentError("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-pseudo-xml", "yet to be done: Xml template", null, f.getOutputNames());
8004    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "pseudo-json"))
8005      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-pseudo-json", sdr.pseudoJson(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8006    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "pseudo-ttl"))
8007      fragmentError("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-pseudo-ttl", "yet to be done: Turtle template", null, f.getOutputNames());
8008    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "uml"))
8009      fragmentError("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-uml", "yet to be done: UML as SVG", null, f.getOutputNames());
8010    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "tx"))
8011      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-tx", sdr.tx(includeHeadings, false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8012    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "tx-must-support"))
8013      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-tx-must-support", sdr.tx(includeHeadings, true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8014    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "tx-diff"))
8015      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-tx-diff", sdr.txDiff(includeHeadings, false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8016    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "tx-diff-must-support"))
8017      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-tx-diff-must-support", sdr.txDiff(includeHeadings, true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8018    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "inv-diff"))
8019      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-inv-diff", sdr.invOldMode(includeHeadings, true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8020    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "inv"))
8021      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-inv", sdr.invOldMode(includeHeadings, false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8022    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "dict"))
8023      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-dict", sdr.dict(true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8024    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "dict-active"))
8025      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-dict-active", sdr.dict(false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8026    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "maps"))
8027      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-maps", sdr.mappings(false, false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8028    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "maps"))
8029      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-maps-all", sdr.mappings(true, false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8030    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "maps"))
8031      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-maps-diff", sdr.mappings(false, true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8032    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "maps"))
8033      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-maps-diff-all", sdr.mappings(true, true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8034    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xref"))
8035      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-sd-xref", sdr.references(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8036    if (sd.getDerivation() == TypeDerivationRule.CONSTRAINT && igpkp.wantGen(r, "span"))
8037      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-span", sdr.span(true, igpkp.getCanonical(), otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8038    if (sd.getDerivation() == TypeDerivationRule.CONSTRAINT && igpkp.wantGen(r, "spanall"))
8039      fragment("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-spanall", sdr.span(true, igpkp.getCanonical(), otherFilesRun), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8040
8041    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "example-list"))
8042      fragment("StructureDefinition-example-list-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId(), sdr.exampleList(fileList, true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8043    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "example-table"))
8044      fragment("StructureDefinition-example-table-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId(), sdr.exampleTable(fileList, true), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8045
8046    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "example-list-all"))
8047      fragment("StructureDefinition-example-list-all-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId(), sdr.exampleList(fileList, false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8048    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "example-table-all"))
8049      fragment("StructureDefinition-example-table-all-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId(), sdr.exampleTable(fileList, false), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8050
8051    String sdPrefix = newIg ? "StructureDefinition-" : "";
8052    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "csv")) {
8053      String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, sdPrefix + r.getId()+".csv");
8054      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
8055      new ProfileUtilities(context, errors, igpkp).generateCsvs(new FileOutputStream(path), sd, true);
8056    }
8057
8058    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "java")) {
8059      ConstraintJavaGenerator jg = new ConstraintJavaGenerator(context, version, tempDir, sourceIg.getUrl());
8060      try {
8061        f.getOutputNames().add(jg.generate(sd));
8062      } catch (Exception e) {
8063        e.printStackTrace();
8064      }
8065    }
8066
8067    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "xlsx")) {
8068      String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, sdPrefix + r.getId()+".xlsx");
8069      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
8070      StructureDefinitionSpreadsheetGenerator sdg = new StructureDefinitionSpreadsheetGenerator(context, true, anyMustSupport(sd));
8071      sdg.renderStructureDefinition(sd);
8072      sdg.finish(new FileOutputStream(path));
8073    }
8074
8075    if (!regen && sd.getKind() != StructureDefinitionKind.LOGICAL &&  igpkp.wantGen(r, "sch")) {
8076      String path = Utilities.path(tempDir, sdPrefix + r.getId()+".sch");
8077      f.getOutputNames().add(path);
8078      new ProfileUtilities(context, errors, igpkp).generateSchematrons(new FileOutputStream(path), sd);
8079      npm.addFile(Category.SCHEMATRON, sdPrefix + r.getId()+".sch", TextFile.fileToBytes(Utilities.path(tempDir, sdPrefix + r.getId()+".sch")));
8080    }
8081    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "sch"))
8082      fragmentError("StructureDefinition-"+prefixForContainer+sd.getId()+"-sch", "yet to be done: schematron as html", null, f.getOutputNames());
8083  }
8084
8085  private boolean anyMustSupport(StructureDefinition sd) {
8086    for (ElementDefinition ed : sd.getSnapshot().getElement()) {
8087      if (ed.getMustSupport()) {
8088        return true;
8089      }
8090    }
8091    return false;
8092  }
8093
8094  private String checkAppendSlash(String s) {
8095    return s.endsWith("/") ? s : s+"/";
8096  }
8097
8098  private void generateOutputsStructureMap(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, StructureMap map, Map<String,String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
8099    StructureMapRenderer smr = new StructureMapRenderer(context, checkAppendSlash(specPath), map, Utilities.path(tempDir), igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, rc);
8100    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary"))
8101      fragment("StructureMap-"+prefixForContainer+map.getId()+"-summary", smr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8102    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary-table"))
8103      fragment("StructureMap-"+prefixForContainer+map.getId()+"-summary-table", smr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8104    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "content"))
8105      fragment("StructureMap-"+prefixForContainer+map.getId()+"-content", smr.content(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8106    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "profiles"))
8107      fragment("StructureMap-"+prefixForContainer+map.getId()+"-profiles", smr.profiles(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8108    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "script"))
8109      fragment("StructureMap-"+prefixForContainer+map.getId()+"-script", smr.script(), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8110// to generate:
8111    // map file
8112    // summary table
8113    // profile index
8114
8115  }
8116
8117  private void generateOutputsCanonical(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, CanonicalResource cr, Map<String,String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
8118    CanonicalRenderer smr = new CanonicalRenderer(context, checkAppendSlash(specPath), cr, Utilities.path(tempDir), igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, rc);
8119    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary"))
8120      fragment(cr.fhirType()+"-"+prefixForContainer+cr.getId()+"-summary", smr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8121    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary-table"))
8122      fragment(cr.fhirType()+"-"+prefixForContainer+cr.getId()+"-summary-table", smr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8123  }
8124
8125  private void generateOutputsLibrary(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Library lib, Map<String,String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
8126    int counter = 0;
8127    for (Attachment att : lib.getContent()) {
8128      String extension = att.hasContentType() ? MimeType.getExtension(att.getContentType()) : null;
8129      if (extension != null && att.hasData()) {
8130        String filename = "Library-"+r.getId()+(counter == 0 ? "" : "-"+Integer.toString(counter))+"."+extension;
8131        TextFile.bytesToFile(att.getData(), Utilities.path(tempDir, filename));
8132        otherFilesRun.add(Utilities.path(tempDir, filename));
8133      }
8134      counter++;
8135    }
8136  }

8138  private void generateOutputsQuestionnaire(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Questionnaire q, Map<String,String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
8139    QuestionnaireRenderer qr = new QuestionnaireRenderer(context, checkAppendSlash(specPath), q, Utilities.path(tempDir), igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, rc.copy().setDefinitionsTarget(igpkp.getDefinitionsName(r)));
8140    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary"))
8141      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-summary", qr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8142    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "summary-table"))
8143      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-summary-table", qr.summaryTable(r, igpkp.wantGen(r, "xml"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "json"), igpkp.wantGen(r, "ttl"), igpkp.summaryRows()), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8144    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "tree"))
8145      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-tree", qr.render(QuestionnaireRendererMode.TREE), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8146    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "form"))
8147      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-form", qr.render(QuestionnaireRendererMode.FORM), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8148    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "links"))
8149      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-links", qr.render(QuestionnaireRendererMode.LINKS), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8150    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "logic"))
8151      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-logic", qr.render(QuestionnaireRendererMode.LOGIC), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8152    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "dict"))
8153      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-dict", qr.render(QuestionnaireRendererMode.DEFNS), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8154    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "responses"))
8155      fragment("Questionnaire-"+prefixForContainer+q.getId()+"-responses", responsesForQuestionnaire(q), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8156  }
8157
8158  private String responsesForQuestionnaire(Questionnaire q) {
8159    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
8160    for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
8161      for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
8162        if (r.fhirType().equals("QuestionnaireResponse")) {
8163          String qurl = r.getElement().getChildValue("questionnaire");
8164          if (!Utilities.noString(qurl)) {
8165            if (b.length() == 0) {
8166              b.append("<ul>\r\n");
8167            }
8168            b.append(" <li><a href=\""+igpkp.getLinkFor(r, true)+"\">"+getTitle(f,r )+"</a></li>\r\n");
8169          }
8170        }
8171      }
8172    }
8173    if (b.length() > 0) {
8174      b.append("</ul>\r\n");
8175    }
8176    return b.toString();
8177  }

8179  private void generateOutputsQuestionnaireResponse(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Map<String,String> vars, String prefixForContainer) throws Exception {
8180    QuestionnaireResponseRenderer qr = new QuestionnaireResponseRenderer(context, checkAppendSlash(specPath), r.getElement(), Utilities.path(tempDir), igpkp, specMaps, markdownEngine, packge, 
8181        rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f, r)).setDefinitionsTarget(igpkp.getDefinitionsName(r)));
8182    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "tree"))
8183      fragment("QuestionnaireResponse-"+prefixForContainer+r.getId()+"-tree", qr.render(QuestionnaireRendererMode.TREE), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8184    if (igpkp.wantGen(r, "form"))
8185      fragment("QuestionnaireResponse-"+prefixForContainer+r.getId()+"-form", qr.render(QuestionnaireRendererMode.FORM), f.getOutputNames(), r, vars, null);
8186  }

8189  private String getTitle(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) {
8190    if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof CanonicalResource) {
8191      return ((CanonicalResource) r.getResource()).getTitle();
8192    }
8193    String t = r.getElement().getChildValue("title");
8194    if (t != null) {
8195      return t;
8196    }
8197    t = r.getElement().getChildValue("name");
8198    if (t != null) {
8199      return t;
8200    }
8201    for (ImplementationGuideDefinitionResourceComponent res : publishedIg.getDefinition().getResource()) {
8202      FetchedResource tr = (FetchedResource) res.getUserData("loaded.resource");
8203      if (tr == r) {
8204        return res.getDescription();
8205      }
8206    }
8207    return "(no description)";
8208  }
8209
8210  private XhtmlNode getXhtml(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r) throws Exception {
8211    if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof DomainResource) {
8212      DomainResource dr = (DomainResource) r.getResource();
8213      if (dr.getText().hasDiv())
8214        return dr.getText().getDiv();
8215    }
8216    if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof Bundle) {
8217      RenderingContext lrc = rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f, r));
8218      Bundle b = (Bundle) r.getResource();
8219      BundleRenderer br = new BundleRenderer(lrc);
8220      if (br.canRender(b)) {
8221        return br.render(b);
8222      }
8223    }
8224    if (r.getResource() != null && r.getResource() instanceof Parameters) {
8225      Parameters p = (Parameters) r.getResource();
8226      return new ParametersRenderer(rc, new ResourceContext(ResourceContextType.PARAMETERS, p, null)).render(p);
8227    }
8228    if (r.fhirType().equals("Bundle")) {
8229      RenderingContext lrc = rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f, r));
8230      return new BundleRenderer(lrc).render(new ElementWrappers.ResourceWrapperMetaElement(lrc, r.getElement()));
8231    } else if (r.fhirType().equals("Parameters")) {
8232      RenderingContext lrc = rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f, r));
8233      return new ParametersRenderer(lrc, new ResourceContext(ResourceContextType.PARAMETERS, r.getElement(), r.getElement())).render(new ElementWrappers.ResourceWrapperMetaElement(lrc, r.getElement()));
8234    } else {
8235      return getHtmlForResource(r.getElement());
8236    }
8237  }
8238  
8239  private XhtmlNode getXhtml(FetchedFile f, FetchedResource r, Resource resource) throws Exception {
8240    if (resource instanceof DomainResource) {
8241      DomainResource dr = (DomainResource) resource;
8242      if (dr.getText().hasDiv())
8243        return dr.getText().getDiv();
8244    }
8245    if (resource instanceof Bundle) {
8246      Bundle b = (Bundle) resource;
8247      return new BundleRenderer(rc).render(b);
8248    }
8249    if (resource instanceof Parameters) {
8250      Parameters p = (Parameters) resource;
8251      return new ParametersRenderer(rc, new ResourceContext(ResourceContextType.PARAMETERS, p, null)).render(p);
8252    }
8253    RenderingContext lrc = rc.copy().setParser(getTypeLoader(f, r));
8254    return RendererFactory.factory(resource, lrc).build(resource);
8255  }
8256
8257
8258  private XhtmlNode getHtmlForResource(Element element) {
8259    Element text = element.getNamedChild("text");
8260    if (text == null)
8261      return null;
8262    Element div = text.getNamedChild("div");
8263    if (div == null)
8264      return null;
8265    else
8266      return div.getXhtml();
8267  }

8269  private void fragmentIfNN(String name, String content, Set<String> outputTracker) throws IOException, FHIRException {
8270    if (!Utilities.noString(content))
8271      fragment(name, content, outputTracker, null, null, null);
8272  }
8273  
8274  private void fragment(String name, String content, Set<String> outputTracker) throws IOException, FHIRException {
8275    fragment(name, content, outputTracker, null, null, null);
8276  }
8277  
8278  private void fragment(String name, String content, Set<String> outputTracker, FetchedResource r, Map<String, String> vars, String format) throws IOException, FHIRException {
8279    String fixedContent = (r==null? content : igpkp.doReplacements(content, r, vars, format));
8280    if (checkMakeFile(TextFile.stringToBytes(wrapLiquid(fixedContent), false), Utilities.path(tempDir, "_includes", name+".xhtml"), outputTracker)) {
8281      if (mode != IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD && makeQA)
8282        TextFile.stringToFile(pageWrap(fixedContent, name), Utilities.path(qaDir, name+".html"), true);
8283    }
8284  }
8285
8286  /**
8287   * None of the fragments presently generated inclde {{ }} liquid tags. So any 
8288   * liquid tags found in the fragments are actually what should be displayed post-jekyll.
8289   * So we're going to globally escape them here. If any fragments want to include actual
8290   * Jekyll tags, we'll have to do something much harder.
8291   * 
8292   * see https://stackoverflow.com/questions/24102498/escaping-double-curly-braces-inside-a-markdown-code-block-in-jekyll
8293   * 
8294   * @return
8295   */
8296  private String wrapLiquid(String content) {
8297    return "{% raw %}"+content+"{% endraw %}";
8298  }
8299
8300
8301
8302  private String pageWrap(String content, String title) {
8303    return "<html>\r\n"+
8304        "<head>\r\n"+
8305        "  <title>"+title+"</title>\r\n"+
8306        "  <link rel=\"stylesheet\" href=\"fhir.css\"/>\r\n"+
8307        "</head>\r\n"+
8308        "<body>\r\n"+
8309        content+
8310        "</body>\r\n"+
8311        "</html>\r\n";
8312  }

8366  private static String getNamedParam(String[] args, String param) {
8367    boolean found = false;
8368    for (String a : args) {
8369      if (found)
8370        return a;
8371      if (a.equals(param)) {
8372        found = true;
8373      }
8374    }
8375    return null;
8376  }
8377
8378  private static boolean hasNamedParam(String[] args, String param) {
8379    for (String a : args) {
8380      if (a.equals(param)) {
8381        return true;
8382      }
8383    }
8384    return false;
8385  }

8398    if (firstExecution)

8400    else
8401      System.out.println(msg);    
8402  }

8411  public static void prop(StringBuilder b, String name, String value) {
8412    b.append(name+": ");
8413    b.append(value);
8414    b.append("\r\n");
8415  }

8417  public static String buildReport(String ig, String source, String log, String qafile, String tx) throws Exception {
8418    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
8419    b.append("= Log =\r\n");
8420    b.append(log);
8421    b.append("\r\n\r\n");
8422    b.append("= System =\r\n");
8423
8424    prop(b, "ig", ig);
8425    prop(b, "current.dir:", getCurentDirectory());
8426    prop(b, "source", source);
8427    prop(b, "user.dir", System.getProperty("user.home"));
8428    prop(b, "tx.server", tx);
8429    prop(b, "tx.cache", Utilities.path(System.getProperty("user.home"), "fhircache"));
8430    prop(b, "system.type", System.getProperty("sun.arch.data.model"));
8431    prop(b, "system.cores", Integer.toString(Runtime.getRuntime().availableProcessors()));   
8432    prop(b, "system.mem.free", Long.toString(Runtime.getRuntime().freeMemory()));   
8433    long maxMemory = Runtime.getRuntime().maxMemory();
8434    prop(b, "system.mem.max", maxMemory == Long.MAX_VALUE ? "no limit" : Long.toString(maxMemory));   
8435    prop(b, "system.mem.total", Long.toString(Runtime.getRuntime().totalMemory()));   
8436
8437    b.append("= Validation =\r\n");
8438    if (qafile != null && new File(qafile).exists())
8439      b.append(TextFile.fileToString(qafile));
8440
8441    b.append("\r\n");
8442    b.append("\r\n");
8443
8444    if (ig != null) {
8445      b.append("= IG =\r\n");
8446      b.append(TextFile.fileToString(determineActualIG(ig, null)));
8447    }
8448
8449    b.append("\r\n");
8450    b.append("\r\n");
8451    return b.toString();
8452  }
8453  
8454  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
8455    int exitCode = 0;
8456    if (hasNamedParam(args, "-gui") || args.length == 0) {
8457      runGUI();
8458      // Returning here ends the main thread but leaves the GUI running
8459      return; 
8460    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-package")) {
8461      System.out.println("FHIR IG Publisher "+IGVersionUtil.getVersionString());
8462      System.out.println("Detected Java version: " + System.getProperty("java.version")+" from "+System.getProperty("java.home")+" on "+System.getProperty("os.arch")+" ("+System.getProperty("sun.arch.data.model")+"bit). "+toMB(Runtime.getRuntime().maxMemory())+"MB available");
8463      System.out.println("dir = "+System.getProperty("user.dir")+", path = "+System.getenv("PATH"));
8464      String s = "Parameters:";
8465      for (int i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
8466          s = s + " "+args[i];
8467      }      
8468      System.out.println(s);
8469      FilesystemPackageCacheManager pcm = new FilesystemPackageCacheManager(!hasNamedParam(args, "system"), ToolsVersion.TOOLS_VERSION);
8470      System.out.println("Cache = "+pcm.getFolder());
8471      for (String p : getNamedParam(args, "-package").split("\\;")) {
8472        NpmPackage npm = pcm.loadPackage(p);
8473        System.out.println("OK: "+npm.name()+"#"+npm.version()+" for FHIR version(s) "+npm.fhirVersionList()+" with canonical "+npm.canonical());
8474      }
8475    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-dicom-gen")) {
8476      DicomPackageBuilder pgen = new DicomPackageBuilder();
8477      pgen.setSource(getNamedParam(args, "src"));
8478      pgen.setDest(getNamedParam(args, "dst"));
8479      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-pattern")) {
8480        pgen.setPattern(getNamedParam(args, "-pattern"));
8481      }
8482      pgen.execute();
8483    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-help") || hasNamedParam(args, "-?") || hasNamedParam(args, "/?") || hasNamedParam(args, "?")) {
8484      System.out.println("");
8485      System.out.println("To use this publisher to publish a FHIR Implementation Guide, run ");
8486      System.out.println("with the commands");
8487      System.out.println("");
8488      System.out.println("-spec [igpack.zip] -ig [source] -tx [url] -packages [path] -watch");
8489      System.out.println("");
8490      System.out.println("-spec: a path or a url where the igpack for the version of the core FHIR");
8491      System.out.println("  specification used by the ig being published is located.  If not specified");
8492      System.out.println("  the tool will retrieve the file from the web based on the specified FHIR version");
8493      System.out.println("-ig: a path or a url where the implementation guide control file is found");
8494      System.out.println("  see Wiki for Documentation");
8495      System.out.println("-tx: (optional) Address to use for terminology server ");
8496      System.out.println("  (default is http://tx.fhir.org)");
8497      System.out.println("  use 'n/a' to run without a terminology server");
8498      System.out.println("-watch (optional): if this is present, the publisher will not terminate;");
8499      System.out.println("  instead, it will stay running, an watch for changes to the IG or its ");
8500      System.out.println("  contents and re-run when it sees changes ");
8501      System.out.println("");
8502      System.out.println("-packages: a directory to load packages (*.tgz) from before resolving dependencies");
8503      System.out.println("           this parameter can be present multiple times");
8504      System.out.println("");
8505      System.out.println("The most important output from the publisher is qa.html");
8506      System.out.println("");
8507      System.out.println("Alternatively, you can run the Publisher directly against a folder containing");
8508      System.out.println("a set of resources, to validate and represent them");
8509      System.out.println("");
8510      System.out.println("-source [source] -destination [dest] -tx [url]");
8511      System.out.println("");
8512      System.out.println("-source: a local to scan for resources (e.g. logical models)");
8513      System.out.println("-destination: where to put the output (including qa.html)");
8514      System.out.println("");
8515      System.out.println("the publisher also supports the param -proxy=[address]:[port] for if you use a proxy (stupid java won't pick up the system settings)");
8516      System.out.println("or you can configure the proxy using -Dhttp.proxyHost=<ip> -Dhttp.proxyPort=<port> -Dhttps.proxyHost=<ip> -Dhttps.proxyPort=<port>");
8517      System.out.println("");
8518      System.out.println("For additional information, see http://wiki.hl7.org/index.php?title=Proposed_new_FHIR_IG_build_Process");
8519    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-convert")) {
8520      // convert a igpack.zip to a package.tgz
8521      IGPack2NpmConvertor conv = new IGPack2NpmConvertor();
8522      conv.setSource(getNamedParam(args, "-source"));
8523      conv.setDest(getNamedParam(args, "-dest"));
8524      conv.setPackageId(getNamedParam(args, "-npm-name"));
8525      conv.setVersionIg(getNamedParam(args, "-version"));
8526      conv.setLicense(getNamedParam(args, "-license"));
8527      conv.setWebsite(getNamedParam(args, "-website"));
8528      conv.execute();
8529    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-delete-current")) {
8530      if (!args[0].equals("-delete-current")) {
8531        throw new Error("-delete-current must have the format -delete-current {root}/{realm}/{code} -history {history} (first argument is not -delete-current)");
8532      }
8533      if (args.length < 4) {
8534        throw new Error("-delete-current must have the format -delete-current {root}/{realm}/{code} -history {history} (not enough arguements)");
8535      }
8536      File f = new File(args[1]);
8537      if (!f.exists() || !f.isDirectory()) {
8538        throw new Error("-delete-current must have the format -delete-current {root}/{realm}/{code} -history {history} ({root}/{realm}/{code} not found)");
8539      }
8540      String history = getNamedParam(args, "-history");
8541      if (Utilities.noString(history)) {
8542        throw new Error("-delete-current must have the format -delete-current {root}/{realm}/{code} -history {history} (no history found)");
8543      }
8544      File fh = new File(history);
8545      if (!fh.exists()) {
8546        throw new Error("-delete-current must have the format -delete-current {root}/{realm}/{code} -history {history} ({history} not found ("+history+"))");
8547      }
8548      if (!fh.isDirectory()) {
8549        throw new Error("-delete-current must have the format -delete-current {root}/{realm}/{code} -history {history} ({history} not a directory ("+history+"))");
8550      }
8551      IGReleaseVersionDeleter deleter = new IGReleaseVersionDeleter();
8552      deleter.clear(f.getAbsolutePath(), fh.getAbsolutePath());
8553    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-go-publish")) {
8554      new PublicationProcess().publish(getNamedParam(args, "-source"), getNamedParam(args, "-destination"), hasNamedParam(args, "-milestone"), getNamedParam(args, "-registry"), getNamedParam(args, "-history"), getNamedParam(args, "-temp"));
8555    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-publish-update")) {
8556      if (!args[0].equals("-publish-update")) {
8557        throw new Error("-publish-update must have the format -publish-update -folder {folder} -registry {registry}/fhir-ig-list.json (first argument is not -publish-update)");
8558      }
8559      if (args.length < 3) {
8560        throw new Error("-publish-update must have the format -publish-update -folder {folder} -registry {registry}/fhir-ig-list.json (not enough args)");
8561      }
8562      File f = new File(getNamedParam(args, "-folder"));
8563      if (!f.exists() || !f.isDirectory()) {
8564        throw new Error("-publish-update must have the format -publish-update -folder {folder} -registry {registry}/fhir-ig-list.json ({folder} not found)");
8565      }
8566      
8567      String registry = getNamedParam(args, "-registry");
8568      if (Utilities.noString(registry)) {
8569        throw new Error("-publish-update must have the format -publish-update -url {url} -root {root} -registry {registry}/fhir-ig-list.json (-registry parameter not found)");
8570      }
8571      String filter = getNamedParam(args, "-filter");
8572
8573      if (!"n/a".equals(registry)) {
8574        File fr = new File(registry);
8575        if (!fr.exists() || fr.isDirectory()) {
8576          throw new Error("-publish-update must have the format -publish-update -url {url} -root {root} -registry {registry}/fhir-ig-list.json ({registry} not found)");
8577        }
8578      }
8579      boolean doCore = "true".equals(getNamedParam(args, "-core"));
8580      
8581      IGRegistryMaintainer reg = "n/a".equals(registry) ? null : new IGRegistryMaintainer(registry);
8582      IGWebSiteMaintainer.execute(f.getAbsolutePath(), reg, doCore, filter);
8583      reg.finish();      
8584    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-multi")) {
8585      int i = 1;
8586      for (String ig : TextFile.fileToString(getNamedParam(args, "-multi")).split("\\r?\\n")) {
8587        if (!ig.startsWith(";")) {
8588          System.out.println("=======================================================================================");
8589          System.out.println("Publish IG "+ig);
8590          Publisher self = new Publisher();
8591          self.setConfigFile(determineActualIG(ig, null));
8592          setTxServerValue(args, self);
8593          if (hasNamedParam(args, "-resetTx")) {
8594            self.setCacheOption(CacheOption.CLEAR_ALL);
8595          } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-resetTxErrors")) {
8596            self.setCacheOption(CacheOption.CLEAR_ERRORS);
8597          } else {
8598            self.setCacheOption(CacheOption.LEAVE);
8599          }
8600          try {
8601            self.execute();
8602          } catch (Exception e) {
8603            exitCode = 1;
8604            System.out.println("Publishing Implementation Guide Failed: "+e.getMessage());
8605            System.out.println("");
8606            System.out.println("Stack Dump (for debugging):");
8607            e.printStackTrace();
8608            break;
8609          }
8610          TextFile.stringToFile(buildReport(ig, null, self.filelog.toString(), Utilities.path(self.qaDir, "validation.txt"), self.txServer), Utilities.path(System.getProperty("java.io.tmpdir"), "fhir-ig-publisher-"+Integer.toString(i)+".log"), false);
8611          System.out.println("=======================================================================================");
8612          System.out.println("");
8613          System.out.println("");
8614          i++;
8615        }
8616      }
8617    } else {
8618      Publisher self = new Publisher();
8619      String consoleLog = getNamedParam(args, "log");
8620      if (consoleLog == null) {     
8621        consoleLog =  Utilities.path("[tmp]", "fhir-ig-publisher-tmp.log");
8622      }
8623      PublisherConsoleLogger logger = new PublisherConsoleLogger();
8624      if (!hasNamedParam(args, "-auto-ig-build") && !hasNamedParam(args, "-publish-process")) {
8625        logger.start(consoleLog);
8626      }
8627        
8628      self.logMessage("FHIR IG Publisher "+IGVersionUtil.getVersionString());
8629      self.logMessage("Detected Java version: " + System.getProperty("java.version")+" from "+System.getProperty("java.home")+" on "+System.getProperty("os.name")+"/"+System.getProperty("os.arch")+" ("+System.getProperty("sun.arch.data.model")+"bit). "+toMB(Runtime.getRuntime().maxMemory())+"MB available");
8630      if (!"64".equals(System.getProperty("sun.arch.data.model"))) {
8631        self.logMessage("Attention: you should upgrade your Java to a 64bit version in order to be able to run this program without running out of memory");        
8632      }
8633      self.logMessage("dir = "+System.getProperty("user.dir")+", path = "+System.getenv("PATH"));
8634      String s = "Parameters:";
8635      for (int i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
8636          s = s + " "+args[i];
8637      }      
8638      self.logMessage(s);
8639      self.logMessage("Start Clock @ "+nowAsString(self.execTime)+" ("+nowAsDate(self.execTime)+")");
8640      self.logMessage("");
8641      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-auto-ig-build")) {
8642        self.setMode(IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD);
8643        self.targetOutput = getNamedParam(args, "-target");
8644      }
8645      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-api-key-file")) {
8646        self.apiKeyFile = new IniFile(new File(getNamedParam(args, "-api-key-file")).getAbsolutePath());
8647      }
8648
8649      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-no-narrative")) {
8650        for (String p : getNamedParam(args, "-non-narrative").split("\\,")) {
8651          self.noNarratives.add(p);
8652        }
8653      }
8654      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-no-validate")) {
8655        for (String p : getNamedParam(args, "-non-validate").split("\\,")) {
8656          self.noValidate.add(p);
8657        }
8658      }
8659
8660      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-validation-off")) {
8661        self.noValidation = true;
8662        System.out.println("Running without validation to shorten the run time (editor process only)");
8663      }
8664      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-generation-off")) {
8665        self.noGenerate = true;
8666        System.out.println("Running without generation to shorten the run time (editor process only)");
8667      }
8668
8669      setTxServerValue(args, self);
8670      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-source")) {
8671        // run with standard template. this is publishing lite
8672        self.setSourceDir(getNamedParam(args, "-source"));
8673        self.setDestDir(getNamedParam(args, "-destination"));
8674        self.specifiedVersion = getNamedParam(args, "-version");
8675      } else if(!hasNamedParam(args, "-ig") && args.length == 1 && new File(args[0]).exists()) {
8676        self.setConfigFile(determineActualIG(args[0], IGBuildMode.MANUAL));
8677      } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-prompt")) {
8678        IniFile ini = new IniFile("publisher.ini");
8679        String last = ini.getStringProperty("execute", "path");
8680        boolean ok = false;
8681        if (Utilities.noString(last)) {
8682          while (!ok) {
8683            System.out.print("Enter path of IG: ");
8684            BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
8685            last = reader.readLine();
8686            if (new File(last).exists()) {
8687              ok = true;
8688            } else {
8689              System.out.println("Can't find "+last);
8690            }
8691          } 
8692        } else {
8693          while (!ok) {
8694            System.out.print("Enter path of IG ["+last+"]: ");
8695            BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
8696            String nlast = reader.readLine();
8697            if (Utilities.noString(nlast))
8698              nlast = last;
8699            if (new File(nlast).exists()) {
8700              ok = true;
8701              last = nlast;
8702            } else {
8703              System.out.println("Can't find "+nlast);
8704            }
8705          }
8706        }
8707        ini.setStringProperty("execute", "path", last, null);
8708        ini.save();
8709        if (new File(last).isDirectory()) {
8710          self.setConfigFile(determineActualIG(Utilities.path(last, "ig.json"), IGBuildMode.MANUAL));
8711        } else {
8712          self.setConfigFile(determineActualIG(last, IGBuildMode.MANUAL));
8713        }
8714      } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-simplifier")) {
8715        if (!hasNamedParam(args, "-destination")) {
8716          throw new Exception("A destination folder (-destination) must be provided for the output from processing the simplifier IG");
8717        }
8718        if (!hasNamedParam(args, "-canonical")) {
8719          throw new Exception("A canonical URL (-canonical) must be provided in order to process a simplifier IG");
8720        }
8721        if (!hasNamedParam(args, "-npm-name")) {
8722          throw new Exception("A package name (-npm-name) must be provided in order to process a simplifier IG");
8723        }
8724        if (!hasNamedParam(args, "-license")) {
8725          throw new Exception("A license code (-license) must be provided in order to process a simplifier IG");
8726        }
8727        List<String> packages = new ArrayList<String>();
8728        for (int i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
8729          if (args[i].equals("-dependsOn")) { 
8730            packages.add(args[i+1]);
8731          }
8732        }
8733        // create an appropriate ig.json in the specified folder
8734        self.setConfigFile(generateIGFromSimplifier(getNamedParam(args, "-simplifier"), getNamedParam(args, "-destination"), getNamedParam(args, "-canonical"), getNamedParam(args, "-npm-name"), getNamedParam(args, "-license"), packages));
8735        self.folderToDelete = Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(self.getConfigFile());
8736      } else {
8737        self.setConfigFile(determineActualIG(getNamedParam(args, "-ig"), self.mode));
8738        if (Utilities.noString(self.getConfigFile())) {
8739          throw new Exception("No Implementation Guide Specified (-ig parameter)");
8740        }
8741        if (!(new File(self.getConfigFile()).isAbsolute())) {
8742          self.setConfigFile(Utilities.path(System.getProperty("user.dir"), self.getConfigFile()));
8743        }
8744      }
8745      self.setJekyllCommand(getNamedParam(args, "-jekyll"));
8746      self.setIgPack(getNamedParam(args, "-spec"));
8747      String proxy = getNamedParam(args, "-proxy");
8748      if (!Utilities.noString(proxy)) {
8749        String[] p = proxy.split("\\:");
8750        System.setProperty("http.proxyHost", p[0]);
8751        System.setProperty("http.proxyPort", p[1]);
8752        System.setProperty("https.proxyHost", p[0]);
8753        System.setProperty("https.proxyPort", p[1]);
8754      }
8755      self.setTxServer(getNamedParam(args, "-tx"));
8756      self.setPackagesFolder(getNamedParam(args, "-packages"));
8757      self.watch = hasNamedParam(args, "-watch");
8758      self.debug = hasNamedParam(args, "-debug");
8759      self.cacheVersion = hasNamedParam(args, "-cacheVersion");
8760      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-publish")) {
8761        self.setMode(IGBuildMode.PUBLICATION);
8762        self.targetOutput = getNamedParam(args, "-publish");   
8763        self.publishing  = true;
8764        self.targetOutputNested = getNamedParam(args, "-nested");        
8765      }
8766      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-resetTx")) {
8767        self.setCacheOption(CacheOption.CLEAR_ALL);
8768      } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-resetTxErrors")) {
8769        self.setCacheOption(CacheOption.CLEAR_ERRORS);
8770      } else {
8771        self.setCacheOption(CacheOption.LEAVE);
8772      }
8773      if (hasNamedParam(args, "-no-sushi")) {
8774        self.noFSH = true;
8775      }
8776      try {
8777        self.execute();
8778        if (hasNamedParam(args, "-no-errors")) {
8779          exitCode = self.countErrs(self.errors) > 0 ? 1 : 0;
8780        }
8781      } catch (Exception e) {
8782        exitCode = 1;
8783        self.log("Publishing Content Failed: "+e.getMessage());
8784        self.log("");
8785        if (e.getMessage() != null &&  e.getMessage().contains("xsl:message")) {
8786          self.log("This error was created by the template");   
8787        } else {
8788          self.log("Use -? to get command line help");
8789          self.log("");
8790          self.log("Stack Dump (for debugging):");
8791          e.printStackTrace();
8792          for (StackTraceElement st : e.getStackTrace()) {
8793            if (st != null && self.filelog != null) {
8794              self.filelog.append(st.toString());
8795            }
8796          }
8797        }
8798        exitCode = 1;
8799      } finally {
8800        if (self.mode == IGBuildMode.MANUAL) {
8801          TextFile.stringToFile(buildReport(getNamedParam(args, "-ig"), getNamedParam(args, "-source"), self.filelog.toString(), Utilities.path(self.qaDir, "validation.txt"), self.txServer), Utilities.path(System.getProperty("java.io.tmpdir"), "fhir-ig-publisher.log"), false);
8802        }
8803      }
8804      logger.stop();
8805    }
8806    if (!hasNamedParam(args, "-no-exit")) {
8807      System.exit(exitCode);
8808    }
8809  }

8811  public static void setTxServerValue(String[] args, Publisher self) {
8812    if (hasNamedParam(args, "-tx")) {
8813      self.setTxServer(getNamedParam(args, "-tx"));
8814    } else if (hasNamedParam(args, "-devtx")) {
8815      self.setTxServer(txServerDev);
8816    } else {
8817      self.setTxServer(txServerProd);
8818    }
8819  }

8821  private static String generateIGFromSimplifier(String folder, String output, String canonical, String npmName, String license, List<String> packages) throws Exception {
8822    String ig = Utilities.path(System.getProperty("java.io.tmpdir"), "simplifier", UUID.randomUUID().toString().toLowerCase());
8823    Utilities.createDirectory(ig);
8824    String config = Utilities.path(ig, "ig.json");
8825    String pages =  Utilities.path(ig, "pages");
8826    String resources =  Utilities.path(ig, "resources");
8827    Utilities.createDirectory(pages);
8828    Utilities.createDirectory(resources);
8829    Utilities.createDirectory(Utilities.path(ig, "temp"));
8830    Utilities.createDirectory(Utilities.path(ig, "txCache"));
8831    // now, copy the entire simplifer folder to pages
8832    Utilities.copyDirectory(folder, pages, null);
8833    // now, copy the resources to resources;
8834    Utilities.copyDirectory(Utilities.path(folder, "artifacts"), resources, null);
8835    JsonObject json = new JsonObject();
8836    JsonObject paths = new JsonObject();
8837    json.add("paths", paths);
8838    JsonArray reslist = new JsonArray();
8839    paths.add("resources", reslist);
8840    reslist.add(new JsonPrimitive("resources"));
8841    paths.addProperty("pages", "pages");
8842    paths.addProperty("temp", "temp");
8843    paths.addProperty("output", output);
8844    paths.addProperty("qa", "qa");
8845    paths.addProperty("specification", "http://build.fhir.org");
8846    json.addProperty("version", "3.0.2");
8847    json.addProperty("license", license);
8848    json.addProperty("npm-name", npmName);
8849    JsonObject defaults = new JsonObject();
8850    json.add("defaults", defaults);
8851    JsonObject any = new JsonObject();
8852    defaults.add("Any", any);
8853    any.addProperty("java", false);
8854    any.addProperty("xml", false);
8855    any.addProperty("json", false);
8856    any.addProperty("ttl", false);
8857    json.addProperty("canonicalBase", canonical);
8858    json.addProperty("sct-edition", "http://snomed.info/sct/731000124108");
8859    json.addProperty("source", determineSource(resources, Utilities.path(folder, "artifacts")));
8860    json.addProperty("path-pattern", "[type]-[id].html");
8861    JsonObject resn = new JsonObject();
8862    json.add("resources", resn);
8863    resn.addProperty("*", "*");
8864    JsonArray deplist = new JsonArray();
8865    json.add("dependencyList", deplist);
8866    for (String d : packages) {
8867      String[] p = d.split("\\#");
8868      JsonObject dep = new JsonObject();
8869      deplist.add(dep);
8870      dep.addProperty("package", p[0]);
8871      dep.addProperty("version", p[1]);
8872      dep.addProperty("name", "n"+deplist.size());
8873    }
8874    Gson gson = new GsonBuilder().setPrettyPrinting().create();
8875    TextFile.stringToFile(gson.toJson(json), config);
8876    return config;
8877  }

8880  private static String determineSource(String folder, String srcF) throws Exception {
8881    for (File f : new File(folder).listFiles()) {
8882      String src = TextFile.fileToString(f);
8883      if (src.contains("<ImplementationGuide ")) {
8884        return f.getName();
8885      }
8886    }
8887    throw new Exception("Unable to find Implementation Guide in "+srcF); 
8888  }

8906  public static String determineActualIG(String ig, IGBuildMode mode) throws Exception {
8907    if (ig.startsWith("http://") || ig.startsWith("https://")) {
8908      ig = convertUrlToLocalIg(ig);
8909    }
8910    File f = new File(ig);
8911    if (!f.exists() && mode == IGBuildMode.AUTOBUILD) {
8912      String s = Utilities.getDirectoryForFile(ig);
8913      f = new File(s == null ? System.getProperty("user.dir") : s);
8914    }
8915    if (!f.exists()) {
8916      throw new Exception("Unable to find the nominated IG at "+f.getAbsolutePath());
8917    }
8918    if (f.isDirectory() && new File(Utilities.path(ig, "ig.json")).exists()) {
8919      return Utilities.path(ig, "ig.json");
8920    } else {
8921      return f.getAbsolutePath();
8922    }
8923  }
8924
8925
8926  private static String convertUrlToLocalIg(String ig) throws IOException {
8927    String org = null;
8928    String repo = null;
8929    String branch = "master"; // todo: main?
8930    String[] p = ig.split("\\/");
8931    if (p.length > 5 && (ig.startsWith("https://build.fhir.org/ig") || ig.startsWith("http://build.fhir.org/ig"))) {
8932      org = p[4];
8933      repo = p[5]; 
8934      if (p.length >= 8) {
8935        if (!"branches".equals(p[6])) {
8936          throw new Error("Unable to understand IG location "+ig);
8937        } else {
8938          branch = p[7];
8939        }
8940      }  
8941    } if (p.length > 4 && (ig.startsWith("https://github.com/") || ig.startsWith("http://github.com/"))) {
8942      org = p[3];
8943      repo = p[4];
8944      if (p.length > 6) {
8945        if (!"tree".equals(p[5])) {
8946          throw new Error("Unable to understand IG location "+ig);
8947        } else {
8948          branch = p[6];
8949        }
8950      }
8951    } 
8952    if (org == null || repo == null) {
8953      throw new Error("Unable to understand IG location "+ig);
8954    }
8955    String folder = Utilities.path("[tmp]", "fhir-igs", makeFileName(org), makeFileName(repo), branch == null ? "master" : makeFileName(branch));
8956    File f = new File(folder);
8957    if (f.exists() && !f.isDirectory()) {
8958      f.delete();
8959    }
8960    if (!f.exists()) {
8961      Utilities.createDirectory(folder);
8962    }
8963    Utilities.clearDirectory(f.getAbsolutePath());
8964    
8965    String ghUrl = "https://github.com/"+org+"/"+repo+"/archive/refs/heads/"+branch+".zip";
8966    InputStream zip = fetchGithubUrl(ghUrl);
8967    Utilities.unzip(zip, Paths.get(f.getAbsolutePath()));
8968    for (File fd : f.listFiles()) {
8969      if (fd.isDirectory()) {
8970        return fd.getAbsolutePath();        
8971      }
8972    }
8973    throw new Error("Extracting GitHub source failed.");
8974  }
8975
8976  private static InputStream fetchGithubUrl(String ghUrl) throws IOException {
8977    URL url = new URL(ghUrl+"?nocache=" + System.currentTimeMillis());
8978    HttpURLConnection c = (HttpURLConnection) url.openConnection();
8979    c.setInstanceFollowRedirects(true);
8980    return c.getInputStream();
8981  }

8991
8992  private static String makeFileName(String org) {
8993    StringBuilder b = new StringBuilder();
8994    for (char ch : org.toCharArray()) {
8995      if (isValidFileNameChar(ch)) {
8996        b.append(ch);
8997      }
8998    }
8999    return b.toString();
9000  }
9001
9002  private static boolean isValidFileNameChar(char ch) {
9003    return Character.isDigit(ch) || Character.isAlphabetic(ch) || ch == '.' || ch == '-' || ch == '_' || ch == '#'  || ch == '$';
9004  }
9005
9006  private String getToolingVersion() {
9007    InputStream vis = Publisher.class.getResourceAsStream("/version.info");
9008    if (vis != null) {
9009      IniFile vi = new IniFile(vis);
9010      if (vi.getStringProperty("FHIR", "buildId") != null) {
9011        return vi.getStringProperty("FHIR", "version")+"-"+vi.getStringProperty("FHIR", "buildId");
9012      } else {
9013        return vi.getStringProperty("FHIR", "version")+"-"+vi.getStringProperty("FHIR", "revision");
9014      }
9015    }
9016    return "?? (not a build IGPublisher?)";
9017  }

9035  private static String nowAsString(Calendar cal) {

9037    return df.format(cal.getTime());
9038  }

9040  private static String nowAsDate(Calendar cal) {
9041    DateFormat df = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ssXXX", new Locale("en", "US"));
9042    return df.format(cal.getTime());
9043  }

9141
9142  private String fetchCurrentIGPubVersion() {
9143    if (currVer == null) {
9144      try {
9145        // This calls the GitHub api, to fetch the info on the latest release. As part of our release process, we name
9146        // all tagged releases as the version number. ex: "1.1.2".
9147        // This value can be grabbed from the "tag_name" field, or the "name" field of the returned JSON.
9148        JsonObject json = JsonTrackingParser.fetchJson("https://api.github.com/repos/HL7/fhir-ig-publisher/releases/latest");
9149        currVer = json.getAsJsonObject().get("name").getAsString();
9150      } catch (IOException e) {
9151        currVer = "?pub-ver-1?";
9152      }
9153    }
9154    return currVer;
9155  }
9156
9157  private void loadMappingSpaces(byte[] source) throws Exception {
9158    ByteArrayInputStream is = null;
9159    try {
9160      DocumentBuilderFactory factory = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
9161      factory.setNamespaceAware(true);
9162      DocumentBuilder builder = factory.newDocumentBuilder();
9163      is = new ByteArrayInputStream(source);
9164      Document doc = builder.parse(is);
9165      org.w3c.dom.Element e = XMLUtil.getFirstChild(doc.getDocumentElement());
9166      while (e != null) {
9167        MappingSpace m = new MappingSpace(XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "columnName").getTextContent(), XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "title").getTextContent(),
9168            XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "id").getTextContent(), Integer.parseInt(XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "sort").getTextContent()), true, false, false, XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "link") != null ? XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "link").getTextContent(): XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "url").getTextContent());
9169        mappingSpaces.put(XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "url").getTextContent(), m);
9170        org.w3c.dom.Element p = XMLUtil.getNamedChild(e, "preamble");
9171        if (p != null) {
9172          m.setPreamble(new XhtmlParser().parseHtmlNode(p).setName("div"));
9173        }
9174        e = XMLUtil.getNextSibling(e);
9175      }
9176    } catch (Exception e) {
9177      throw new Exception("Error processing mappingSpaces.details: "+e.getMessage(), e);
9178    }
9179  }
9180
9181
9182  @Override
9183  public void recordProfileUsage(StructureDefinition profile, Object appContext, Element element) {
9184    if (profile.getUrl().startsWith(igpkp.getCanonical())) { // ignore anything we didn't define
9185      FetchedResource example;
9186      if (appContext instanceof ValidatorHostContext) {
9187        example = (FetchedResource) ((ValidatorHostContext) appContext).getResource().getUserData("igpub.context.resource");
9188      } else {
9189        example= (FetchedResource) ((Element) appContext).getUserData("igpub.context.resource");
9190      }
9191      if (example != null) {
9192        FetchedResource source = null;
9193        for (FetchedFile f : fileList) {
9194          for (FetchedResource r : f.getResources()) {
9195            if (r.getResource() == profile) {
9196              source = r;
9197            }
9198          }
9199        }
9200        if (source != null) {
9201          source.addFoundExample(example);
9202          example.getFoundProfiles().add(profile.getUrl());
9203        }
9204      }
9205    }
9206    
9207  }
9208
9209  public static void publishDirect(String path) throws Exception {
9210    Publisher self = new Publisher();
9211    self.setConfigFile(Publisher.determineActualIG(path, IGBuildMode.PUBLICATION));
9212    self.execute();
9213    self.setTxServer(txServerProd);
9214    if (self.countErrs(self.errors) > 0) {
9215      throw new Exception("Building IG '"+path+"' caused an error");
9216    }
9217    
9218  }
